śmaśānaciticaityādau pañcamīpakṣasandhiṣu।
aṣṭamīnavamīsandhyāmadhyarātridineṣu ca॥
au41.77
yāmyāgneyamaghāśleṣāviśākhāpūrvanairṛte।
nairṛtākhye muhūrte ca daṣṭaṃ marmasu ca tyajet॥
au41.78
daṣṭamātre sitāsyākṣaḥ śīryamāṇaśiroruhaḥ।
stabdhajihvo muhurmūrcchan śītocchvāso na jīvati॥
au41.79
hidhmā śvāso vamiḥ kāso daṣṭamātrasya dehinaḥ।
jāyate yugapadyasya sa hṛcchūlī na jīvati॥
au41.80
vepathurvedanāstīvrā grīvābhaṅgokṣiraktatā।
mūrcchā galagrahaśchardiḥ pretarājasyakiṅkarāḥ॥
au41.81
jāmbavapratimo daṃśaḥ kūrmapṛṣṭhavadunnataḥ।
raktaṃ khebhyaḥ samastebhyo vartate na tu daṃśataḥ॥
au41.82
romṇāṃ na śītalairharṣaḥ śvayathurlohitāsitaḥ।
hṛṣṭamehanatā vakravaktratvaṃ yasya taṃ tyajet॥
au41.83
phenaṃ vamati nissaṃjñaḥ śyāvapādakarānanaḥ।
nāsāvasādo bhaṅgoṅge viḍbhedaḥ ślathasandhitā॥
au41.84
viṣapītasya daṣṭasya digdhenābhihatasya ca।
bhavantyetāni rūpāṇi samprāpte jīvitakṣaye॥
au41.85
na nasyaiścetanā tīkṣṇairna kṣatāt kṣatajāgamaḥ।
daṇḍāhatasya no rājiḥ prayātasya yamāntikam॥
au41.86
atonyathā tu tvarayā pradīptāgāravad bhiṣak।
rakṣan kaṇṭhagatān prāṇān viṣamāśu śamaṃ nayet॥
।iti ekacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
dvicatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
au42.1
athātaḥ sarpaviṣapratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayomaharṣayaḥ॥
au42.2
mātrāśataṃ viṣaṃ sthitvā daṃśe daṣṭasya dehinaḥ।
dehaṃ prakramate dhātūn rudhirādīn pradūṣayat॥
au42.3
etasminnantare karma daṃśasyotkartanādikam।
kuryācchīghraṃ yathā dehe viṣavallī na rohati॥
au42.4
daṣṭamātro daśedāśu tameva pavanāśinam।
loṣṭaṃ mahīṃ vā daśanaiśchitvā vānu sasambhramam॥
au42.5
niṣṭhīvena samālimpeddaṃśaṃ karṇamalena vā।
daṃśasyopari badhnīyādariṣṭāṃ caturaṅgule।
kṣaumādibhirveṇikayā siddhairmantraiśca mantravit॥
au42.6
bandho deśānusāreṇa nātigāḍhaślatho hitaḥ।
daṃśapūtitvaśophādīn kurute hyatipīḍitaḥ।
aśaktaḥ śithilo rodhduṃ viṣaṃ deśāntaraṃ vrajat॥
au42.7
ambuvat setubandhena bandhena stabhyate viṣam।
na vahanti sirāścāsya viṣaṃ bandhābhipīḍitāḥ॥
au42.8
niṣpīḍya coddhareddaṃśaṃ marmasandhyagataṃ tathā।
na jāyate viṣāvego bījanāśādivāṅkuraḥ।
marmage prāpnuyānmṛtyuṃ sandhisthe vikalāṅgatām॥
au42.9
daṃśaṃ maṇḍalināṃ muktvā pittalatvādathāparam।
prataptairhemalohādyairdahedāśūlmukena vā।
karoti bhasmasāt sadyo vahniḥ ki nāma na kṣaṇāt॥
au42.10
ācūṣet pūrṇavaktro vā mṛdbhasmāgadagomayaiḥ।
pracchāyāntarariṣṭāyāṃ māṃsalaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ॥
au42.11
aṅgaṃ sahaiva daṃśena lepayedagadairmuhuḥ।
candanośīrayuktena salilena ca secayet॥
au42.12
viṣe pravisṛte vidhyet sirāṃ sā paramā kriyā॥
au42.13
rakte nirddriyamāṇe hi kṛtsnaṃ nirddriyate viṣam।
duṣṭe hi vyāpnuyādaṅgaṃ dhruvaṃ mṛtyurbhavatyataḥ॥
au42.14
sirāvyadhoditairasramapravṛttaṃ pravartayet।
stambhayedativṛttaṃ ca taireva prāṇarakṣayā॥
au42.15
durgandhaṃ saviṣaṃ raktamagnau caṭacaṭāyate।
yathādoṣaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca pūrvavallakṣayedasṛk॥
au42.16
sirāsvadṛśyamānāsu yojyāḥ śṛṅgajalaukasaḥ॥
au42.17
śoṇitaṃ srutaśeṣaṃ ca pravilīnaṃ viṣoṣmaṇā।
lepasekaiḥ subahuśaḥ stambhayed bhṛśaśītalaiḥ॥
au42.18
askanne viṣavegāddhi mūrcchāyamadahṛddravāḥ।
bhavanti tān jayecchītairvījeccāromaharṣataḥ॥
au42.19
viṣaṃ karṣati tīkṣṇatvāddhṛdayaṃ tasya guptaye।
pibed ghṛtaṃ ghṛtakṣaudramagadaṃ vā ghṛtāplutam॥
au42.20
majjānaṃ gomayarasaṃ bhasmāmbhaḥ kṛṣṇamṛjjalam।
aikadhyaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā dadhi gairikavāri vā॥
au42.21
khādedvā kovidārārkaśirīṣakaṭabhīcchadān।
chāgameṣavarāhāsṛkśiśusthavirayoṣitaḥ॥
au42.22
pibeyurgarbhiṇī śītamadhurān payasā gadān।
tathā mūrcchādayo na syurviṣaṃ cāśvetinānilam॥
au42.23
hṛdayāvaraṇenāsya śleṣmā hṛdyupacīyate।
pravṛttagauravotkleśahṛllāsaṃ vāmayettataḥ॥
au42.24
dravaiḥ kāñjikakaulatthatailamadyādivarjitaiḥ।
vamanairviṣahṛdbhiśca naivaṃ vyāpnoti tadvapuḥ॥
au42.25
bhujaṅgadoṣaprakṛtisthānavegaviśeṣataḥ।
susūkṣmaṃ samyagālocya viśiṣṭāṃ cācaretkriyām॥
au42.26
sinduvārakamūlāni rasena svena peṣayet।
madhuyuktoyamagadaḥ pānaṃ darvīkṛtāṃ viṣe॥
au42.27
sinduvārakamūlāni śvetā ca girikarṇikā।
pānaṃ darvīkarairdaṣṭe nasyaṃ madhu sapākalam॥
au42.28
kṛṣṇasarpeṇa daṣṭasya limpeddaṃśaṃ hṛte'sṛji।
cāraṭīnākulībhyāṃ vā tīkṣṇamūlaviṣeṇa vā॥
au42.29
pānaṃ ca kṣaudramañjiṣṭhāgṛhadhūmayutaṃ ghṛtam॥
au42.30
taṇḍulīyakakāśmaryakiṇihīgirikarṇikāḥ।
mātuluṅgī sitā śeluḥ pānanasyāñjane hitaḥ।
agadaḥ phaṇināṃ ghore viṣe rājīmatāmapi॥
au42.31
samāḥ sugandhāmṛdvīkāśvetākhyāgajakarṇikāḥ।
arddhāṃśaṃ saurasaṃ patraṃ kapitthaṃ bilvadāḍimam।
sakṣaudro maṇḍaliviṣe viśeṣādagado hitaḥ॥
au42.32
pañcavalkavarāyaṣṭī nāgapuṣpailavālukam।
jīvakarṣabhakau śītaṃ sitā padmakamutpalam॥
au42.33
sakṣaudro himavān nāma hanti maṇḍalināṃ viṣam।
lepācchvayathuvīsarpavisphoṭajvaradāhahā॥
au42.34
kāśmaryaṃ vaṭaśṛṅgāṇi jīvakarṣabhakau sitām।
mañjiṣṭhāṃ madhukaṃ ceti daṣṭo maṇḍalinā pibet॥
au42.35
vaṃśatvagbījakaṭukā pāṭalībījanāgaram।
śirīṣabījātiviṣe mūlaṃ gāvedhukaṃ vacām।
piṣṭo govāriṇāṣṭāṅgo hanti gonasajaṃ viṣam॥
au42.36
kaṭukātiviṣākuṣṭhagṛhadhūmahareṇukāḥ।
sakṣaudravyoṣAtagarā ghnanti rājamitāṃ viṣam॥
au42.37
nikhanetkāṇḍacitrāyā daṃśaṃ yāmadvayaṃ bhuvi।
uddhṛtya pracchitaṃ sarpirddhānyamṛdbhyāṃ pralepayet॥
au42.38
pibet purāṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ varācūrṇāvacūrṇitam।
jīrṇe virikto bhuñjīta yavānnaṃ sūpasaṃskṛtam॥
au42.39
karavīrārkakusumamūlalāṅgalikā kaṇāḥ।
kalkayedāranālena pāṭhāmaricasaṃyutāḥ।
eṣa vyantaradaṣṭānāmagadaḥ sārvakārmikaḥ॥
au42.40
śirīṣapuṣpasvarase saptāhaṃ maricaṃ sitam।
bhāvitaṃ sarpadaṣṭānāṃ pānanasyāñjane hitam॥
au42.41
dvipalaṃ vakrakuṣṭhābhyāṃ ghṛtakṣaudraṃ catuṣpalam।
api takṣakadaṣṭānāṃ pānametat sukhapradam॥
au42.42
gṛhadhūmaṃ haridre dve samūlaṃ taṇḍulīyakam।
api vāsukinā daṣṭaḥ pibenmadhughṛtāplutam॥
au42.43
raktaṃ māṃsaṃ ca godhāyāḥ śuṣkaṃ cūrṇīkṛtaṃ hitam।
viṣe rasagate pānaṃ kapittharasasaṃyutam॥
au42.44
śelumūlatvagagrāṇi bādarodumbarāṇi ca।
kaṭabhyāśca pibedraktagate māṃsagate punaḥ॥
au42.45
sakṣaudraṃ khādirāriṣṭakauṭajaṃ mūlamambhasā।
sarveṣvapi balāyugmaṃ madhukaṃ madanaṃ natam॥
au42.46
śirogate viṣe mūlaṃ nasyakarmaṇi yojayet।
bandhujīvasya bhāṅrgyāśca surasasyāsitasya ca॥
au42.47
athavā pippalīhiṅguvṛścikālīmanaśśilāḥ।
śirīṣabījāpāmārgalavaṇaṃ cetanākaram।
kalkaśrūrṇothavā kṛṣṇākṣavakātiviṣoṣaṇāt॥
au42.48
pippalī maricakṣāravacāsaindhavaśigrukāḥ।
piṣṭā rohitapittena ghnantyakṣigatamañjanāt॥
au42.49
candanaṃ madhukaṃ māṃsī pippalīmaricotpalam।
saindhavaṃ cāñjanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ gavāṃ pittena kalkitam॥
au42.50
naktamālaphalaṃ vyoṣaṃ bilbamūlaṃ niśādvayam।
puṣpaṃ ca saurāsaṃ piṣṭamañjanaṃ bastavāriṇā।
bhojavaitaraṇoddiṣṭaṃ viṣasuptaprabodhanam॥
au42.51
vāriguñjāphalośīraṃ netrayorviṣaduṣṭayoḥ।
añjanaṃ vāriṇā piṣṭaṃ gāruḍaṃ garuḍopamam॥
au42.52
samudraphenaṃ maricaṃ kaṇāsauvīrakāñjam।
cūrṇāñjanaṃ sasindhūtthaṃ viṣopahatacakṣuṣām॥
au42.53
kapitthamāṃsaṃ sasitākṣaudraṃ kaṇṭhagate viṣe।
lihyādāmāśayagate tābhyāṃ cūrṇapalaṃ natāt॥
au42.54
viṣe pakvāśayagate mañjiṣṭhārajanīdvayam।
pippalīṃ ca samaṃ piṣṭvā gavyapittena pāyayet॥
au42.55
pippalīnāgarakṣāraṃ navanītena mūrcchitam।
pravṛddhe kaṇṭhage dadyācchleṣmaṇi pratisāraṇam॥
au42.56
jayet saṅkrāmaṇairāśu viṣaṃ śirasi saṃśritam।
dadyādadhastāddaṣṭasya mūrdhni kākapade kṛte॥
au42.57
kākadakṣaśikhicchāgagavyamāhiṣakaukkuṭam।
bilvapramāṇaṃ māṃsāsnamūrdhvadaṣṭasya pādayoḥ।
viṣaṃ saṅkramate tatra nihanyācchīghramanyathā॥
au42.58
tīkṣṇanasyāñjanānte ca bhūrimātraṃ pibet ghṛtam।
viṣaṃ hi netraṃ rūkṣasya tīkṣṇairhanti samīritam॥
au42.59
vāmayeta tataścainaṃ viṣaśeṣopaśāntaye।
śleṣmalaṃ śleṣmalairdaṣṭaṃ nābherūrdhvaṃ viśeṣataḥ॥
au42.60
dhāmārgavaḥ śakrayavāḥ sarṣapā madanaṃ madhu।
saindhavaṃ vamanaṃ koṣṇaṃ viṣe śleṣmāśrayaśrite॥
au42.61
surasaṃ sarpavetālīmīśvarāṃ gaurasarṣapam।
paṭolanimbapatraṃ ca pibet sakṣaudrasaindhavam॥
au42.62
śukāhvājālinīdantīmadanekṣvākukauṭajam।
kālā lāṅgalikā tiktā vamanaṃ taṇḍulāṃbunā॥
au42.63
paittikaṃ paittikairdaṣṭamadho nābherviśeṣataḥ।
viṣe pittāśayagate pāyayeta virecanam॥
au42.64
sanīlīphaladāṃ dantīṃ payasā mastunāthavā।
ślakṣṇacūrṇīkṛtaṃ kumbhaṃ kvāthena traiphalena vā।
kṣīreṇa vā trivṛcchyāmāsurasānīlinīrajaḥ॥
au42.65
piṇḍītakaphalaṃ vyoṣaṃ trivṛdvellaṃ harītakī।
virecanaṃ kaphaprāye lavaṇaṃ mūtrasamplutam॥
au42.66
ghṛtāplutaṃ salavaṇaṃ mārute nīlinīphalam॥
au42.67
śayānaḥ śayane chidre virecyo viṣapīḍitaḥ।
muhuruttiṣṭhato hyasya viṣaṃ dūṣayatenilam।
pibedvānto virikto vā yavāgūṃ viṣanāśinīm॥
au42.68
viṣe vātāśayagate sarpiṣaḥ pānamiṣyate।
ādyapaścimayoryacca proktaṃ viṣaniṣedhayoḥ॥
au42.69
atha darvīkṛtāṃ vege pūrve visrāvya śoṇitam।
agadaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ saṃyuktaṃ tvaritaṃ pibet॥
au42.70
dvitīye vamanaṃ kṛtvā tadvadevāgadaṃ pibet।
viṣāpahe prayuñjīta tṛtīyeñjananāvane॥
au42.71
pibeccaturthe pūrvoktāṃ yavāgūṃ vamane kṛte।
ṣaṣṭhapañcamayoḥ śītairdigdhasiktamabhīkṣṇaśaḥ॥
au42.72
pāyayedvamanaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yagāgūṃ yathoditām।
agadaṃ saptame tīkṣṇaṃ yuñjyādañjananasyayoḥ॥
au42.73
kṛtvāvagāḍhaṃ śastreṇa mūrdhni kākapadaṃ tataḥ।
māṃsaṃ sarudhiraṃ tasya carma vā tatra nikṣipet॥
au42.74
tṛtīye vāmitaḥ peyāṃ vege maṇḍalināṃ pibet।
atīkṣṇamagadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe gaṇaṃ vā padmakādikam॥
au42.75
ādyevagāḍhaṃ pracchāya vege daṣṭasya rājilaiḥ।
alābunā haredraktaṃ pūrvavaccāagadaṃ pibet॥
au42.76
ṣaṣṭhe vegeñjanaṃ tīkṣṇamavapīḍaṃ ca yojayet।
anukteṣu ca vegeṣu kriyāṃ darvīkaroditām॥
au42.77
garbhiṇībālavṛddheṣu mṛdu vidhyet sirāñca na॥
au42.78
tvaṅmanohvā niśe vakraṃ rasaḥ śārdūlajo nakhaḥ।
tamālaḥ kesaraṃ śītaṃ pītaṃ taṇḍulavāriṇā।
hanti sarvaviṣāṇyetadvajraṃ vajramivāsurān॥
au42.79
prapauṇḍarīkaṃ kaṭukā devadārusuvarcikā।
kālānusārī sthauṇeyaśaileyaghanapadmakam॥
au42.80
kuṭanneṭalāpunnāganatakuṣṭhīprayaṅgukam।
lodhraguggulutālīsapippalīsvarṇagairikam॥
au42.81
sinduvāraḥ sitaḥ śuṇṭhī dhyāmakaṃ lavaṇottamam।
ślakṣṇacūrṇīkṛtaṃ śṛṅge nidadhyānmākṣikadrutam॥
au42.82
tārkṣyastārkṣyopamaḥ pānanāvanābhyañjanāñjanaiḥ।
agadastakṣakasyāpi viṣavegaṃ nivartayet॥
au42.83
lodhraṃ śirīṣaṣuṣpāṇi samaṅgā hiṅgu reṇukāḥ।
kaṇoṣaṇailānepālī vacā yaṣṭī madhūtpalam॥
au42.84
sinduvārakamandāramūlaṃ bījaṃ karañjajam।
jyotiṣmatī nataṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śvetā ca girikarṇikā॥
au42.85
cūrṇitaḥ kanyayā kṣaudragopittābhyāṃ ca vartitaḥ।
agado hanti sarpākhukaṇabhaṃ ca sṛgālajam॥
au42.86
biḍālakāṇḍacitrotthaṃ viṣaṃ bhūtagrahaṃ jvaram।
apasmāragrahonmādagulmājīrṇaṃ viṣūcikām॥
au42.87
bilvasya mūlaṃ surasasya puṣpaṃ phalaṃ karañjasya nataṃ surāhvam।
phalatrayaṃ vyoṣaniśādvayaṃ ca bastasya mūtreṇa susūkṣmapiṣṭam॥
au42.88
bhujaṅgalūtonduruvṛścikādyairviṣūcikājīrṇagājvaraiśca।
ārttān narān bhūtavidharṣitāṃśca svasthīkarotyañjanapānanasyaiḥ॥
au42.89
trivṛdviśalyā madhukaṃ niśe lavaṇapañcakam।
maṃjiṣṭhā tryūṣaṇaṃ tadvat kalkayet sa mahāgadaḥ॥
au42.90
māṃsīhareṇutriphalā muruṅgī madhuyaṣṭikā।
maṃjiṣṭā padmakāśokakuṣṭhatālīsacandanam॥
au42.91
sugandhikailā kiṇihī tvakpaṭolī mṛgādinī।
bhārṅgī viḍaṅgaṃ pālindī pāṭhā kroṣṭukamekhalā॥
au42.92
puṣpamāruṣkaraṃ patraṃ saurasaṃ kramukaṃ puram।
pittaṃ nakulamārjāragodhāśalyakasūkarāt॥
au42.93
pṛṣatāccitrapatrācca gośṛṅge pūrvavat sthitaḥ।
yatra gehe na tatrāhikīṭādibhyo bhayodbhavaḥ॥
au42.94
etena bherīpaṭahāḥ patākāśca pralepitāḥ।
ārṣabheṇa viṣaṃ ghnanti sparśaśravaṇadarśanaiḥ॥
au42.95
pralepādyaiśca niśśeṣaṃ daṃśādapyuddharedviṣam।
bhūyo vegāya jāyeta śeṣaṃ dūṣīviṣāya vā॥
au42.96
viṣāpāyenilaṃ kruddhaṃ snehādibhirupācaret।
tailamadyakulatthāmlavarjyaiḥ pavananāśanaiḥ॥
au42.97
pittaṃ pittajvaraharaiḥ kaṣāyasnehabastibhiḥ॥
au42.98
samākṣikeṇa vargeṇa kaphamāragvadhādinā॥
au42.99
sitā vaigandhiko drākṣā payasyā madhukaṃ madhu।
pānaṃ samantrapūtāmbuprokṣaṇaṃ sāntvaharṣaṇam।
sarpāṅgābhihate yuñjyāttathā śaṅkāviṣārdite॥
au42.100
pūtanopratakūṣmāṇḍapiśācādyā naradviṣaḥ।
hanyurauṣadhavīryāṇi rakṣākarmaṇyavāritāḥ।
tasmādrakṣāṃ prayuñjīta rakṣogaṇanivāriṇīm॥
au42.101
gomayena susammṛṣṭe dhūpāgarusudhūpite।
gandhamālyopahārādyairgṛhe pūjitadaivate॥
au42.102
sūtrakārān samabhyarcya śaṅkarāstikakāśyapān।
santarpya havyakavyābhyāṃ samiddhānanaladvijān॥
au42.103
prāṅmukhāyopaviṣṭāya viṣārtāya cikitsakaḥ।
uttarābhimukho yuñjyādvidyāṃ mantrāṇi bheṣajam॥
au42.104
samapramāṇairharitairdarbhaiḥ prāgabhimantritaiḥ।
acchinnāgraiḥ samūlaiśca kuryāttasyāpamārjanam॥
au42.105
brāhmādyai ragadairenaṃ nityamevānulepayet।
sañjīvanādīn pānādau daṃśalepe ca yojayet॥
au42.106
pūrṇakumbhaṃ sakusumaṃ sarṣapān chāgalaṃ payaḥ।
śastraṃ dūrvāṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ kuryāddaṣṭasya mūrddhataḥ।
evaṃ śāmyati saptāhādviṣamātmavataḥ sataḥ॥
au42.107
karketanaṃ marakataṃ vajraṃ vāraṇamauktikam।
vaiḍūryaṃ gardabhamaṇiṃ picukāṃ viṣamuṣṭikām॥
au42.108
himavadgirisambhūtāṃ somarājīṃ punarnavām।
tathā droṇaṃ mahādroṇaṃ mānasīṃ sarpajaṃ maṇim।
viṣāṇi viṣaśāntyarthaṃ vīryavanti ca dhārayet॥
au42.109
chatrī jharjharapāṇiśca caredrātrau viśeṣataḥ।
tacchāyāśabdavitrastāḥ praṇaśyantibhujaṅgamāḥ॥
।iti dvicatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
atha tricatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
au43.1
athātaḥ kīṭaviṣapratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ॥
au43.2
sarpāṇāmeva viṇmūtraśukrāṇḍaśavakothajāḥ।
doṣairvyastaiḥ samastaiśca yuktāḥ kīṭāścaturvidhāḥ॥
au43.3
kumbhīnasastuṇḍikerī śṛṅgī śatakulīrakaḥ।
ucciṭiṅgognināmā ca cicciṭāṅgo mayūrakaḥ।
ahijorabhrakābartaśārikāmukhavaidalāḥ॥
au43.4
śarāvakurdau paruṣaścitraśīrṣo hi jārakaḥ।
aṣṭādaśeti vāyavyāḥ kīṭā vātaprakopanāḥ॥
au43.5
kauṇḍinyakaḥ kaṇabhako varaṭī patravṛścikaḥ।
vināsikā brāhmaṇikā vindulo bhramarastathā॥
au43.6
bāhyakī picciṭaḥ kumbhī varcaḥkīṭorimedakaḥ।
dundubhiḥ padmakīṭaśca makaraḥ śatapādakaḥ॥
au43.7
pañcālaḥ pākamatsyaśca sūkṣmatuṇḍotha gardabhiḥ।
klītaḥ kṛmiśarārī ca yaścāpyutkleśakaḥ smṛtaḥ।
caturviṃśatirāgreyāḥ kīṭāḥ pittavikāradāḥ॥
au43.8
viśvambharaḥ pañcaśuṣkaḥ pañcakṛṣṇotha kokilaḥ।
sthairyakaḥ pracalākaśca vaṭabhaḥ kiṭibho jaṭī॥
au43.9
sūcīmukhaḥ kṛṣṇagodhā dabhraḥ kāṣāyavāsikaḥ।
trayodaśaite nirdiṣṭāḥ saumyāḥ śleṣmaprakopaṇāḥ॥
au43.10
tuṅganāsaścipilakastālako vāhakastathā।
koṣṭhāgārī kṛmikaro yaśca maṇḍalapucchakaḥ॥
au43.11
tuṇḍanābhaḥ sarṣapako madguliḥ śambukastathā।
agnikīṭaśca saṅkīrṇā dvādaśa prāṇanāśanāḥ॥
au43.12
daṣṭasyakīṭairvāyavyairdaṃśastodarujolbaṇaḥ।
āgneyairalpasaṃsrāvo dāharāgavisarpavān।
pakkapīluphalaprakhyaḥ kharjūrasadṛśotha vā॥
au43.13
kaphādhikairmandarujaḥ pakkodumbarasannibhaḥ।
srāvāḍhyaḥsarvaliṅgastudaṃśaḥ syātsānnipātikaiḥ॥
au43.14
vegāśca sarpavacchopho varddhiṣṇurvisraraktatā।
śirokṣigauravaṃ mūrcchā bhramaḥ śvāsotivedanā॥
au43.15
sarveṣāṃ karṇikā śopho jvaraḥ kaṇḍūrarocakaḥ॥
au43.16
vātikaḥ pakṣavātena sparśāddaśati paittikaḥ।
mukhena ślaiṣmikaḥ kīṭaḥ sarvathā sānnipātikaḥ॥
au43.17
daṣṭasya kaṇabhaiḥ śopho visarpo vamathurjvaraḥ।
daṃśaśca karṇikākāraḥ śyāvarakto viśīryate॥
au43.18
trikaṇṭakaistu daṣṭasya nānāvarṇotha vā sitaḥ।
daṃśo bhavecchvayathumān moho bhedaśca varcasaḥ॥
au43.19
kṛkalāserddhacandrābhaḥ srāvavāt bhṛśalohitaḥ।
daṃśo raktaiścitaḥ sphoṭaiḥ saśūlairdambhavodbhavaḥ॥
au43.20
ekadaṃṣṭrārpitaḥ pītaḥ kaṇḍūmān dārduraḥ saruk।
daṃśo daṣṭaḥ satṛṇnidro mūrcchāvān haritaṃ vamet॥
au43.21
mātsyo daṃśaḥ sarugdāhaḥ prāgevokto jalaukasām।
viśvambharakṛto daṃśaḥ śophakaṇḍūrujānvitaḥ।
kaphodvamamatīsāraṃ kurute koṭhajanma ca॥
au43.22
pītaḥ śatapadīdaṃśaḥ svedarugrāgaśophavān।
atasīpuṣpavarṇo vā piṭakāvān bhramagradaḥ॥
au43.23
gṛhagodhikayā sghedatodaśvayathudāhavān।
kledī ca daṃśo daṣṭasya hṛspīḍā granthisambhavaḥ॥
au43.24
kaṇḍūmān maśakairīṣacchvayathurmandavedanaḥ।
asādhyakīṭasadṛśamasādhyamaśakakṣatam॥
au43.25
prāyeṇa makṣikā netre daśanti śvayathūlvaṇaḥ।
taddaṃśo dāhakaṇḍūmāṃstāsāṃ tu sthālikāṃ tyajet।
tadṛṣṭe piṭakā śyāvā srāviṇī bhūryupadravā॥
au43.26
rugvān pipīlikādaṃśo vahnineva ca dahyate॥
au43.27
jalabindunibhaiḥ sphoṭairdāhakaṇḍūrujānvitaiḥ।
yat gātramācitaṃ soṣma tadvidyādavamūtritam॥
au43.28
vṛścikasya viṣaṃ tīkṣṇamādau dahati vahnivat।
ūrdhvamārohati kṣipraṃ daṃśe paścāttu tiṣṭhati।
daṃśaḥ sadyotiruk śyāvastudyate sphuṭatīva ca॥
au43.29
te gavādiśakṛtkothaddigdhadaṣṭādikothataḥ।
sarpakothācca sambhūtā mandamadhyamahāviṣāḥ॥
au43.30
mandāḥ pītāḥ sitāḥ śyāvā rukṣāḥ karburamecakāḥ।
romaśā bahuparvāṇo lohitāḥ pāṇḍurodarāḥ॥
au43.31
dhūmrodarāstriparvāṇo madhyāstu kapilāruṇāḥ॥
au43.32
piśaṅgāḥ śabalāścitrāḥ śoṇitābhā mahāviṣāḥ॥
au43.33
agnyābhā dvyekaparyāṇo raktāsitasitodarāḥ॥
au43.34
tairdaṣṭaḥ śūnarasanaḥ stabdhagātro rujārditaḥ।
kharvaman śoṇitaṃ kṛṣṇamindriyārthanasaṃvidan॥
au43.35
svidyan mūrcchan viśuṣkāsyo vihṇalo vedanāturaḥ।
viśīryamāṇamāṃsaśca prāyaśo vijahātyasūn॥
au43.36
ucciṭiṅgastu vaktreṇa daśatyabhyadhikavyathaḥ॥
au43.37
sādhyato vṛścikāt stambhaṃ śephaso hṛṣṭaromatām।
karoti sekamaṅgānāṃ daṃśaḥ śītāmbuneva ca॥
au43.38
uṣṭravarṇatayā proktaḥ sa eva hyuṣṭradhūmakaḥ।
rātriko rātricārācca pṛthak tu kaṇabhādiṣu।
vikārasādhanābhedāt bhedāḥ santopi noditāḥ॥
au43.39
vātapittottarāḥ kīṭā ślaiṣmikāḥ kaṇabhondurāḥ।
prāyo vātolbaṇaviṣā vaścikāḥ soṣṭradhūmakāḥ॥
au43.40
yatra yasyaiva doṣasya liṅgādhikyaṃ pratarkayet।
tatra tasyauṣadhaiḥ kuryādviparītaguṇaiḥ kriyām॥
au43.41
hṛtpīḍordhvānilaḥ stambhāḥ sirāyāmosthi parvaruk।
ghūrṇanodveṣṭanaṃ gātraśyāvatā vātike viṣe॥
au43.42
saṃjñānāśoṣṇaniśvāsau hṛdāhaḥ kaṭukāsyatā।
māṃsāvadaraṇaṃ śopho raktapittaṃ ca paittike॥
au43.43
chardyarocakahṛllāsaprasekotkleśapīnasaiḥ।
saśaityamukhamādhuryairvidyācchraleṣmādhikaṃviṣam॥
au43.44
piṇyākena vraṇālepastailābhyaṅgaśca vātike।
svedo nāḍīpulākādyairbṛṃhaṇaśca vidhirhitaḥ॥
au43.45
paittikaṃ stambhayet sekaiḥ pradehaiścātiśītalaiḥ॥
au43.46
lekhanacchedanasvedavamanaiḥ ślaiṣmikaṃ jayet॥
au43.47
kīṭānāṃ triprakārāṇāṃ traividhyena kriyā hitā॥
au43.48
ssvedālepanasekāṃstu koṣṇān prāyovacārayet।
anyatra mūrcchitāddaṃśapākataḥ kothatopi vā॥
au43.49
nṛkeśāḥ sarṣapāḥ pītā guḍo jīrṇaśca dhūpanam।
viṣadaṃśasya sarvasya kāśyapaḥ paramabravīt॥
au43.50
viṣaghnaṃ ca vidhiṃ sarvaṃ kuryāt saṃśodhanāni ca॥
au43.51
sādhayet sarpavaddaṣṭān viṣograiḥ kīṭavṛścikaiḥ॥
asa43.52। taṇḍulīyakatulyāṃśāṃ trivṛtāṃ sarpiṣā piben।
yāti kīṭaviṣaiḥ kampaṃ na kailāsa ivānilaiḥ॥
au43.53
kṣīrivṛkṣatvagālepaḥ śuddhe kīṭaviṣāpahaḥ।
muktālepo varaḥ śophatodadāhajvarapraṇut॥
au43.54
vacā hiṅguviḍaṅgāni saindhavaṃ gajapippalī।
pāṭhāprativiṣāvyoṣaṃ kāśyayena vinirmitam।
daśāṅgamagadaṃ pītvā sarvakīṭaviṣaṃ jayet॥
au43.55
aikadhyaṃ kīṭaviṣajinmahāsnehaṃ payo madhu।
śikhikukkuṭajaiḥ picchaiḥ satailalavaṇottamaiḥ।
dhūpo hanti kṛtaḥ śīghraṃ kīṭavṛścikajaṃ viṣam॥
au43.56
viṣe kaṇabhaje kuryādunduroktamupakramam।
śirīṣabījaṃ maṇḍūke lepaḥ snukkṣīrakalkitam।
madhu trikaṭukaṃ śvetapiṇḍāmūlaṃ ca matsyaje॥
au43.57
vacāṃ vaṃśatvacaṃ pāṭhāṃ nataṃ surasamañjarīm।
dve bale nākulīṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śirīṣaṃ rajanīdvayam॥
au43.58
guhāmatiguhāṃ śvetāmajagandhāṃ śilājatu।
kattṛṇaṃ kaṭabhīkṣāraṃ gṛhadhūmaṃ bhanaśśilām॥
au43.59
rohītakaṃ ca pittena kalkayet sa varo'gadaḥ।
viśvambharādiṣvālepanāvanāñjanapānataḥ॥
au43.60
svarjikājaśakṛtkṣāraḥ surasaḥ sākṣipīḍakaḥ।
madirāmaṇḍasaṃyukto hitaḥ śatapadīviṣe॥
au43.61
kapitthamakṣipīḍorkabījaṃ trikaṭukānvitam।
karañjo dve haridre ca gṛhagodhīviṣāpahaḥ॥
au43.62
kākāṇḍayuktaḥ sarveṣāṃ viṣāṇāṃ taṇḍulīyakaḥ।
praśasto barhiṇoṇḍena tadvadvāyasapīlukaḥ॥
au43.63
tagaraṃ nāgaraṃ nāgakesaraṃ maricāni ca।
prayuktaṃ pānalepābhyāṃ makṣikāviṣanāśanam॥
au43.64
sitāsite ca lavaṇe maricaṃ ca sanāgaram।
phaṇijjakarasopetaṃ varaṭīnāṃ viṣāpaham॥
au43.65
sadyo vṛścikajaṃ daṃśaṃ cakratailena secayet।
vidārigandhāsiddhena kavoṣṇenetareṇa vā॥
au43.66
lavaṇottamayuktena sarpiṣā vā punaḥ punaḥ।
siñcetkoṣṇāranālena sakṣīralavaṇena vā।
upanāho ghṛte bhṛṣṭaḥ kalkojājyāḥ sasaindhavaḥ॥
au43.67
ādaṃśaṃ sveditaṃ cūrṇaiḥ pracchāya pratisārayet।
rajanīsaindhavavyoṣaśirīṣaphalapuṣpajaiḥ॥
au43.68
mātuluṅgāmlagomūtrapiṣṭaṃ ca surasāgrajam।
lepaḥ sukhoṣṇaśca hitaḥ piṇyāko gomayopi vā॥
au43.69
pāne sarpirmadhuyutaṃ kṣīraṃ vā bhūriśarkaram।
guḍodakaṃ vā suhimaṃ cāturjātakavāsitam॥
au43.70
palāśabījaṃ śūlaghno leporkakṣīrabhāvitam।
pārāvataśakutpathyā tagaraṃ viśvabheṣajam।
bīja pūrarasonmiśraṃ varo'yaṃ vṛścikāgadaḥ॥
au43.71
manohnā saindhavaṃ hiṅgu mālatīpallavāni ca।
gośakṛdrasapiṣṭeyaṃ guṭikā vṛścikārdite॥
au43.72
laśuno maricaṃ hiṅgu surasaṃ viśvabheṣajam।
arkakṣīreṇa guṭikā vṛścikārditaśaṅkarī॥
au43.73
saśaivaloṣṭradaṃṣṭrā ca hanti vṛścikajaṃ viṣam॥
au43.74
hiṅgunā haritālena mātuluṅgarasena ca।
lepāñjanābhyāṃ guṭikā paramaṃ vṛścikāpahā॥
au43.75
karañjārjunaśelūnāṃ kaṭabhyāḥ kuṭajasya ca।
śirīṣasya ca puṣpāṇi mastunā daṃśalepanam॥
au43.76
pippalīṃ maricaṃ yaṣṭiṃ śvetāṃ surasamañjarīm।
sahadevāmapāmārgaṃ taṇḍulīyaṃ ca kalkayet।
kutalakṣāratoyena lepo'liviṣanāśanaḥ॥
au43.77
yo muhyati praśvasiti pralapatyugravedanaḥ।
tasya pathyāniśākṛṣṇāmañjiṣṭhātiviṣoṣaṇam।
sālābuvṛntaṃ vārtākarasapiṣṭaṃ pralepanam॥
au43.78
ādaṃśe yasya kaṇḍūḥsyāt kothaḥ koṭhaṃ ca dāruṇam।
tasya lepastrikaṭukaṃ yavakṣārokṣipīḍakaḥ॥
au43.79
pārāvataśakṛtkāntāsvarjjikāgnihareṇavaḥ।
rasena mātuluṅgasya kṣīreṇārkasyavā drutāḥ॥
au43.80
hṛdayaṃ pīḍyate yasya mūrcchā cimicimāyanam।
dantauṣṭhadaṃśo romṇāṃ ca harṣastasya nivartate।
vego viṣasya pañcāhānnaiva vā kriyayā vinā॥
au43.81
tatra kurvīta daṃśasya lepanaṃ mastukalkitaiḥ।
śvetapāṭalyativiṣāharidrāhariṇīnataiḥ।
bilvamūlayavakṣārasūkṣmamāgadhikāyutaiḥ॥
au43.82
utkṛtyata ivādaṃśaḥ śūnaḥ klinno hatacchaviḥ।
jambūphalanibhaṃ raktaṃ kūjan vamati veṣṭate॥
au43.83
indriyārthaṃ na jānāti prasvidyati ca yo muhuḥ।
svarjikākuṣṭhatagaranākulīpīlupippalīḥ।
bṛhatīṃ cācchasurayā tasya piṣṭvā vilepanam॥
au43.84
sarvatra cogrāliviṣe pāyayenmadhusarpiṣī।
vidhyet sirāṃ vidadhyācca vamanāñjananāvanam।
uṣṇasnigdhāmlamadhuraṃ bhojanaṃ cānilāpaham॥
au43.85
nāgaraṃ gṛhakapotapurīṣaṃ bījapūrakaraso haritālam।
saindhavaṃ ca vinihantyagado'yaṃ lepato'likulajaṃ viṣamāśu॥
au43.86
ante vṛścikadaṣṭānāṃ samudīrṇe bhṛśaṃ viṣe।
viṣeṇālepayeddaṃśaṃ sthāvareṇa yathocitam॥
au43.87
kriyeyamucciṭiṅgepi pratilomaṃ ca pāṃsubhiḥ।
udvartanaṃ sukhāmloṣṇaistathā pracchādanaṃ ghanaiḥ॥
au43.88
kuṭajasya phalaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ mālatī phalinī natam।
tiktekṣvākuśca piṣṭāni pānapnadhdmanādibhiḥ॥
au43.89
vṛścikondurulūtānāṃ sarpāṇāṃ ca viṣāpaham।
samānamamṛtenedaṃ garaśeṣaṃ ca nāśayet॥
au43.90
arkasya dugdhena śirīṣabījaṃ trirbhāvitaṃ pippalicūrṇamiśram।
eṣo'gado hanti viṣāṇi kīṭabhujaṅgalūtonduruvṛścikānām॥
।iti tricatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
atha catuścatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
au44.1
athāto lūtāpratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ॥
au44.2
viśvāmitrāya ruṣṭasya vasiṣṭhasya lalāṭajāḥ।
svedaleśāḥ smṛtā lūtā lūne ye patitāstṛṇe॥
au44.3
khāṇḍave dahyamānānāmasurāṇāṃ śarīrataḥ।
ye sphuliṅgā viniśceruste lūtā iti kecana॥
au44.4
anye vadanti bhuktasya duṣṭasyānnasya mūrcchanāt।
sambhavanti viṣasphoṭā ye lūtāḥ kīṭalakṣaṇam।
yathāsvaṃ dhārayantaste lūtāḥ kīṭāśca saṃjñitāḥ॥
au44.5
tatra ghoratamā lūtā bhidyante tā api tridhā।
takṣṇimadhyāvaratvena ghnanti vāśvacikitsitāḥ।
saptāhena daśāhena pakṣeṇa ca paraṃ kramāt॥
au44.6
kapilāgnimukhī pītā padmā mūtrā sitāsitā।
āgneyyaḥ svedajāḥ sapta lūtāḥ pittavikāradāḥ॥
au44.7
pāṇḍurā raktapadikā bhṛṅgā piṅgā trimaṇḍalā।
pūtirvīrāṇḍajāḥsapta saumyāḥ śleṣmavikāradāḥ॥
au44.8
kumudālaviṣā raktā ścitrā santā nimecakā।
kasanā codbhidāḥ sapta vāyavyā vāyurogadāḥ॥
au44.9
kākāṇḍyeṇapadī lājā vaidehī jālinī tathā।
mālāguṇā suvarṇā ca miśrāḥ saptopapādikāḥ॥
asa44.10। vyāpnuvantyāśu gātrāṇi jvalatpāvakasannibhāḥ।
sannipātakṛto'sādhyāḥ sādhyāḥ kṛcchreṇacetarāḥ॥
au44.11
tā daśanti site pakṣe'site sandhau sadaiva ca॥
au44.12
daṃśaḥ sāmānyatastāsāṃ dadrumaṇḍalasannibhaḥ।
sito'sito'ruṇaḥpītaḥśyāvo vā mṛdurunnataḥ॥
au44.13
madhye kṛṣṇo'thavā śyāvaḥ paryante jālakāvṛtaḥ।
visarpavāñchophayutastapyate bahuvedanaḥ॥
au44.14
jvarāśupākavikledakothāvadaraṇānvitaḥ।
kledena yatspṛśatyaṅgaṃ tatrāpi kurute vraṇam॥
au44.15
śvāsadaṃṣṭrāśakṛnmūtraśukralālānakhārtavaiḥ।
aṣṭābhirudvamantyetā viṣaṃ vaktrādviśeṣataḥ॥
au44.16
śvāsena daṃśaḥ sahasā śūyate jvaradāhavān।
daṃṣṭrākṛtastūgrataro vivarṇaḥ kaṭhitaḥ sthiraḥ॥
au44.17
gambhīraśophavastodavedanādāhasaṃyutaḥ।
durgandhī śakṛtā dāhakaṇḍūcimicimānvitaḥ॥
au44.18
pacyate cāśu pakvaśca pāṇḍuḥ pīluphalopamaḥ।
mūtreṇa raktaparyanto madhye kṛṣṇo viśīryate॥
au44.19
āvartasadṛśaḥ śūnaḥ pūtiḥ sarpati dahyate।
śukreṇa granthisaṃsthānaḥ kaṭhinastīvravedanaḥ॥
au44.20
alpamūlolparukvoṭho lālayā kaṇḍuro mṛduḥ।
nakhena coṣapiṭakākaṇḍūdhūmāyanānvitaḥ।
kiṃśukodaravarṇastu rajasā cañcumālavān॥
au44.21
lūtā nābherdaśantyūrdhvamūrdhvaṃ cādhaśca kīṭakāḥ।
taddūṣitaṃ ca vastrādi dehe pṛktaṃ vikārakṛt॥
au44.22
dinārdhaṃ lakṣyate naiva daṃśo lūtāviṣodbhavaḥ॥
au44.23
sūcīvyadhavadābhāti tatosau prathame'hani।
avyaktavarṇaḥ pracalaḥ kiñcit kaṇḍūrujānvitaḥ॥
au44.24
dvitīye'tyunnatonteṣu piṭakairiva cācitaḥ।
vyaktavarṇo nato madhye kaṇḍūmān granthisannibhaḥ॥
au44.25
tṛtīye sajvaro romaharṣakṛdraktamaṇḍalaḥ।
śarāvarūpastodāḍhyo romakūpeṣu sāsravaḥ॥
au44.26
mahāṃścaturthe śvayathustāpaśvāsabhramapradaḥ॥
au44.27
vikārān kurute tāṃstān pañcame viṣakopajān।
ṣaṣṭhe vyāpnoti marmāṇi saptame hanti jīvita॥
au44.28
viṣamityatitīkṣṇānāmitare vibhajedataḥ॥
au44.29
viṣaṃ śāmyati sarvāsāmekaviṃśatirātrataḥ॥
au44.30
daṃśaḥ pittātmako dāhatṛṭsphoṭajvaradāhavān।
saśophaḥ kaṭhinaḥ pāṇḍuḥ kaṇḍūmān ślaiṣmikolparuk।
vātikaḥ paruṣaḥ śyāvaḥ parvabhedādirukkaraḥ॥
au44.31
sarpajñānoditairliṅgairddoṣodrekaṃ ca lakṣayet॥
au44.32
tridoṣāḥ prāyaśaḥ sarvā lūtāḥ pittakaphādhikāḥ॥
au44.33
prāṇāntikīṣu hṛnmohaśvāsahidhmāśirograhāḥ।
śvetāsitāḥ pītaraktāḥ piṭakāḥ śvayathūdbhavaḥ॥
au44.34
veputhurvamathurdāhastṛḍāndhyaṃ vakranāsatā।
śyāvoṣṭhavaktradantatvaṃ pṛṣṭhagrīvāvabhañjanam।
pakvajambūsavarṇaṃ ca daṃśāt sravati śoṇitam॥
au44.35
athāśu lūtādaṣṭasya śastreṇādaṃśamuddharet।
dahet jāṃbavoṣṭhādyairna tu pittottaraṃ dahet॥
au44.36
karkaśaṃ bhinnaromāṇaṃ marmasandhyādisāṃśritam।
prasṛtaṃ sarvato daṃśaṃ na chindīta dahet vā॥
au44.37
lepayeddagdhamagadairmadhusaindhavasaṃyutaiḥ।
suśītaiḥ secayeccānu kaṣāyaiḥ kṣīrivṛkṣajaiḥ॥
au44.38
sarvatopaharedraktaṃ śṛṅgādyaiḥ sirayāpi vā।
srute rakte parīṣeko ghṛtakṣīrādibhirhitaḥ॥
au44.39
prapauṇḍarīkaddrīberasārivośīrajīvakāḥ।
lodhracandanajīvantīmañjiṣṭhāsarjavañjulāḥ॥
au44.40
mṛṇālabisaśaivālakumudotpalagairikāḥ।
nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthaniculaplakṣavetasāḥ॥
au44.41
samaṅgāpāṭalīgundrākākolīśataparvikāḥ।
śirīṣadhātakīmūrvāvidārīpadmakiṃśukāḥ॥
au44.42
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ kośavatīvāyasīsomarājayaḥ।
madhukāṃśumatīmūrvā yathālābhaṃ samāhṛtāḥ।
śastaḥ paryuṣito lepaḥ saghṛtaḥ paittike varṇe॥
au44.43
śyāmādvayaniśāmustānakharāsnāmahāsahāḥ।
vāsāpattaṅgasuvahānākulīgirikarṇikāḥ॥
au44.44
sarpagandhāyavaphalānirguṇḍyaśmantakasthirāḥ।
śukākhyā mahiṣakrāntā kuṣṭhendrayavakuṅkumam॥
au44.45
karavīrāgarunataṃ sugandhā sinduvārakam।
āsphoṭagundrā ca hitā pralepaḥ ślaiṣmike viṣe॥
au44.46
bimbīvidulabandhūkakovidārapalāśakāḥ।
suvahāriṣṭakabrāhmīguḍūcīviśvasairyakāḥ॥
au44.47
siddhārthakā devadāru viḍaṅgānīndravāruṇī।
śatāvarīlāṅgalikīrājavṛkṣapunarnavāḥ॥
au44.48
jīvantī vāyasī bhārṅgī katakendrayavārjunāḥ।
misivyāghrapadīsiṃhapucchīmaṇḍalaparṇikāḥ॥
au44.49
śvadaṃṣṭrā kolabṛhatī revatī śvetapuṣpikā।
prapunnāṭaḥ kuravakaḥ pralepo vātike viṣe॥
au44.50
sarvatraiva ca śasyante bodhiśleṣmātakākṣakāḥ॥
au44.51
udīrṇadoṣān balino viṣe mahati vābhayen।
kākaṇḍakīkośavatī lodhrendrayavasaindhavaiḥ॥
au44.52
paṭolapatramaricakaraghāṭapriyaṅgubhiḥ।
kṛṣṇāśukanasānīpanimbasaptāhvayaṣṭibhiḥ॥
au44.53
virecayecca triphalātrivṛttrikaṭusaindhavaiḥ।
sadantīpūgamṛdvīkā viḍaṅgairathavā pacet।
ebhiḥ palārdhikaiḥ prasthaṃ samabrāhmīrasaṃ ghṛtāt॥
au44.54
pañcamūlaśṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ toyaṃ vā śodhanauṣadhaiḥ।
yathāsvaṃ kalkitairyuktaṃ pṛthagdadyādvirecanam॥
au44.55
pippalīpippalīmūlaśuṇṭhīndrayavasaindhavaiḥ।
pāṭhājamodāyaṣṭyāhvamustāsarṣapadārubhiḥ॥
au44.56
laghunā pañcamūlena saralena ca sādhitā।
peyā saṃsarjane yojyā saghṛtā viṣanāśinī॥
au44.57
ādhmānahidhmāśvāseṣu pṛṣṭhagrīvāvabhañjane।
saṅkocastambhakampeṣu śūleṣvardhāvabhedake॥
au44.58
vātarogeṣu cānyeṣu parvabhedārditādiṣu।
eraṇḍavilvasaralacirivilvārkapāṭalīḥ॥
au44.59
śigrupāṭhā kuśavṛṣaṃ vidulaṃ ca jale pacet।
kanīyaḥ paścamūlaṃ ca tasmin maṇḍaṃ pacet ghṛtāt॥
au44.60
dviguṇe tulyagokṣīre piṣṭairyaṣṭīniśānataiḥ।
surāhvavellasaralaśatāhvālodhragairikaiḥ॥
au44.61
payasyākuṣṭhāgāṅgeyīkṛṣṇāmadanasaindhavaiḥ।
bastau pratyāgateśnīyāt pañcamūlānvitaiḥ rasaiḥ॥
au44.62
nāvanaṃ gaurave śophe lālāsrāve hanugrahe।
girikarṇī phalasaro bandhūkaṃ kiṇihī sitā॥
au44.63
ṣaḍgranthālaśunavyoṣabṛhatīvellasaindhavam।
apāmārgaphalaṃ bhārṅgī nākulī sarpagandhikā॥
au44.64
śyāmā yavaphalā bījaṃ phaṇijjakaśirīṣayoḥ।
vārtākarasapiṣṭāni nasyaṃ viṣaharaṃ param॥
au44.65
viriktaśirasaścāsya sarpirmaṇḍonu nāvanam॥
au44.66
netroparodhaśvayathukaṇḍūnidrāsamāgame।
vacāmanohvātrikaṭutriphalālodhragairikāḥ॥
au44.67
śaṅkho nīlotpalaṃ tāmraṃ hema pravālakam।
jīvantī laśunaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ katakaṃ mārkavaṃ natam॥
au44.68
prapaiṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ karañjaphalasaindhavam।
niśe phaṇijjakaṃ tutthaṃ srotoñjanarasāñjane।
meṣaśṛṅgayāśca kusumaṃ piṣṭaṃ govāriṇāñjanam॥
au44.69
surasaprasavavyoṣavilvamūlasurāhvayam।
haridrā chāgalīmūtraṃ lūtākīṭaghnamañjanam॥
au44.70
śirīṣapadmakośīrapāṭalīsinduvārakam।
kṣīriśuṅganatodīcyasārivākuṣṭhacandanam॥
au44.71
śelusvarasapiṣṭoyamagado nāvaneñjane।
pāne pralepe seke ca lūtāsu paramaṃ hitaḥ॥
au44.72
payasyā madhumṛdvīkāśvadaṃṣṭrākṣīramoraṭāḥ।
gojīvidārīyaṣṭyāhvamadhukāni ca tadguṇaḥ॥
au44.73
tathā śirīṣakusumaṃ candralekhodbhavaṃ phalam।
surālā kaṭabhī jātiḥ śvetā ca girikarṇikā॥
au44.74
tadvacca yuñjyāttagarakuṣṭhanāgabalābalāḥ॥
au44.75
haridrāyugalaṃ nāgadantī lodhraṃ ca śābaram।
śirīṣapuṣpaṃ tagaraṃ sahadevā śatāvarī॥
au44.76
punarnavā nāgabalā sarpagandhā kuṭannaṭam।
gavādanī dantaśaṭhasomavalkendurājayaḥ।
viṣeṣu sarveṣvagadaḥ sakṣaudraḥ sarvakarmakṛt॥
au44.77
sarpākṣī candanaṃ vakraṃ mṛgākṣī gandhanākulī।
elā mahāsugandhā ca bastamūtreṇa kalkitaḥ।
lepe pāne ca lūtāsu nānena sadṛśogadaḥ॥
au44.78
kaṭabhīmūlatagarasamaṅgodavadārubhiḥ।
bṛhatīdvayagāṅgeyīrocanācandanairghṛtam॥
au44.79
siddhaṃ caturguṇakṣīraṃ pānābhyañjanayorhitam।
lūtākaṇabhakīṭānāṃ viṣe paramadāruṇe॥
au44.80
nivṛtte dāhaśophādau karṇikāṃ pātayedvraṇāt॥
au44.81
kusumbhapuṣpaṃ godantaḥ svarṇakṣīrī kapotaviṭ।
trivṛtā saindhavaṃ dantī karṇikāpātanaṃ tathā॥
au44.82
haridrā gugguluḥ kiṇvaṃ vaṃśalekhaḥ kapotaviḍ।
tadvacca saindhavaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ dantīkaṭukadaugdhikam।
rājakrośātakīmūlaṃ kiṇvo vā mathitodbhavaḥ॥
au44.83
karṇikāpātasamaye bṛṃhayeta viṣāpahaiḥ॥
au44.84
ṛtukāle ca lūtānāṃ yāvantaḥ śukravindavaḥ।
dehe patanti tāvatyo jāyante karṇikāḥ samam॥
au44.85
godantadantī trivṛtā haridre saindhavaṃ tilāḥ।
madhukaṃ nimbapatrāṇi ghṛtaṃ ca vraṇaśodhanam॥
au44.86
kāntāviḍaṅgakhadiranimbakampillakāmbudaiḥ।
sarjailādhātakīlohaiḥ siddhaṃ sarpirvraṇāpaham॥
au44.87
śirīṣakaṭabhīśelukṣīrivṛkṣārjunatvacaḥ।
kalkacūrṇaparīṣekaiḥ kīṭalūtāvraṇāpahāḥ॥
au44.88
śatāhvālodhrakāsīsadārvījambvasthirocanāḥ।
harītakī pūgaphalaṃ cūrṇoyaṃ vraṇaropaṇaḥ॥
au44.89
lākṣā rajanyau mañjiṣṭhā haritālaṃ manaśśilā।
sarpirmadhu ca lepoyaṃ tvagviśuddhikaraḥ param॥
au44.90
romasañjananaṃ kuryādyaduktaṃ vraṇasādhane॥
au44.91
snehakāryamaśeṣaṃ ca sarpiṣaiva samācaret।
viṣasya vṛddhaye tailamagneriva tṛṇolapam॥
॥iti catuścatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ॥
atha pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
au45.1
athātaḥ pratyekalūtāpratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ॥
au45.2
ādaṃśe piṭakā tāmrā bhavet kapilayā sthirā।
lasīkā romakūpeṣu dāho'kṣṇo mūrdhni gauravam॥
au45.3
pānanasyāñjanālepasekeṣvatra prayojayet।
niśāpadmakakuṣṭhailākarañjakakubhatvacaḥ॥
au45.4
sthirārkaparṇyapāmārgabrāhmījvalananākulīḥ।
athavā kuṣṭhapattaṅganakhajoṅgakakuṅkumam॥
au45.5
agnimukhyātiruksphoṭaḥ sambhavatyagnidagdhavat।
agnijvālāsamānena prasvidyati viṣoṣmaṇā॥
au45.6
tṛḍdāhakampamūrcchāvān pittāsramatisāryate।
yojayet pūrvavattatra pratyākhyāya tvarānvitaḥ॥
au45.7
kuṣṭhalāmajjakośīramadhūkaṃ madhukaṃ madhu।
lābhataḥ śītavīryāṇi tālīsaṃ gopakanyakām॥
au45.8
pītayā pītaviṇmūtradaṃśakledākṣidarśanam।
mūrcchācchardiṃśiroduḥkhajvarārocakaśūlavān॥
au45.9
tatreṣṭāḥ kaṭabhośīramuñjāvañjulapadmakāḥ।
vaṃśakāśārjunakuśāḥ śirīṣakiṇihītvacaḥ।
athavā vanyabālhīkakuṣṭhakesarajoṅgapham॥
au45.10
padmābhaḥ padmayā sphoṭo bhinno'bhinnaḥ punarbhavet।
klidyatyāśu sravatyuṣṇaṃ kledaṃ sparśe'tirukkaraḥ॥
au45.11
tatra padmotpalānnālo himavetasavañjulāḥ।
samṛṇālāḥ sakumudāḥ sakṣaudraghṛtaśarkarāḥ॥
au45.12
pūtirmūtraviṣādaṃśo visarpī kṛṣṇaśoṇitaḥ।
śvāsakāsajvaracchardiṃmūrchādāhabhramānvitaḥ॥
au45.13
manaśśilālamadhukamadhūkotpalacandanam।
kuṣṭhālāmajjakośīrapadmakaṃ tatra bheṣajam॥
au45.14
ādaṃśe śvetayā śvetā piṭakā bhṛśakaṇḍulā।
dāhamūrchājvararujāvisarpakledakāriṇī॥
au45.15
tatreṣṭāḥ śītarāsnailāhareṇunalavañjulāḥ।
kuṣṭhamāṃsīnatośīrakāntādhyāmakapadmakāḥ॥
au45.16
ādaṃśaḥ kṛṣṇayā kṛṣṇo viṅgandhiḥ kledaśophavān।
utthāpyate kṛṣṇamasṛgduṣṭaṃ tatra ca bheṣajam।
mahāsugandhā sarpakṣī vakrailā gandhanākulī॥
au45.17
śūnaḥ pāṇḍūrayā daṃśaḥ śopho vaktrasya gauravam।
jvaro vighūrṇanaṃ jṛmbhā śiroruk tatra bheṣajam।
mūlaṃ vāruṇapuṣpāyā rocanā gośakṛdrasaḥ॥
au45.18
āpāṇḍupiṭako daṃśaḥ śophavān raktapādayā।
asrasruttatra naladasevyodīcyahimaṃ madhu॥
au45.19
bhṛṅgābho bhṛṅgayā daṃśaḥ piṭakā dāharukkarī।
koṭhaiśca cīyate gātraṃ tatra śastaṃ bhiṣagjitam।
aṅkolasāraḥ phalinī gavāṃ pittaṃ misirgadaḥ॥
au45.20
piṅgayā vahnidagdhābho daṃśaḥ sphoṭo bahusrutiḥ।
tībraśophajvararujāhṛtpīḍādāhatṛṅyutaḥ॥
au45.21
tatrāgadaḥ sitā gundrā mallikā madhukotpalam।
jīvaṃkaḥ kṣīriṇāṃ śuṅgā dvihimaṃ nāgakesaram॥
au45.22
trimaṇḍalāyā bahalo daṃśaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ sravatyasṛk।
arucirnetrayordāhaḥ kaluṣasrutidṛṣṭitā॥
au45.23
vividhairmaṇḍalaiścāsya śarīramupacīyate।
tatrārkamūladviniśāsurālāpṛśniparṇikāḥ।
dadhitthanākulībrāhmījyotiṣmatyo hito'gadaḥ॥
au45.24
ādaṃśaḥ pūtigandhāyā visarpakledadāhavān।
alajīsannibho rugvān vibaddhapiṭakācitaḥ॥
au45.25
bhārṅgīnidigdhikānimbapāṭalīsinduvārakam।
dūrvā haridre vāsā ca pūtigandhāviṣāpaham॥
au45.26
citramaṇḍalavān daṃśaḥ piṭakājālakāvṛtaḥ।
vīrāyā mūrdharuk śītajvarānnadveṣasaṃyutaḥ॥
au45.27
haridre naladaṃ kuṣṭhamelā surasamañjarī।
tagaraṃ ca śvapittena piṣṭaṃ vīrāviṣāpaham॥
au45.28
daṃśaḥ kumudayā dāhasphoṭasphuraṇatodavān।
picchilakledavisrāvī saśvāsassagalagrahaḥ।
pratyākhyāyātra kurvīta sāmānyoktaṃ kriyākramam॥
au45.29
bhavantyalaviṣādaṃśe pītalohitamaṇḍalāḥ।
piṭakāḥ sarṣapaprakhyāstāluśoṣo rujā jvaraḥ॥
au45.30
chardirdāhaḥ śiraḥkampastatra sevyaḥ samākṣikaḥ।
sakāsīsakahrīberaḥ sapippalivaṭāṅkuraḥ॥
au45.31
raktānto raktayā daṃśaḥ sapāṇḍupiṭakājvaraḥ।
śvetotisāraḥ śvasanaṃ dāhaḥ kledaḥ saśoṇitaḥ।
śastaṃ śelvarjunāmrātāttvaṅmūlaṃ sinduvārataḥ॥
au45.32
ādaṃśe citrayā raktā piṭakā visṛtā sthirā।
parvabhedaśirastāpajvaraśophā visarpiṇī॥
au45.33
bhinnā kṛṣṇatvamabhyeti pītāsrāvā mahāvraṇā।
tatreṣṭāḥ kuṣṭhanaladaśirīṣanalareṇukāḥ॥
au45.34
daṃśe ca santānikayā śūlamākulatāśruṇaḥ।
pradarākṣepakau tatra kesaraṃ kṣīriṇāṃ tvacaḥ।
āmrasya sinduvārasya mūlamaśmantakasya ca॥
au45.35
piṭakā mecakā daṃśamadhye jatukaṇopamā।
jvaraḥ śophotra vāruṇyāṃ rocanā rajanīdvayam॥
au45.36
rājīmān kasanādaṃśaḥ śiroruk śvāsakāsavān।
śītapicchilaraktasrudraktokaṃ tatra meṣajam॥
au45.37
pāṇḍurakto'tirugdaṃśaḥ kākāṇḍyāḥ smṛtimoṣakṛt।
hidhmā śvasanatṛṇmūrcchā nidrākṣepakahṛdgadāḥ॥
au45.38
raktāntarstveṇapādāyā daṃśaḥ kṛṣṇatilākṛtiḥ।
dāhamohāgnivīsarpatṛṅvamiśvāsakāsavān॥
au45.39
pūtiḥ śyāvotiruk sāsṛgādaṃśo lājavarṇayā।
śītajvarasamutthāno dāhamūrchātisāravān॥
au45.40
agnidagdhanibho daṃśo vaidehyā bhṛśavedanaḥ।
gambhīraḥ sajvarastīkṣṇamoho hṛdayapīḍanam॥
au45.41
ūrdhvarājīcito daṃśo jālinyāstīvraśopharuk।
udīrṇatṛṅbhramaśvāsastambhamohavidīryate॥
au45.42
rakto mālāguṇādaṃśo dhūmagandhiḥ sapīvraruk।
dīryate pārśvatastaistaiḥ saṃrabdhairmaṇḍalairyutaḥ॥
au45.43
antardāho bahiḥ śaityamādhmānaṃ mūtrakṛcchratā।
mūrcchāpralāpātīsārajvarāḥ prāṇāntakāriṇaḥ॥
au45.44
dhmātaḥ sauvarṇikādaṃśaḥ syandate matsyagandhikaḥ।
śirokṣirugjvaraḥ kāsastṛṇā śopho vamirbhramaḥ॥
au45.45
āsādhyānāmapi hitaṃ pratyākhyāyāśu yojayet।
doṣocchrāyaviśeṣeṇa chedadāhādivarjitam॥
au45.46
kapilā tatra nāsāyāmagnirdaśati jatruṇi।
pītā tu gaṇḍayoḥ padmā dakṣiṇāṃsetha kakṣayoḥ॥
au45.47
lūtā mūtraviṣā śvetā cibuke kālikākṣiṇi।
pāṇḍurā dakṣiṇaskandhe karayo raktapādikā॥
au45.48
vāmapārśve daśet bhṛṅgā vāmāṃse piṅgalā daśet।
trimaṇḍalodare pūtiḥ pṛṣṭhe vīrā tu dakṣiṇe॥
au45.49
bāhau nābhyāṃ kumudikā vāmaskandhe'lasaṃjñitā।
kaṇṭhe raktā lalāṭe tu citrā santānikauṣṭhayoḥ॥
au45.50
mecakā mūrdhni kasanāddhastayoḥ kakṣamūlayoḥ।
kākāṇḍyeṇī tu hṛdaye lājavarṇā stanāntare॥
au45.51
bāhusandhiṣu vaidehī lūtāpāṅge tu jālinī।
mālāguṇākhyā grīvāyāṃ sauvarṇī karṇamūlayoḥ॥
au45.52
iti kṣetrāṇi niyatānyatyudīrṇaviṣāḥ punaḥ।
parakṣetrepi vartante rājānotibalā iva॥
॥iti pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ॥

au46.1
athāto mūṣikālarkapratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ॥
au46.2
lālanaścapalaḥ putro hasiraścikiro'jinaḥ।
kaṣāyadantaḥ kulakaḥ kokilaḥ kapilo'sitaḥ॥
au46.3
aruṇaḥ śabalaḥ śvetaḥ kapotaḥ palitonduruḥ।
cucchundāro rasālākhyo daśāṣṭau ceti mūṣikāḥ॥
au46.4
yasminnaṅge patatyeṣāṃ śukramaṅgaiḥ spṛśanti vā।
yacchukradigdhaistatrāsre dūṣite pāṇḍutāṃ gate॥
au46.5
granthayaḥ śvayathuḥ koṭho maṇḍalāni bhramoruciḥ।
śītajvararotiruksādo vepathuḥ parvabhedanam॥
au46.6
romaharṣaḥ snutirmūrcchā dīrghakālānubandhanam।
śleṣmānuviddhabahvākhupotakachardanaṃ sakṛt॥
au46.7
vyavāyyākhuviṣaṃ kṛcchraṃ bhūyo bhūyaśca kupyati॥
au46.8
mūrcchāṅgaśophavaivarṇyakledaśabdāśrutijvarāḥ।
śirogurutvaṃ lālāsṛkchardiścāsādhyalakṣaṇam॥
au46.9
śūnabastiṃ vivarṇauṣṭhamākhvābhairgranthibhiścitam।
cucchundurusagandhaṃ ca varjayedākhudūṣitam॥
au46.10
śunaḥ śleṣmolbaṇā doṣāḥ saṃjñāṃ saṃjñāvahāśritāḥ।
muṣṇantaḥ kurvate kṣobhaṃ dhātūnāmatidāruṇam॥
au46.11
lālāvānandhabadhiraḥ sarvataḥ sobhidhāvati।
srastapucchahanuskandhaḥ śiroduḥkhī natānanaḥ॥
au46.12
daṃśastena vidaṣṭasya suptaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ kṣaratyasṛk।
hṛcchirorugjvarastambhatṛṣṇāmūrchodbhavo'nu ca॥
au46.13
anenānyepi boddhavyā vyālā daṃṣṭrāprahāriṇaḥ।
sṛgālāśvatarāśvarkṣadvīpivyāghravṛkādayaḥ॥
au46.14
kaṇḍūnistodavaivarṇyasuptikledajvarabhramāḥ।
vidāharāgarukpākaśophagranthi vikuñcanam॥
au46.15
daṃśāvadaraṇaṃ sphoṭāḥ karṇikā maṇḍalāni ca।
sarvatra saviṣe liṅgaṃ viparītaṃ tu nirviṣe॥
au46.16
daṣṭo yena tu tacceṣṭārutaṃ kurvan vinaśyati।
paśyaṃstameva cākasmādādarśasalilādiṣu॥
au46.17
jaladarśanasaṃsparśaśabdebhyo yaśca santraset।
adaṣṭamapi taṃ jahyājjalasantrāsarogiṇam॥
au46.18
ākhunā daṣṭamātrasya daṃśaṃ kāṇḍena dāhayet।
darpaṇenāthavā tīvrarujā syāt karṇikānyathā॥
au46.19
dagdhaṃ visrāvayeddaṃśaṃ pracchitaṃ ca pralepayet।
śirīṣarajanīvakrakuṅkumāmṛtavallibhiḥ॥
au46.20
agāradhūmamañjiṣṭhā rajanī lavaṇottamaiḥ।
lepo jayatyākhuviṣaṃ karṇikāyāśca pātanaḥ॥
au46.21
tatomlaiḥ kṣālayitvā tu toyairanu ca lepayet।
pālindī śvetakaṭabhī bilvamūlaguḍūcibhiḥ।
anyaiśca viṣaśophaghnaiḥ sirāṃ vā mokṣayet drutam॥
au46.22
chardanaṃ jālinīkāthaiḥ śukākhyāṅkolayorapi।
kośavatyāḥ śukākhyāyāḥ phalaṃ jīmūtakasya ca।
madanasya ca sañcūrṇya dadhnā pītvā viṣaṃ vamet॥
au46.23
vacāmadanajīmūtakuṣṭhaṃ vā mūtrapeṣitam।
pūrvakalpena pātavyaṃ sarvonduruviṣāpaham॥
au46.24
niṣpāvāḥ kadalīmūlaṃ bandhujīvaphalāni ca।
suvarcalārāmaṭhakaṃ svarjikātiviṣādvayam। śyāmādrikarṇikāmūlamūrdhacaiṃvamanatrayam॥
au46.25
vāntasya śuddhe hṛdaye śūlaṃ hidhmārucirvamiḥ।
uṣṇodgārānubandho vā syāccettatraitadauṣadham॥
au46.26
jīrakaṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ tuṅgākhyaṃ nāgakesaram।
rajanyau saindhavaṃ sevyaṃ yaṣṭīmadhusuvarcalām॥
au46.27
madhuraṃ ca gaṇaṃ piṣṭvā bījapūrakapitthayoḥ।
rasena ṣāḍavaṃ kuryānmadhumatsyaṇḍikānvitam।
gandhavarṇarasopetaḥ sa pīto viṣadoṣajit॥
au46.28
dvipippalīdvyaṃśumatīkvāthe peyā ca tadguṇā॥
au46.29
virecane trivṛnnīlītriphalākalka iṣyate।
śirovirecane sāraḥ śirīṣasya phalāni ca॥
au46.30
añjane gomayaraso vyoṣasūkṣmarajonvitaḥ।
kapitthagomayaraso madhumānavalehane॥
au46.31
taṇḍulīyakamūlena siddhaṃ pāne hitaṃ ghṛtam।
dviniśā kaṭabhī raktā yaṣṭyāhvairvāmṛtānvitaiḥ।
āsphotamūlasiddhaṃ vā pañcakāpitthameva vā॥
au46.32
adhobhāge viśuddhasya śūlaṃ nābhyāṃ bhavedyadi।
purīṣaṃ vā vibadhyeta gude syādvā vikartikā॥
au46.33
tatra peyāṃ pibecchītāṃ śarkarāmadhusaṃyutām।
pippalī pippalīmūlasārivā kaṭukāhvayaiḥ।
śṛtaiḥ siddhāṃ saha balāsamaṅgāviśvabheṣajaiḥ॥
au46.34
naladadhyāmakavyoṣalodhracitrakadīpyakam।
kutalakṣāratoyena piṣṭaṃ mākṣikasarpiṣā॥
au46.35
dadhnā vā prāśayet kṣaudraṃ yavakṣārapayodadhi।
phaṇitaṃ tailamājyaṃ ca viṣaghnaṃ pītamekataḥ॥
au46.36
sinduvāraṃ nataṃ śigru bilvamūlaṃ punarnavam।
vacā śvadaṃṣṭrā jīmūtameṣāṃ kvāthaṃ samākṣikam।
pibecchālyodanaṃ dadhnā bhuñjāno mūṣikārditaḥ॥
au46.37
takreṇa śarapuṅkhāyā bījaṃ sañcūrṇya vā pibet।
aṅkolamūlavalko vā bastamūtreṇa kalkitaḥ।
pānalepanayoryuktaḥ sarvonduruviṣāpahaḥ॥
au46.38
payaḥ payasyayā yuktaṃ sitayā madhukena ca॥
au46.39
kirātatiktamamṛtāṃ samaṅgāṃ kakubhatvacam।
bāṇaṃ palāśaṃ kāśmaryaṃ payasyāṃ taṇḍulīyakam॥
au46.40
ākhuvinnāṃ mahānimbaṃ saptaparṇaṃ madhūlikām।
kapitthaṃ rājavṛkṣaṃ vā pibedanyatamaṃ jvarī॥
au46.41
sthirāṃ mandarujāṃ pracchet karṇikāṃ pātayeta vā।
śyāmā lāṅgalikā dantī kiṇihī girikarṇikā॥
au46.42
ākhuvṛkṣo mahāvṛkṣastrivṛdañjanakī snuhī।
karṇikāpātanaṃ kalkamekaikaṃ tilakalkavat॥
au46.43
kṣīripravālamañjiṣṭhābalādārvīhayāhvayāḥ।
ropaṇyaḥ kalkitāstailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā sādhitaṃ tathā।
dviniśā tilayaṣṭyāhvatagarośīrapadmakaiḥ॥
au46.44
sāmānyeneti nirdiṣṭā kriyākhūnāṃ viśeṣataḥ॥
au46.45
lālanena vamirmūrcchā lālāsrāvaśca jāyate।
lihyāt samākṣikaṃ tatra cūrṇitaṃ taṇḍulīyakam॥
au46.46
capalena vamirmūrcchā tṛḍvā tatrāvalehayet।
sadārumustāṃ triphalāṃ putrakeṇa tu pāṇḍutā॥
au46.47
sādoṅge sarvataścākhusadṛśagranthisambhavaḥ।
śirīṣabījaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ ca madhunā tatra lehayet॥
au46.48
hasireṇānnavidveṣo jṛmbhaṇaṃ romaharṣaṇam।
āragvadhadiniryūhaṃ suvāntaṃ tatra pāyayet॥
au46.49
cikireṇa śiroduḥkhaṃ śopho hidhmā vamirbhramaḥ।
vāntotra jālinīkvāthaiḥ sāramaṅkolajaṃ pibet॥
au46.50
ajinenāṅgakṛṣṇatvaṃ mūrcchā chardiśca hṛdgrahaḥ।
madhunā tatra mañjiṣṭhāṃ lihyāt snukkṣīrakalkitām॥
au46.51
nidrā kaṣāyadantena hṛcchoṣaḥ kṛśatāti ca।
śirīṣasāratvagbījaṃ tatra kṣaudreṇa lehayet॥
au46.52
kulakena rujāsrāvau rājayo daṃśamaṇḍale।
sa sinduvārakau tatra sahau lihyānmadhuplutau॥
au46.53
granthayaḥ kokilenogrā jvaro dāhaśca dāruṇaḥ।
nīlīpunarnavākvāthe siddhaṃ tatra pibet ghṛtam॥
au46.54
kapilena vraṇe kotho jvaro granthirbhramaḥ satṛṭ।
lehayenmadhunā śvetāṃ śvetāṃ cātra punarnavām॥
au46.55
raktaṃ kṛṣṇena vamati viśeṣād durdine pibet।
tatra kiṃśukabhasmāmbu śirīṣaphalavālakam॥
au46.56
aruṇādyāḥ pṛthagdoṣasannipātāsrasambhavān।
janayanti kramādrogān sarve ca granthikarṇikāḥ॥
au46.57
karañjāragvadhavyoṣabṛhatyaṃśumatīdvayāt।
kvāthe dadhipayaḥ sarpiḥ pṛthakprasthonmitaṃ pacet॥
au46.58
kapitthadāḍimavarī viśālātrisugandhikāḥ।
trivṛtāmṛttikā vakraguḍūcīścātrakalkitāḥ॥
au46.59
kṣipettadaruṇādīnāṃ pañcānāṃ viṣanāśanam।
kākādanī kākamācī svarasena śṛtaṃ ghṛtam॥
au46.60
klamaścucchundareṇogro grīvāstambho viṣūcikā।
yavanālarṣabhakṣāraṃ bṛhatyau vātra pāyayet॥
au46.61
grīvāstambho rasālena vedanā daṃśamaṇḍale।
lihyānmahāgadaṃ tatra ghṛtamākṣikasaṃyutam॥
au46.62
saśeṣaṃ mūṣikaviṣaṃ prakupyatyabhradarśane।
yathāyathaṃ vā lākeṣu doṣāṇāṃ vṛddhihetuṣu॥
au46.63
tatra sarve yathāvasthaṃ prayojyāḥ syurupakramāḥ।
yathāsvaṃ ye ca nirdiṣṭāstathā dūṣīviṣāpahāḥ॥
au46.64
daṃśatvalarkadaṣṭasya dagdhamuṣṇena sarpiṣā।
pradihyādagadaistaistaiḥ purāṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ pibet।
vraṇasyopari niṣpīḍyaḥ pratyakpuṣpīrasothavā॥
au46.65
tilagugguludūrvāṇāṃ dāḍimasya guḍasya ca।
kalko muhurmuhurlepaḥ śvadaṃśaviṣajitparam॥
au46.66
nalamūlaṃ jale piṣṭaṃ pānalepanayorhitam।
mātuluṅgacchadairdaṃśaṃ badhnīyāddantacarvitaiḥ॥
au46.67
arkakṣīrayutaṃ cāsya yojyamāśu virecanam॥
au46.68
pibet punarnavāṃ śvetāṃ dhurdhūrakaphalānvitām॥
au46.69
phalaṃ dhurdhūrakānmūlaṃ kākodumbarikodbhavam।
śīdhunā śvaviṣaṃ hanti pītaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbunā॥
au46.70
aikadhyaṃ palalaṃ tailaṃ rūpikāyāḥ payo guḍaḥ।
bhinatti viṣamālarkaṃ ghanavṛndamivānilaḥ॥
au46.71
laśunoṣaṇavaidehī varā gopittakalkitāḥ।
pānanasyāñjanālepaiḥ śvadaṣṭasyauṣadhaṃ param॥
au46.72
jalavetasapatratvaṅmūlaṃ kṣuṇṇaṃ pacejjale।
sa kvāthaḥ śītalaḥ pītaḥ paraṃ śvaviṣabheṣajam॥
au46.73
tatsiddhaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ pānanasyābhyañjanalepanam।
jalatrāse samaste ca viṣe tat garuḍopamam॥
au46.74
yavamāṣakulatthānāṃ pañcamūlasya cāmbhasi।
kṣīradviguṇite sarpiḥ sādhayecchlakṣṇakalkitaiḥ॥
au46.75
aśvagandhāsahākuṣṭhabṛhatīrajanīdvayaiḥ।
vidārīnatakaṭvaṅga payasyāsinduvārakaiḥ॥
au46.76
sarpagandhānakhābhīruśarkarāraktacandanaiḥ।
śvasaṃṣṭropadravān sarvān pānābhyaṅgairnihantitat॥
asa46.77। hṛdvidāhe praseke ca virekavamane bhṛśam।
viṣadoṣahare yojye śuddhe saṃsarjanakramaḥ॥
au46.78
dadyāt saṃśodhanaṃ tīkṣṇamavaśyaṃ viṣanāśanam।
aśuddhasya nirūḍhepi vraṇe kupyati tadviṣam॥
au46.79
saratrabījauṣadhibhiḥ kumbhaiḥ śītāmbupūritaiḥ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vārān siddhamantrābhimantritai॥
au46.80
aṣṭottaraśatonmānaiḥ puṣpamālāvaguṇṭhitaiḥ।
gocarmamātrake lipte jvalitāgnau kuśāstṛte।
sthaṇḍile saritastīre snānaṃ vāsya catuṣpathe॥
au46.81
alarkādhipate yakṣa sārameyagaṇādhipa।
alarkajuṣṭametaṃ me nirviṣaṃ kuru mā cirāt।
svāhetimantrolarkārtte sarvakarmasu śasyate॥
au46.82
catuṣpādbhidvipādbhirvā nakhadantaparikṣatam।
śūyate pacyate rāgajvarasrāvarujānvitam॥
au46.83
somavalkośvakarṇaśca gojihvā haṃsapādikā।
rajanyau gairikaṃ lepo nakhadantaviṣāpahaḥ॥
॥iti ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ॥
atha saptacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
au47.1
athāto viṣopadravapratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ॥
au47.2
jvarakāsavamiśvāsahidhmā tṛṣṇātimūrcchanam।
viśobhedo'tikāṭhinyamānāho bastimūrddharuk॥
au47.3
śvayathuḥ pūtidaṃśatvaṃ raktasrāvo viṣānilaḥ।
iti ṣoḍaśa nirdiṣṭā viṣārtānāmupadravāḥ।
gacchantyupokṣitā nāśaṃ yairjuṣṭā viṣarogiṇaḥ॥
au47.4
rājavṛkṣaphalośīrakāśmaryaghanapadmakāt।
kvāthaḥ saśarkarākṣaudro viṣajvaraharaḥ param॥
au47.5
pītā taṇḍulatoyena kaṭukā sasitopalā।
viṣajvaraharājājī jīvakarṣabhakotpalam॥
au47.6
kolamajjasitādhānyabhārṅgīyaṣṭyāhvakesaram।
viṣajvaravamiśvāsakāsatṛṣṇānibarhaṇam॥
au47.7
triphalāragvadhavyāghrīkvātho jvaravibandhajit।
bālabilvavacāmustā kaṣāyaḥ sapunarnavaḥ।
jvarāgnisādaśvayathūnnihanti viṣasambhavān॥
au47.8
vaidehikārāmaṭhakaṃ kapittharasasaindhavam।
sasitāmākṣikaṃ līḍhaṃ śvāsakāsajvarāpaham॥
au47.9
sadrākṣānāgarāṃ kṛṣṇāmathavā savarāghanām।
līḍhvājyamadhunā kāsānmucyate viṣasambhavāt॥
au47.10
sapāṭhāñjanamañjiṣṭhādviniśāmadhukāṃ tathā।
yaṣṭyāhvamambhasā pītvā maricairavacūrṇitam॥
au47.11
viṣavamyāṃ pibet kvāthaṃ vilbamūlādrajo'thavā।
dhātrīṣarūpakadrākṣā madhukaṃ payasā drutam॥
au47.12
vellāgryāñjanasośīrayaṣṭyailākaṇakesaram।
lihyānmaricakumbhīṃ vā ghṛtapuṣparasadrutām॥
au47.13
kṣīrivṛkṣāṅkurakṣaudrasitāstṛḍvamathucchidaḥ॥
au47.14
jīrṇaśālyodanaṃ kṣaudraṃ kṣīraṃ candanasādhitam।
śītānbhonupibet bhuktvā viṣacchardimapohati॥
au47.15
tailagoviḍrasakṣaudrailihyāt kṛṣṇāpriyaṅguke॥
au47.16
śvāsī kṣaudreṇa vā drākṣāśṛṅgīmāgadhikāsitāḥ।
guḍanāgaravaidehīvijayāmalakāni vā॥
au47.17
hidhmāyāṃ śaṅkhakanakakaṭukāsvarṇagairikam।
vellaśuṇṭhīkaṇośīrarajanīdvitayāni vā॥
au47.18
lihyādvā vyoṣamṛdvīkāṃ bījapūrarasena vā।
sakṣaudraṃ vālakarajaḥ kvāthaṃ vā saguḍaṃ pibet॥
au47.19
viśvabheṣajagāyatrīharidrāmaradārujam।
dantīndravāruṇīdvīpīkalkaṃ sauvīrakeṇa vā॥
au47.20
tṛṇmūrcchayoraśiraso lepasekā himā hitāḥ।
ambhojanālakusumacandanośarīmauktikaiḥ।
vaihāyasasitātoyakṣīrājyekṣurasāplutaiḥ॥
au47.21
vījanaṃ tālavṛntena śīte sikatile sthitiḥ॥
au47.22
kamalotpalakiñjalkapaṭalāvṛtavāriṣu।
viṣatṛḍdāhamūrcchāghnaṃ sarasīṣvavagāhanam॥
au47.23
viṣavegasamutthāyāṃ tṛṣṇāyāṃ lājatarpaṇam।
śarkarādāḍimakṣaudrasalilāplāvitaṃ pibet।
vaṭavetasajambvāmrasevyatoyaṃ ca śītalam॥
au47.24
bhūnimbamustakaṭukātrāyantīndrayavān samān।
dvau bhāgau citrakādaṣṭau kuṭajādvāriṇā pibet।
viṣātisārodāvartakāsaśvāsajvarāpaham॥
au47.25
lodhramocarasāmbaṣṭhādhātakīstaṇḍulāmbunā।
samākṣikāḥ pibettadvannāgarātiviṣābhayāḥ॥
au47.26
sadhātakīḥ sakuṭajāḥ sāñjanāḥ ślakṣṇacūrṇitāḥ।
pāṭhānāgaracūrṇaṃ vā dadhnā yuktaṃ samākṣikam॥
au47.27
bastirugvartanāheṣu phalavartiṃ prayojayet।
sāragvadhāṃ satrivṛtāṃ sopakulyāṃ harītakīm।
pibet ghṛtena sakṣaudrāṃ bastiśūlādināśinīm॥
au47.28
gṛhadhūmanataśyāmā nīlinī taṇḍulīyakaiḥ।
siddhaṃ vājyaṃ tathāsiddhaṃ varā kvāthatrivṛdyutam॥
au47.29
kākolī kṣīrivṛkṣatvagdrākṣāyaṣṭyāhvaśarkarāḥ।
nasyaṃ viṣaśirorughnaṃ saṃyojyaṃ śītavāriṇā॥
au47.30
śvayathau śuddhakoṣṭhasya payaḥ pāne hitaṃ śṛtam।
viśvabheṣajavaidehīkaṭukādevadārubhiḥ।
surasāmlakalkairvā chāgaṃ vā pippalīśṛtam॥
au47.31
triphalāyāḥ kaṣāyeṇa trivṛtā bhāvitā tryaham।
āloḍya sarpiṣā pītā viṣaśvayathunāśinī॥
au47.32
madhuvellavarāvyoṣasurāhvośīrapadmakaiḥ।
viṣaśvayathujillepastathā svādukaṣāyakaiḥ॥
au47.33
śirīṣapuṣpāhiśironatakuṣṭhairghṛtānvitaḥ।
dhūpo'gadaḥ śvayathujit samastaviṣanāśanaḥ॥
au47.34
alpenāpyapacāreṇa daṃśaḥ pūtitvamaśnute।
prāyo na sahate tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ vā bheṣajaṃ viṣam॥
au47.35
madhurasnigdhaśītāni yuñyāttasmādviṣavraṇe।
sekālepāṃśca sakṣīraiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ kṣīrivṛkṣajaiḥ॥
au47.36
nyagrodhaśuṅgamadhukatilasarṣapasaindhavam।
sābhayā nimbapatrājyaṃ daṃśapūtitvanāśanam।
karṇikāpātanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ viṣavraṇavināśanam॥
au47.37
rakte sravatyatibhṛśaṃ ghṛtaṃ samaricaṃ pibet।
taṇḍulīyakamūlena sitayā vā samanvitam॥
au47.38
daṃśaṃ pralepayeccāsya dārvyā suślakṣṇapiṣṭayā।
sitopalākṣaudraghṛtacchāgadugdhāni nāvanam॥
au47.39
śamīkalkaṃ pibecchlakṣṇamaṅgaṃ limpodviśālayā।
nāvane hemaṃ śuklā ca tataḥ śāmyati śoṇitam॥
au47.40
kdśasyātisrute rakte rūkṣairatyarthasevitaiḥ।
viṣasya ca svabhāvena mātariśvā prakupyati॥
au47.41
unmādākṣepakamanobhraṃśāpasmṛtayastataḥ।
tatreṣṭaṃ snehanaṃ bastinasyapradhamānāñjanam॥
au47.42
nāgadantyabhayākuṣṭhapippalīvṛṣakaṭphalam।
bhallātakāsthikaṭukābilvaprativiṣāgnikāḥ।
sakṣīraṃ tairghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ viṣavātavikārajit॥
au47.43
pibederaṇḍatailaṃ vā chāgamāṃsarasānvitam।
aikadhyaṃ ghṛtatailaṃ vā medhyamāṃsarasāśanaḥ॥
au47.44
kārpāsamūlaṃ maricaṃ haridre naladaṃ nalam।
pippalīṃ svarjikāṃ kuṣṭhaṃ jalenāloḍya pāyayet।
unmattaṃ viṣavātena tathāpasmāriṇaṃ naram॥
au47.45
vacāhaṃsapadīvyoṣadadhitthaṃ hastipippalīm।
devadārubalābilvakṛmijit kuṣṭhaṭuṇṭukam॥
au47.46
lodhrākhukarṇyativiṣāḥ kṣīraṃ sarpiśca pāyayet।
nihanti pānābhyaṅgābhyāṃ ghṛtaṃ sarvaviṣāṇi tat॥
au47.47
pratikuryādyathāsvaṃ ca rogeṣvevaṃ pareṣu ca।
doṣānubandhamālocya viṣatantrāvirodhataḥ॥
au47.48
dṛśyaśabdāgadairasya viṣaśeṣaṃ nivartayet।
alpamapyavaśiṣṭaṃ hi vyādhaye maraṇāya vā॥
au47.49
dhavāśvakarṇatiniśakaraghāṭakapītanān।
palāśāmrātakakubhapāribhadrakatilvakān॥
au47.50
kapitthakuṭajāṅkolapragrahāmalakībhujān।
śamīśleṣmātakāśmantagojīyamalakaṇṭakān॥
au47.51
cirivilvārkakaṭvaṅgasamaṅgāmadhuśigrukān।
gopaghoṇṭāhimārau ca bhasmīkṛtyāmbhasā gavām॥
au47.52
kṣārakalpenavisrāvya pacet kṣiptvāvacūrṇitān।
pippalīdvayakośāsrasaptaparṇailavālukān॥
au47.53
varāṅgacocamañjiṣṭhākuṣṭhavañjulaṭuṇṭukān।
viḍaṅgātiviṣānantāsarṣapataṇḍulīyakān॥
au47.54
surāhvasaralaplakṣagṛhadhūmakarañjakān।
nāgadantī sutaśreṇī niculaṃ varuṇaṃ vacām॥
au47.55
varddhamānamayo bilvaṃ kṣāravatpākamāgatam।
tat lohakumbhe nihitaṃ kāryaṃ sannihitaṃ sadā॥
au47.56
tena dundubhimālimbet patākāstaraṇāni ca।
darśanaśravaṇasparśairnirviṣaṃ tāni kurvate॥
au47.57
pānāt kṣārāgadaścaiṣa viṣaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam।
śūlagulmodarājarṇiśvāsakāsāśmaśarkarāḥ॥
au47.58
śophārśograhaṇīdoṣānaruciṃ ca niyacchati।
api takṣakatulyānāṃ sarpāṇāṃ darpanāśanaḥ॥
au47.59
śrīveṣṭakamanohvālaṃ sasarjarasavālakam।
karṣāṃśaṃ nāgapuṣpasya prakuñcaṃ truṭiviṃśakam॥
au47.60
hareṇavaścatuḥṣaṣṭiḥ kuṭannaṭacatuṣṭayam।
śatāhvāṃ ṣoḍaśaitāni puṣye sambhṛtya peṣayet॥
au47.61
āśleṣāsu gavāṃ madhye śastramantrābhirakṣitam।
kumāryā snātayā tatra mantroyaṃ viṣṇunirmitaḥ॥
au47.62
mātā me vijayānāma jayo nāma pitā mama।
ajayyasya ca putrosau vijaye ca jayāmi vaḥ॥
au47.63
sugandhākhyoyamagado nityaṃ dehavilepanāt।
abhaṅgakaraṇo yuddhe vivāde ca jayāvahaḥ॥
au47.64
amunā lepitāśchatradundubhidhvajatoraṇāḥ।
dṛṣṭaspṛṣṭaśrutā ghnanti viṣaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam।
bhūtabālagrahonmādān gehasthopi nivārayet॥
au47.65
prapauṇḍarīkasaraladevadārukuṭannaṭam।
jaṭāśatāhvātiviṣātilaparṇīsugandhikā॥
au47.66
nīlīyivaphalābhārṅgīmadhuyaṣṭyailavālukam।
toyatoyadakālīyatagaradhyāmakatvacaḥ॥
au47.67
nakhapadmakapunnāgapatrakālānusārivāḥ।
tālīsapatraṃ maricaṃ joṅgakaṃ candanadvayam॥
au47.68
dvyelādvisevyadvitā dviniśā naladadvayam।
lākṣāśītaśivavyoṣaphalinīdhānyagairikam॥
au47.69
śaileyakaśilāpuṣpagranthilā corakābhayāḥ।
arkasthauṇeyapṛthvīkā kaṭukā candrarājayaḥ॥
au47.70
kaliṅgakaḥ sarjarasaḥ kuṣṭhaṃ lavaṇapañcakam।
śrīparṇikāśmarīśeluśiṃśapā sinduvārajaḥ॥
au47.71
campakāśokasurasasumanastilvakodbhavāḥ।
pāṭalyāstṛṇaśūlyāśca prasavāḥ kumudotpalam॥
au47.72
tiniśārjunaśamyākadhavapuṣpaṃ sapaṅkajam।
pañcāśīteridaṃ cūrṇaṃ samūtraghṛtamākṣikam॥
au47.73
nidhāpayet gavāṃ śṛṅge manuṣyaṃ punarāharet।(manuṣyaṃ tena jīvayet) bhagnaskandhaṃ vivṛttākṣaṃ mṛtyordaṃṣṭrāntaraṃ gatam॥
au47.74
mahāsugandho nāmnāyamativīryotitejasā।
vārayatyatidurvāraṃ viṣāgniṃ vāsukerapi॥
au47.75
nṛponenānuliptāṅgo bhavet sarvajanapriyaḥ।
tejasvitāṃ ca labhate rājakasyāpi madhyagaḥ॥
au47.76
śītameva ca kurvīta vidhānaṃ viṣarogiṇām।
muktvā kīṭaviṣaṃ taddhi śītenātiprabarddhate॥
au47.77
śālayaḥ ṣaṣṭikā jīrṇāḥ koradūṣāḥ priyaṅgavaḥ।
mudgo hareṇustuvarī paṭolaṃ vetrapallavāḥ॥
au47.78
taṇḍulīyakajīvantī vārtākaṃ suniṣaṇṇakaḥ।
jāṅgalaṃ dāḍimaṃ dhātrī kapitthaṃ saindhavaṃ sitā॥
au47.79
avidāhiyadanyacca vijñāyānnasvarūpataḥ।
tattaddadyādviṣārtebhyaḥ kāryā vyañjanasaṃskṛtiḥ।
kaṣāyairviṣahantṝṇāṃ ghṛnaiḥ kalyāṇakādibhiḥ॥
au47.80
divyasārasakūpotthamanyadvā śṛtaśītalam।
madhvāmalakayuktaṃ vā viṣārttaḥ salilaṃ pibet।
nadītaṭākajaṃ tyājyaṃ viśeṣeṇa ghanāgame॥
au47.81
śuklavastrodarāyātaiḥ sukṛtāḥ saktavo yavaiḥ।
takreṇa saghṛtāḥ pītāḥ paramaṃ viṣanāśanāḥ॥
au47.82
tilamadyakulatthakṣutkrudbhayāyāsamaithunam।
varjayedviṣamuktopi divāsvapnaṃ viśeṣataḥ॥
au47.83
praśāntadoṣaṃ prakṛtisthadhātu māhārakāmaṃ samamūtraviṭkam।
prasannavarṇendriyacittaceṣṭaṃ vaidyovagacchedaviṣaṃ manuṣyam॥
॥iti saptacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ॥
atha aṣṭacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
au48.1
athāto viṣopayogīyaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ।
viṣe prativiṣaṃ yojyaṃ mantratantrairasidhyati।
atīte pañcame vege saptamasyānatikrame।
prabhonirvadye prayato naiva vākhyāya kasyacit॥
au48.2
siddhamantradharaḥ kṛtvā dharaṇībandhamāditaḥ।
nahi mantrasahāyasya viṣaṃ yātyavidheyatām॥
au48.3
śleṣmatulyaguṇaṃ prāyaḥ sthiramūrdhvagamaṃ viṣam।
prāyaḥ pittaguṇairyuktamadhogāmi ca jaṅgamam॥
au48.4
guṇairiti viparyastairnihataste parasparam।
yuñjyānmūlaviṣaṃ tasmāddaṣṭānāṃ pānalepayoḥ॥
au48.5
viṣapītaṃ ca kuśalo daṃśayet pavanāśibhiḥ।
na viṣapratimaṃ kiñcinnirviṣīkaraṇaṃ viṣe॥
au48.6
caturbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiraṣṭābhirhīnamadhyottamāṃ yavaiḥ।
mātrāṃ viṣasya maulasya prayuñjīta yathāyatham॥
au48.7
daṣṭasya dvau yavau kīṭaistilamātraṃ tu vṛścikaiḥ।
naiva svasṛksthe pāne tu lūtādaṣṭasya neṣyate॥
au48.8
saviṣe yuktamamṛtaṃ viṣamevāviṣe viṣam।
abale cātibalavadvyāpannaṃ ca prayogataḥ॥
au48.9
saviṣāviṣaśaṅkāyāmagadānupayojayet।
aviruddhān prayukto hi nirviṣasyāgado gadaḥ॥
au48.10
tadvacca saviṣatyāpi kriyākālātipātataḥ।
jānīyādviṣasadbhāvaṃ bhiṣaktasmāt prayatnataḥ॥
au48.11
sāktukaṃ mustakaṃ śṛṅgī vālakaṃ sarṣapāhvayam।
vatssnābhaṃ ca karmaṇyaṃ viṣaṃ snigdhaṃ ghanaṃ guru। najātvanyat prayoktavyaṃ kālakūṭaṃ viśeṣataḥ॥
au48.12
viṣe'vacārite tīkṣṇe peyaṃ ghṛtamanantaram।
sabhārṅgīdadhidhūmotthasārivātaṇḍulīyakam॥
au48.13
agāradhūmamañjiṣṭhāyaṣṭyāhvairvā samanvitam।
lihyādvā madhusarpirbhyāṃ cūrṇitāmarjunatvacam॥
au48.14
kṣīrakṣaudraghṛtairyuktaṃ pītaṃ hanti viṣaṃ viṣam।
au48.15
sasinduvāratagaraṃ mṛtasañjīvanaṃ viṣam॥
au48.16
śirīṣakusumaṃ vakraṃ viṣamākhuviṣāpaham॥
devadārunataṃmāṃsī drāmilībākucīviṣam।
kuṣṭhaṃ ca pānalepābhyāṃ samastaviṣaśāśanam॥
au48.17
manaśśilājjanālailā sinduvārāmarāhvayam।
saraktākuṃkumaviṣaṃ dhmānaṃ nissaṃjñabodhanam॥
au48.18
dāhe viṣodbhave lepaḥ saktukṣīraghṛtairhitaḥ॥
au48.19
yastu saṃroṣito bhogī dhūmaṃ vaktrādvimuñjcati।
daṇḍāgre piśitaṃ badhvā bahuśastena daṃśayet॥
au48.20
aśakyamagadairanyairviṣapītaṃ cikitsakaḥ।
pāyayenmāṃsacūrṇaṃ taṃ jñātvā viṣabalābalam॥
au48.21
anyeṣvapi ca rogeṣu śeṣopāyaparikṣaye।
viṣaṃ yuñjīta nityaṃ ca rasāyanagaveṣiṇaḥ॥
au48.22
ghṛtopaskṛtadehasya viśuddhasya hitāśinaḥ।
sātvikasyodite bhānau yojyaṃ śītavasantayoḥ॥
au48.23
grīṣmepyātyayike vyādhau na ca varṣāsu durdine॥
au48.24
na krodhane na pittārte na klībe rājani dvije।
kṣuttṛṣṇāśramagharmādhvavyādhyantaranipīḍite।
garbhiṇībālavṛddheṣu na rūkṣeṣu na marmasu॥
au48.25
abhyastepi viṣe yatnādvarjanīyān vivarjayet।
kaṭvamlatailalavaṇadivāsvapnātapānalān।
rūkṣamannaṃ viśeṣeṇa bhayaṃ vājīrṇataḥ sadā॥
au48.26
dṛgvibhramaṃ karṇarujāmanyāṃścānilajān gadān।
viṣaṃ rūkṣāśinaḥ kuryānmṛtyumeva tvajīrṇataḥ॥
au48.27
alaṃ gomūtrasaṃyuktamātape śoṣayet tryaham।
viṣaṃ bṛṃhaṇametaddhi viṣasyādau praśasyate॥
au48.28
tat pibenmastunā vātajvare kṣīreṇa paittike।
yuktaṃ mūtreṇa kaphaje sarvaje triphalāmbhasā॥
au48.29
lodhracandanaṣaḍgranthāśarkarāghṛtamākṣikaiḥ।
kṣīreṇa ca viṣaṃ yuktaṃ jīrṇajvaraharaṃ param॥
au48.30
nikumbhakumbhatriphalāsarpirmadhuviṣaiḥkṛtaḥ।
nihanti modako jīrṇajvaramehatvagāmayān।
śikhikarkirasopetaṃ viṣamajvarajidviṣam॥
au48.31
viṣaṃ yaṣṭyāhvayaṃ rāsnāsevyamutpalakandakam।
taṇḍulodakapītāni raktapittasya bheṣajam॥
au48.32
viṣaṃ rasāñjanaṃ bhārṅgī vṛścikālī mahāsahā।
savedane sapāke ca vraṇe duṣṭe pralepanam॥
au48.33
sitāviṣakṣīratarupravālā madhunā drutāḥ।
śvāsahidhmāpahā līḍhāśchardidhnyastu viṣānvitāḥ।
kṣaudrośīramadhukṣārarajanīkuṭajatvacaḥ॥
au48.34
vijayāpippalīmūlapippalīdvayacitrakaiḥ।
puṣkarāhvaśaṭhīdrākṣāyavānīkṣāradīpyakaiḥ॥
au48.35
sitāyaṣṭīdvibṛhatīsaindhavaiḥ pālikaiḥ pacet।
saviṣārddhapalaiḥ prasthaṃ ghṛtāttajjīrṇabhukpibet॥
au48.36
durnāmamehagulmārmatimirakrimipāṇḍutāḥ।
galagrahagrahonmādakuṣṭhāni ca niyacchati॥
au48.37
kṛcchraghnā viṣapathyāgnidantīdrākṣāniśāviṣāḥ।
śilājatu viṣaṃ mūtramudāvartāśmarīharam॥
au48.38
gomūtrakṣārasindhūtthaṃ viṣaṃ pāṣāṇabhedakam।
vajravaddārayatyetadekataḥ pītamaśmarīm॥
au48.39
samūlā pippalī mūtraṃ viṣaṃ śūlaharaṃ tathā।
viṣadravantīmadhukadrākṣārāsnāśaṭhī kaṇāḥ॥
au48.40
eraṇḍatailaṃ triphalā gomūtraṃ citrako viṣam।
sarpiṣā sahitaṃ pītaṃ vātāṇḍatvamapohati॥
au48.41
triphalā svarjikākṣāro viṣaṃ gulmaprabhedanam।
viṣavellamisikṣīraṃ gulmaplīhanibarhaṇam॥
au48.42
plīhodaraghnaṃ payasā śatāhvā krimijidviṣam॥
au48.43
vāyasīmūlaniṣkkāthapītaṃ kuṣṭhaharaṃ viṣam॥
au48.44
vāyasyārājavṛkṣatvaktrāyantībākucīphalāt।
plīhaghnebhakaṇābhyāṃ ca viṣaṃ kvāthena kuṣṭhajit॥
au48.45
avalgujaiḍagajayorbījaṃ kṣāradvayaṃ viṣam।
lepaḥ sasaindhavaḥ piṣṭo vāriṇā kuṣṭhanāśanaḥ॥
au48.46
citrakārkajaṭāhastipippalībākucīviṣaiḥ।
gomūtrapiṣṭairanyonyomanohvāsnukpayoviṣaiḥ॥
au48.47
sacandralekhaiḍagajakarañjaphalasaindhavaiḥ।
savyoṣasvarjikākṣārayavakṣāraniśādvayaiḥ।
agāradhūmasahitairbastamūtreṇa kalkitaiḥ।
bhallātakāgniśamyākaviṣairgomūtrapeṣitaiḥ।
lepo vicarcikādaduśatāruḥkiṭibhāpahaḥ।
śamyākapatratvaṅmūlaṃ viṣaṃ takraṃ ca tadguṇam॥
au48.48
viṣabhallātakadvīpiguñjānimbaphalairjayet।
lepomlapiṣṭaiḥ śvitrāṇi puṇḍarīkaṃ ca dāruṇam॥
au48.49
vakrakuṣṭharasadvīpispṛkkāpatrailavālukam।
piṣṭaṃ khadiratoyena trirātramuṣitaṃ pibet॥
au48.50
śvitrī viṣeṇa saṃsṛṣṭaṃ tataḥ sphoṭān kilāsajān।
kaṇṭakena vibhidyānu lepairlimpeta kauṣṭhikaiḥ॥
au48.51
athavā karavīrārkamūlabākucikāviṣaiḥ।
batāmbupiṣṭaiḥ sadvīpidvipapippalyaruṣkaraiḥ॥
au48.52
lākṣāsurāhvāmañjiṣṭhākuṣṭhapadmakasārivāḥ।
guñjāphalaṃ kurabako lāṅgalī vajrakandakaḥ॥
au48.53
vārāhīkandakāsphotā saptāhvagirikarṇikāḥ।
arkāśvamārayormūlaṃ nāgapuṣpaṃ nataṃ niśe॥
au48.54
dantī viṣaṃ sātiviṣaṃ pippalī maricāni ca।
taistailaṃ kaṭutailaṃ vā śvitrasyābhyañjanaṃ pacet।
savarṇīkaraṇaṃ śreṣṭhamāstikasya vaco yathā॥
au48.55
vīrā lāṅgalikī dantī viṣapāṣāṇabhedakaiḥ।
prayojyo mūḍhagarbhāṇāṃ pralepo garbhamocanaḥ॥
au48.56
svarasaṃ bījapūrasya vacāṃ brāhmīrasaṃ ghṛtam।
bandhyā pibantī saviṣaṃ suputraiḥ parivāryate॥
au48.57
naṣṭaśukraḥ payo drākṣākapikacchu vacā viṣam॥
au48.58
viṣaṃ sarpiḥ sitā kṣaudraṃ timirāpahamañjanam।
viṣaṃ caikamajākṣīrakalkitaṃ ghṛtadhūpitam॥
au48.59
viṣaṃ dhātrīphalarasairasakṛt paribhāvitam।
añjanaṃ śaṅkhasahitaṃ pragāḍhatimirapraṇut॥
au48.60
viṣamindrāyudhaṃ stanye ghṛṣṭaṃ kācajidañjanam।
bījapūrarase ghṛṣṭaṃ viṣaṃ tadvatsitāyutam।
viṣaṃ māgadhikā dve ca niśe kācaghramañjanam॥
au48.61
śuklārmajidviṣaṃ kṛṣṇāyuktaṃ gomūtrabhāvitam॥
au48.62
samudraphenasphaṭikakuruvindasudhāñjanam।
kūrmapṛṣṭhaṃ ca tulyāni tebhyorddhāṃśā manaśśilā॥
au48.63
arddhahīnāni maricasaindhavāyorajāṃsi ca।
ato yathottaraṃ dadyādayasā ca samaṃ viṣam।
rasakriyeyaṃ madhunā śuklapillārmakācahṛt॥
au48.64
abhīkṣṇaṃ śītatoyena siñjcennetre viṣāñjite॥
au48.65
rasonakandamaricaviṣasarṣapasaindhavaiḥ।
pillekṣi likhitaṃ pūrvaṃ surasārasapeṣitaiḥ॥
au48.66
pūrayet sarpiṣā cānu sarpireva ca pāyayet।
madhūkasāramadhukaviṣakṣīrajalairghṛtam।
pakvaṃ santarpaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rātryandhatve cirotthite॥
au48.67
nasyaṃ śirorukśamanaṃ pratyakpuṣpī sitā viṣam।
athavā ghṛtayaṣṭyāhvaśarkarā viṣasaṃyutāḥ॥
au48.68
śuṇṭhī pathyā viṣaṃ pāṭhā dravantī pūtināsajit॥
au48.69
kaṭutailaṃ viṣaṃ nasyaṃ palitārūṃṣikāpaham॥
au48.70
svarjikākṣārasindhūtthaśuktayuktaṃ viṣaṃ param।
karṇayoḥ pūraṇaṃ tīvrakarṇaśūlanibarhaṇam॥
au48.71
prapauṇḍarīkamañjiṣṭhāviṣasindhusamudbhavaiḥ।
nihanti sādhitaṃ tailaṃ gaṇḍūṣeṇa mukhāmayān॥
au48.72
devadāru viṣaṃ sarpirgomūtraṃ kaṇṭakārikā।
vācaḥskhalanatāṃ hanti pītamityāha kāśyapaḥ॥
au48.73
śatruprayuktādviṣato garādvā।
lūtābhujaṅgākhugaṇājjarāyāḥ।
akālamṛtyorgrahapāpmato vā।
viṣāśino nāsti bhayaṃ narasya॥
।iti aṣṭacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ।
॥iti viṣatantraṃnāma ṣaṣṭhamaṅgaṃ sampūrṇam॥
atha ekonapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ।
au49.1
athāto rasāyanavidhiṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ।
dīrghamāyuḥ smṛtiṃ medhāmārogyaṃa taruṇaṃ vayaḥ।
prabhā varṇasvaraudāryaṃ dehendriyabalodayam॥
au49.2
vāksiddhiṃ vṛṣatāṃ kāntimavāpnoti rasāyanāt।
lābhopāyo hi śasyānāṃ rasādīnāṃ rasāyanam॥
au49.3
pūrve vayasi madhye vā tatprayojyaṃ jitātmanaḥ।
snigdhasya srutaraktasya viśuddhasya ca sarvathā॥
au49.4
aviśuddhe śarīre hi yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ।
na bhāti malasaṃsṛṣṭe vastre rāga ivārpitaḥ॥
au49.5
yuktaṃ saṃskārahīnasya samyagapyapramādinaḥ।
yathaiva pauruṣaṃ tadvannasidhyati rasāyanam॥
au49.6
sarve ca doṣā bhavanti grāmyādāhārādamlalavaṇakaṭukakṣāravirudvāsātmyarūkṣābhiṣyandiklinnagurupūtipuryuṣitanavadhānyaśuṣkaśākāmamāṃsatilakulatthadadhiśuktakāñjikapiṣṭānnavirūḍhakaniṣeviṇāṃ divāsvapnastrīmadyanityānāṃ viṣamātimātravyāyāmāyāmasaṅkṣobhitavapuṣāṃ krodhalobhabhayaśokāyāsabahulānā pāpakarmaṇāmasamañjasāhāravihāranirhāraniratānām॥
au49.7
ato nimittaṃ hyaviśuddhaḥ sañjāyate raso vidahyate raktaṃ śithilībhavanti māṃsāni viṣyandate medo dūṣyante doṣā vimucyante sandhayo na sandhīyantesthiṣu majjāno nāpyāyate śukraṃ naujo na balaṃ na vīryam॥
au49.8
tataḥ sa evaṃbhūto glāyati sīdati nidrātandrālasyasamanvitaḥ khidyate nirvidyate nirutsāho'samarthaḥ śārīramānasānāṃ viśiṣṭānāṃ ceṣṭānāṃ bhraṣṭacchāyo naṣṭasmṛtiralpabuddhirasampādyamānābhilaṣitārtho'harniśamaniśamaniśaṃ niśvasannadhiṣṭhānabhūto rogāṇāṃ nopāttamapi sarvamāyuravāpnoti॥
au49.9
tasmāt buddhimānapāsya yathoktānāhārādidoṣān nirvāhya ca pūrvopacitān rasāyanaṃ vidhivihitamupaseveta॥
au49.10
tattu dvividhaṃ kuṭīprāveśikaṃ vātātapikaṃ ca।
tatra vīryaprabhāvaprayogaparihāragurutvāt kuṭīprāveśikaṃ mahāphalataram॥
au49.11
tasya vidhiḥ kṣemasubhikṣadhārmikaśaddadhānajananṛpavaidyavipre sulabhamahauṣadhighṛtakṣīrapathyabhojanopakaraṇe grame nagare vā pūrvottarasyāṃdiśi prāgudakpravaṇe suvibhaktavihāroddeśe deśe dṛḍhaghanasumṛṣṭabhittimutsedhavistārasampannāṃ sūkṣmalocanāṃ trigarbhāmṛtusukhāṃ nirvātāṃ pravātaikadeśāṃ prāgdvārāmudagdvārāṃ vā śamīvilvakṣīrivṛkṣaparigṛhītāmaniṣṭendriyārthavātātaparajodhūmasvedakledadaṃśamaśakasarīsṛpavyālabālastrīdāsāntāvasāyināmagamyāṃ sannihitasadvaidyaparicārakopakaraṇāṃ kuṭīṃ kārayet॥
au49.12
tasyāṃ rasāyanārthī śaradi vasante vā śuklapakṣe praśaste ahani pūjayitvā yathārhaṃ devaguruviprān praṇamya brahmadakṣāśviprabhṛtīn parimṛśya suvarṇaghṛtamadhusiddhārthakapriyaṅgurocanāḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya gobrāhmaṇānanu praviśet॥
au49.13
tatra saṃśodhanaiḥ śuddhaḥ sukhī jātabalaḥ punaḥ।
brahmacārī dhṛtiyutaḥ śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ॥
au49.14
dānaśīladayāsatyavratadharmaparāyaṇaḥ।
devatānusmṛtau yukto yuktasvapnaprajāgaraḥ।
priyauṣadhaḥ peśalabāgārabheta rasāyanam॥
au49.15
harītakīmāmalakaṃ saindhavaṃ nāgaraṃ vacām।
haridrāṃ pippalīṃ vellaṃ guḍaṃ coṣṇāmbunā pibet।
snigdhasvinno naraḥ pūrvaṃ tena sādhu viricyate॥
au49.16
tataḥ śuddhaśarīrāya kṛtasaṃsarjanāya ca।
trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā ghṛtānvitam।
dadyādyāvakamāśuddheḥ purāṇaśakṛto'thavā॥
au49.17
itthaṃ saṃskṛtakoṣṭhasya rasāyanamupāharet।
yasya yadyaugikaṃ paśyet sarvamālocya sātmyavit॥
au49.18
haraṇāt sarvarogāṇāṃ yāsāvuktā harītakī।
pathyatvāt sarvadhātūnāṃ pathyā śivatayā śivā॥
au49.19
yasmādvijayate vyādhīn samagrānvijayā tataḥ।
abhayaṃ sarvarogebhyo bhavatyāyuśca śāśvatam।
yataḥ śīlayatāmenāṃ teneyamabhayā smṛtā॥
au49.20
navā vṛttā ghanā snigdhā gurvī majjati cāpsu yā।
bālasya sā prayoktavyā navanītasamanvitā॥
au49.21
vāte sasarpirlavaṇā pitte saguḍaśarkarā।
kaphe sapippalīkṣaudrā sarvadā sā praśasyate॥
au49.22
atha harītakīnāṃ himavacchailasambhavānāṃ kālajātānāmāpūrṇarasavīryāṇāmanāmayānāṃ dviśastriśo vā śakalitānāmanasthnāmāḍhakaṃ caturguṇena payasā saṃsvedya mṛdubhūtamavatārya śītaṃ sarpirmadhvāḍhakābhyāṃ saṃsṛjya suguptaṃ sthāpayet।
tatastrirātrādūrdhvamāhārānuparodhinīṃ mātrāṃ pratyahamupayojayet jīeṇe śāliṣaṣṭikaṃ payasā bhuñjīta।
prayogānte ca tāvantameva kālam।
asya prayogādvarṣaśatamajaro nirvalīkhalatipalitāmayaḥ śrutismṛtisampannaḥ samiddhānalaśca puruṣo bhavati॥
au49.23
bṛhaccharīraṃ girisārasāraṃ svaro ghanaughastanitānukārī।
bhavatyapatyaṃ vipulaṃ sthiraṃ ca samaśnato yogamimaṃ prayatnāt॥
au49.24
pathyāsahastraṃ triguṇadhātrīphalasamanvitam।
pañcānāṃ pañcamūlānāṃ sārddhaṃ palaśatadvayam॥
au49.25
jale daśaguṇe paktvā daśabhāgasthite rase।
āpothya kṛtvā vyasthīni vijayāmalakānyathā॥
au49.26
vinīya tasmin niryūhe yojayet kuḍavāṃśakam।
tvagelāmustarajanīpippalyagarucandanam॥
au49.27
maṇḍūkaparṇīkanakaśaṅkhapuṣpīvacāplavam।
yaṣṭyāhvayaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca cūrṇitaṃ tulayādhikam॥
au49.28
sitopalārddhabhāraṃ ca prātrāṇi trīṇi sarpiṣaḥ।
dve ca tailāt pacet sarvaṃ tadagnau lehatāṃ gatam॥
au49.29
avatīrṇaṃ himaṃ yuñjyādviṃśaiḥ kṣaudraśataistribhiḥ।
tataḥ khajena mathitaṃ nidadhyāt ghṛtabhājane॥
au49.30
etadrasāyanaṃ brāhmaṃ samaṃ pūrveṇa sarvathā।
vaikhānasā bālakhilyāḥ prāśya prāptā navaṃ vayaḥ।
ārogyamamitaṃcāyurvītatandrāśramaklamāḥ॥
au49.31
abhayāmalakavibhītakapañcātmakapañcamūlaniryūhe।
vallīpalāśakarase dviguṇe kṣīreṣṭaguṇe ca vipacet॥
au49.32
ghṛtasyakumbhaṃ madhukaṃ madhūkaṃ kākoliyugmaṃ ca balāṃ svaguptām।
sakṣīraśuklāmṛṣabhaṃ sajīvaṃ sukhāmbupastaccapibet guṇāḍhyam॥
au49.33
āmalakasahastraṃ piṣṭasvedanavidhānena kṣīroṣmaṇā susvinnamanātapaśuṣkamanasthi cūrṇayet।
tadāmalakasahasrasvarasaparipītaṃ sthirājīvantīpunarnavānāgabalāmaṇḍūkaparṇībrahmasuvarcalābhīruśaṅkhapuṣpīvacāpippalīviḍaṅgasvaguptāmṛtāgarucandanamadhukamadhūkapuṣpapadmotpalanavamālikāyuvatiyūthikācūrṇāṣṭabhāgasampṛktaṃ punarnāgabalāpalasahasrasvarasaparipītaṃ chāyopaśoṣitaṃ dviguṇitasarpiṣā kṣaudreṇa kṣudraguḍākṛti kṛtvā ghṛtabhājanasthaṃ bhasmarāśeradhaḥ sthāpayedantarbhūmeḥ pakṣamatharvavedavitkṛtarakṣaṃ pakṣātyaye coddhṛtya kanakarajatatāmrapravālakālāyaścūrṇāṣṭabhāgasaṃyuktamarddhakarṣābhivṛddhyā yathāgni prātaḥ prayojayediti samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.34
āmalakasahasramārdrapalāśadroṇyāṃ sāpidhānāyāṃ bāṣpamanudvamantyāmāraṇyagomayāgnibhirupasvedayet।
tāni susvinnaśītānyuddhṛtya niṣkulīkṛtānyāpothya pippalī viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ pṛthagāḍhakenādhyarddhena śarkarāyāḥ ṣaḍbhirmadhughṛtatailānāṃ saṃyojya ghṛtakumbhe sthāpayedviṃśatirātraṃ paraṃ copayojayediti samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.35
abhayāmalakasahasraṃ pippalīsahasrayuktaṃ taruṇapalāśakṣārodakenāplāvya śucau bhāṇḍe sthāpayet।
tatonugatakṣāramanātapaśuṣkamāsthirahitaṃ cūrṇayitvā sitopalāpādena caturguṇābhyāṃ ca madhughṛtābhyāṃ saṃyojya ghṛtabhājane ṣaṇmāsānantarbhūmeḥ sthāpayitvā parato yathāgnibalamupayuñjīteti samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.36
āmalakacūrṇāḍhakamekaviṃśatirātramāmalakasvarasabhāvitaṃ madhughṛtāḍhakābhyāṃ pippalīcūrṇāṣṭabhāgena śarkarācaturbhāgena ca saṃsṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtabhājanasthaṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśau nidadhyāt।
taccharadi copayojayediti samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.37
viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāmāḍhakamāḍhakaṃ pippalītaṇḍulānāmadhyarddhaṃ sitopalānāṃ madhughṛtatailāḍhakaiḥ ṣaḍbhirekīkṛtaṃ ghṛtabhājanasthaṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśāvitisamānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.38
abhayāmalakabibhītakānāṃ dviśastriśo vā saṃyojitānāṃ palāśatvagavanaddhānāṃ mṛdāvaliptānāṃ kukūlasvinnānāṃ nirasthīkṛtānāṃ palasahastramulūkhale saṅkṣudya dadhibhadhughṛtatailapalalaśarkarāsampṛktaṃ bhakṣayedanannabhugyathoktena vidhinā prayogānte tato dviguṇaṃ kālaṃ yavāgūyūṣakṣīraghṛtaṣaṣṭikānnamāhārobhyañjanaṃ sarpirudvartanaṃ yavacūrṇamiti samānaṃ pūrveṇābhyadhikaphalaṃ vā॥
au49.39
daśamūlabalāmustajīvakarṣabhakotpalam।
parṇinyau pippalī śṛṅgī medā tāmalakī truṭiḥ॥
au49.40
jīvantī joṅgakaṃ drākṣā pauṣkaraṃ candanaṃ śaṭhī।
punarnavadvikākolī kākanāsāmṛtādvayam॥
au49.41
vidārī vṛṣamūlaṃ ca tadaikadhyaṃ palenmitam।
jaladroṇe pacet pañca dhātrīphalaśatāni ca॥
au49.42
pādaśeṣaṃ rasaṃ tasmādvyasthīnyāmalakāni ca।
gṛhītvā bharjayettailaghṛtādvādaśabhiḥpalaiḥ॥
au49.43
matsyaṇḍikātulārdhena yuktaṃ tallehavat pacet।
snehārddhaṃ madhunaḥ śīte tugākṣīryāścatuṣpalam॥
au49.44
pippalyā dve pale dadyācaturjātaṃ kaṇārdhikam।
atovalehayenmātrāṃ kuṭīsthaṃ pathyabhojinam॥
au49.45
ityeṣa cyavanaprāśo yaṃ prāśya cayvano muniḥ।
jarājarjaritopyāsīnnārīnayananandanaḥ॥
au49.46
kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ jvaraṃ śoṣaṃ hṛdrogaṃ vātaśoṇitam।
mūtraśukrāśrayāntoṣān vaisvaryaṃ ca vyapohati।
bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇakṛśānāmaṅgavarddhanaḥ॥
au49.47
medhāṃ smṛtiṃ kāntimanāmayatvamāyuḥprakarṣaṃ pavanānulomyam।
strīṣu praharpaṃ balamindriyāṇāmagneśca kuryādvidhinopayuktaḥ॥
au49.48
madhukena tavakṣīryā pipalyā sindhujanmanā।
pṛthaglohaiḥ suvarṇena vacayā madhusarpiṣā॥
au49.49
sitayā vā samāyuktā samāyuktā rasāyanam।
triphalā sarvarogaghnī medhāyuḥsmṛtibuddhidā॥
au49.50
traiphalenāyasīṃ pātrīṃ kalkenālepayennavām।
tamahorātrikaṃ lepaṃ pibet kṣaudrodakāplutam॥
au49.51
prabhūtasnehaśamanaṃ jīrṇe tatra praśasyate।
jīvatyarugjarastasya samābhyāsātsamāḥ śatam॥
au49.52
varṣaṃ khādet prāṇadāṃ prātarekāmaśnannannāt pūrvamakṣadvayaṃ ca।
sājyakṣaudraṃ bhojanānte catuṣkaṃ dhātrīkānāṃ tadvayaḥsthāpane'lam॥
au49.53
athāyasāni caturaṅguladīrghavistṛtāni tilotsedhāni patrāṇi kārayet।
tannyagnivarṇāni kṛtvāmalakasvarase nirvāpayedekaviṃśatikṛtvaḥ।
teṣāṃ tādṛśānāṃ palaśatamāyasyāṃ sthālyāṃ prakṣipyāmalakasvarasottaraṃ kṛtvā supihitaṃ bhasmahitaṃ bhasmarāśau nikhanet।
māsi māsi coddṛtyāyasena daṇḍena ghaṭṭayet।
śuṣyatyāmalakasvarasaṃ pūrvavadāvapet।
evaṃ tāni lohapatrāṇi saṃvatsarāt dravībhavanti।
tataścottarakālaṃ kṛtvā vamanavirecanaṃ snigdhatanureva kevalaṃ samantatoṅguṣṭhaparvamātramukhenāyasena sruveṇāyasa eva bhājane tasmāt kalkīkṛtāt sruvamekaṃ gṛhītvā madhudhṛtābhyāṃ pṛthak sruveṇa saṃyojya prāśnīyāt।
jīrṇe kṣīrarasayūṣāṇāmanyatamena sarpirmiśraṃ navaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanamaśnīyāt।
anena vidhinā varṣamupayujya varṣameva cānyadapyuddiṣṭāhāro yantritātmā kuṭīṃ samadhivaset।
tataḥ sarvopatāpān jitvā vyādhijarāmaraṇaśastrāgnitoyaviṣāṇāmagamyaḥ sarvabhāveṣvatīndiryo varṣasahasradvayaṃ jīvati॥
au49.54
vājivego gajaprāṇo bhavecca smṛtibuddhimān।
vāgmī vṛṣaḥ śrutadharo mahābhogo mahādhanaḥ॥
au49.55
tāmrarūpyasuvarṇānāmayameva pṛthagvidhiḥ।
dviguṇaṃ tadguṇotkarṣaṃ jānīyāduttarottaram॥
au49.56
hemadhātrīphalakṣaudraṃ gāyatrīparimantritam।
lihannanupiban kṣīraṃ dṛpṭariṣṭopi jīvati॥
au49.57
suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ priyaṅgavaḥ।
kṣīreṇa pītaṃ paramamalakṣmīvinivāraṇam॥
au49.58
sapadmabījāmalakābhayākṣaṃ sarpirmadhubhyāṃ kanakaṃ lihantaḥ।
dīrghāyuṣo mandajaropatāpāḥ sarīsṛpāṇāṃ ca bhavantyagamyāḥ॥
au49.59
madhumāgadhikāviḍaṅgasāratriphalā hema ghṛtaṃ sitāṃ ca khādan।
jarasānavalīḍhadehakāntiḥ samadhātuśca samāḥ śataṃ ca jīvet॥
au49.60
hemabilvavacārsīparaikadhyamupayojitam।
medhyamāyuṣyamārogyakāntisaubhāgyapuṣṭidam॥
au49.61
śatāvarīghṛtaṃ līḍhaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ samākṣikam।
karoti cirajīvitvaṃ rājānaṃ ca vaśānugam॥
au49.62
āyuṣkāmaḥ śaṅkhapuṣpyāsametaṃ medhākāmaḥ kāñcanaṃ sogragandham।
lakṣmīkāmaḥ padmakiñjalkayuktaṃ yuktaṃ khādet kāmakāmo vidāryā॥
au49.63
maṇḍūkaparṇyāḥ svarasaṃ yathāgni kṣīreṇa yaṣṭīmadhukasyacūrṇam।
rasaṃ guḍūcyāḥ sahamūlapuṣpyāḥ kalkaṃ prayuñjīta ca śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ॥
au49.64
āyuḥpradānyāmayanāśanāni balāgnivarṇasvaravarddhanāni।
medhyāni caitāni rasāyanāni medhyā viśeṣeṇa tu śaṅkhapuṣpī॥
au49.65
naladaṃ kaṭurohiṇī payasyā madhukaṃ candanasārivogragandhāḥ।
triphalā kaṭukatrayaṃ haridre sapaṭolaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca taiḥ supiṣṭaiḥ॥
au49.66
triguṇena rasena śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ sapayaskaṃ ghṛtanalvaṇaṃ vipakvam।
upayujya bhavejjaḍopi vāgmī śrutadhārī pratibhānavānarogaḥ॥
au49.67
peṣyairmṛṇālavisakesarapatrabījaiḥ siddhaṃ sahemaśakalaṃ payasā ca sarpiḥ।
pañcāravindamiti tatprathitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ prabhraṣṭapauruṣabalapratibhairniṣevyam॥
au49.68
yannālakandadalakesaravadvipakaṃ nīlotpalasyatadapi prathitaṃ pṛthivyām।
sarpiścatuṣkuvalayaṃ sahiraṇyapatraṃ medhyaṃ gavāmapi bhavet kimumānuṣāṇām॥
au49.69
brāhmīvacāsaindhavaśaṅkhapuṣpī matsyākṣakabrahmasuvarcalaindrayaḥ।
vaidehikā ca triyavāḥ pṛthaksyuryavau suvarṇasya tilo viṣasya॥
au49.70
sarpiṣaśca palamekata eta dyojayet pariṇate ca ghṛtāḍhyām।
bhojanaṃ samadhu vatsaramevaṃ śīlayannadhikadhīsmṛtimedhāḥ॥
au49.71
atikrāntajarāvyādhitandrālasyaśramaklamaḥ।
jīvatyabdaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ śrītejaḥkāntidīptimān॥
au49.72
viśeṣataḥ kuṣṭhakilāsagulma viṣajvaronmādagarodarāṇi।
atharvamantrādikṛtāśca kṛtyāḥ śāmyantyanenātibalāśca vātāḥ॥
au49.73
yathoktaguṇāyāṃ bhūmau jātāmabālāmajīrṇāṃ śīrṇapurāṇaparṇāmasañjātānyaparṇāṃ tape tapasye vā māse yathoktena vidhinā puṣyayukte candramasi sumuhurte nāgabalāṃ samūlāmuddharet।
tasyā mūlānāṃ tvakpiṇḍamāmramātramakṣamātraṃ vā ślakṣṇapiṣṭamavacūrṇitaṃ vā payasā pibenmadhughṛtābhyāṃ vā lihyāt।
jīrṇe kṣīravṛttireva syāt।
kṣīreṇaiva vā sasarṣiṣkaṃ śāliṣaṣṭikamaśnīyāt।
evaṃ saṃvatsaraprayogādvarṣaśatamajara ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.74
balātibalācandanāgarudhavatiniśakhadirakadaraśākaśiṃśapāsanasurasāpunarnavānantāśca vayaḥsthāpanoktā daśauṣadhayaḥ savidārīśvadaṃṣṭrāśvagandhāvārāhīśatāvaryo nāgabalayā vyākhyātāḥ॥
au49.75
tatra sāravṛkṣāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ svarasārthī kuṣṭhacikitsite khadirakalpamīkṣeta।
ārdravṛkṣāsambhave tu sāraśakalānidvyaṅgulatryaṅgulāni tanūni caturguṇembhsyā plāvyātape trirātraṃ sthāpayet।
tatastānyuddhṛtyānyāni tatra kṣipet।
trirātrācca punaranyānyevaṃ navarātreṇa triḥprakṣepaṇoddhāreṇa ca svarasaḥ parikalpito bhavati॥
au49.76
phalānāṃ punarvīrudauṣadhīnāṃ ca yantreṇolūkhalena vā saṅkṣudya niṣpīḍya svarasaṃ gṛhṇīyāt॥
au49.77
pariśuṣkāṇāṃ tu cūrṇikṛtānāmāḍhakamāḍhakamudakasyāhorātrasthitaṃ vimṛditapūtaṃ svarasavat prayojyam।
tuvarakabhallātakādīnāṃ punaḥ pṛthagevopadeśaḥ॥
au49.78
vṛkṣāstuvarakā nāma paścimārṇavatīrajāḥ।
vīcītaraṅgavikṣobhamārutoddhūtapallavāḥ॥
au49.79
tebhyaḥ phalānyādadīta supakvānyambudāgame।
majñaḥ phalemyaścādāya śoṣayitvāvacūrṇyaṃ ca॥
au49.80
tilavatpīḍayedroṇyāṃ kvāthayedvā kusumbhavat।
tattailaṃ sambhṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ pacedāsalilakṣayāt॥
au49.81
avatārya karīṣe ca pakṣamātraṃ nidhāpayet।
snigdhasvainno hṛtamalaḥ pakṣāduddhṛtya yatnavān॥
au49.82
caturthabhaktāntaritaḥ prātaḥ pāṇitalaṃ pibet।
mantreṇānena etasya tailasya divase śubhe॥
au49.83
majjasāra mahāvīrya sarvān dhātūn viśodhaya।
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇistvāmājñāpayate'cyutaḥ॥
au49.84
tenāsyordhvamadhastācca doṣā yāntyasakṛttataḥ।
sāyamasnehalavaṇāṃ yavāgūṃ śītalāṃ pibet॥
au49.85
pañcāhāni pibettailamitthaṃ varjyāni varjayet।
pakṣaṃ mudgarasānnāśī sarvakuṣṭhairvimucyate॥
au49.86
tadevakhadirakvāthe triguṇe sādhu sādhitam।
nihitaṃ pūrvavat pakṣaṃ pibenmāsaṃ suyantritaḥ॥
au49.87
tenābhyaktaśarīraśca kurvannāhāramīritam।
bhinnasvaraṃ raktanetraṃ śīrṇāṅgaṃ kṛmibhakṣitam।
anenāśu prayogeṇa sādhayet kuṣṭhinaṃ naram॥
au49.88
sarpirmadhuyutaṃ pītaṃ tadeva khadirādvinā।
pakṣaṃ māṃsarasāhāraṃ karoti dviśatāyuṣam॥
au49.89
tadeva nasye pañcāśaddivasānupayojitam।
valīpalitanirmuktasthirasmṛtikacadvijam॥
au49.90
vapuṣmantaṃ śrutadharaṃ karoti triśatāyuṣam।
antrdhūmaṃ tasya majjā sudagdhaḥ kṣiptastaile saindhavaṃ cāgnivarṇam।
tulyaṃ hanyādarmanaktāndhyakācān nīlīrogaṃ taimiraṃ cāñjanena॥
au49.91
ekāntaraṃ tauvarakañca tailaṃ pibeddhitāśī niyamena māsam।
prabhinnakoṣṭho galitāṅgadeśastvacaṃ tyajet sarpaivāśu jīrṇam॥
au49.92
sādhayet ṣoḍaśaguṇe salile tuvarāḍhakam।
aṣṭāṃśaśeṣe visrāvya saṅkṣudyolūkhale tataḥ॥
au49.93
śuṣkāragvadhavalkapādarajasā vyāmiśrita kalkitaṃ।
tasya kvāthajalairudumbarasamān chāyāviśuṣkān guḍān॥
au49.94
kuryādekatamaṃ ca sārddhamathavā govāriṇāloḍitaṃ।
kuṣṭhī taddivasāsthito niraśanaḥ sūrye gate'staṃ pibet॥
au49.95
tāvadeva ca tathaiva ca bhūyaḥ pāyayettamaruṇodayakāle।
apyajīrṇamavicintya vamiṃ vā bheṣajaṃ puruṣadoṣabalajñaḥ॥
au49.96
madhyāhne'dyāt bhūriniṣpāvatailaṃ kaṅgūkūraṃ śigrukandopadaṃśam।
dadhnāyuktaṃ svalpasindhūtthacūrṇaṃ gavyenānu stokatakrāmbupāyī॥
au49.97
tailāktagātro divasāntaraṃ ca kaṅgviṣṭikācūrṇakṛtapragharṣaḥ।
snāyāt sukhāmbhobhiramadyamāṃsa strīsaṅgatiḥ syāttriguṇaṃ ca yogāt॥
au49.98
upayujya yogamakhilaṃ pratidinameva dvikālamabhiyuktaḥ।
kuṣṭhī kuṣṭhamapohati viśīrṇakarṇauṣṭhanāsamapi॥
au49.99
atha bhallātakānyanupahatānyanāmayānyāpūrṇarasaprpamāṇavīryāṇi pakrajāmbavaprakāśāni śucau śukre vā māse saṅgṛhya yavapalle māṣapalle vā nidhāpayet।
tāni caturmāsasthitāni sahe sahasye vā māse prayoktumārabheta।
śītasnigdhamadhuropaskṛtaśarīraḥ pūrvaṃ daśabhallātakānyāpothyāṣṭaguṇenāmbhasā sādhu sādhayet।
teṣāṃ rasamaṣṭabhāgāvaśiṣṭamanuṣṇaṃ sapayaskaṃ sarpirgaṇḍūṣābhyaktoṣṭhatālujihvaḥ prātaḥ pibet।
evametānī daśabhallātakānyekaikotkarṣāpakarṣeṇa triṃśatprayojyāni।
vidhinānena sahasraprayogastriguṇaśca kālo ghṛtakṣīrābhyāṃ śāliṣaṣṭikamaśanamevaṃ viśeṣādvigatakuṣṭhadurnāmakṛmipramehamedodoṣo varṣaśatamajara ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.100
pūrvamekaikabhallātakakvāthaṃ sapayaskaṃ pibedekaikaṃ ca bhallātakamabhivarddhayedyāvat pañca।
tataḥ pañca pañcavardhayedyāvat saptatiḥ।
prāpya ca saptatimapakarṣayet bhūyaḥ pañca pañca yāvat pañca।
pañcabhyaścaikaikaṃ yāvadekam।
vidhinānenasahasraṃ prayoga ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.101
saptativacca śatamupayuñjīta।
tathā ca sahasradvayan।
prayoga ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa।
dviguṇastvāyuṣaḥ kālaḥ॥
au49.102
bhallātakānāṃ jarjarīkṛtānāṃ piṣṭasvedanaṃ pūrayitvā bhūmāvākāṇṭhanikhātasya snehabhāvitasya dṛḍhasyoparikumbhasyāropyoḍupenāpidhāyakṛṣṇabhṛdāvaliptaṃ gomayāgninopasvedayet।
teṣāṃ yaḥ svarasaḥ kumbhaṃ prapadyate tamaṣṭabhāgamadhusaṃyuktaṃ dviguṇitaghṛtamadyāt।
triguṇaśca kālo ghṛtakṣīrābhyāmityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.103
anenaiva vidhinā bhallātakasya rasaṃ gṛhītvā kevalameva māsamekaṃ prayuñjīta।
triguṇaśca kāla ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa।
māsi māsi varṣaśatamāyuṣobhivṛddhiḥ।
evaṃ daśamāsānupayujya varṣasahasramāyurbhavati॥
au49.104
bhallātakatailapātraṃ sapayaskaṃ madhukākṣamātreṇa śatapākamupayuñjīta।
triguṇaścakāla ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.105
bhallātakatailaṃ kṛṣṇatilatailaṃ sarpirāmalakaraso'sanādisārakaṣāya ityeṣāṃ droṇaṃ droṇaṃ triphalātrikaṭukaviḍaṅgasāracitrakaharidrādvayatrivṛddantīndrayavayaṣṭīmadhukaviṣātiviṣārasāñjanapriyaṅgūnāṃ pālikābhāgāstadaikadhyaṃ snehapākavidhinā vipācyāvatārya paripūyacānuguptaṃ nidadhyāt।
tata upaskṛtaśarīraḥ prātaḥ prātaḥ pāṇiśuktimātraṃ kṣaudreṇa pratisaṃsṛjyopayuñjīta।
jīrṇe mudvāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena sarpiṣmatā khadirodakasiddhaṃ mṛdumodanamaśnīyāt।
khadirodakenodakakāryāṇītyevamato droṇamupayujya vigatakuṣṭhadurnāmetyādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.106
puṣṭāni pākenaparicyutāni bhallātakānyāḍhakasammitāni।
ghṛṣṭveṣṭikācūrṇakaṇairjalena prakṣālya saṃśoṣya ca mārutena॥
au49.107
jarjarāṇi vipacejjalakumbhe pādaśeṣadhṛtagālitaśītam।
tadrasaṃ punarapi śrapayeta kṣīrakumbhasahitaṃ caraṇasthe॥
au49.108
sarpiḥ pakvaṃ tena tulyapramāṇaṃ yuñjyāt svecchaṃ śarkarāyā rajobhiḥ।
ekībhūtaṃ tatkhajakṣobhaṇena sthāpyaṃ dhānye saptarātraṃ suguptam॥
au49.109
tamamṛtarasapākaṃ yaḥ prage prāśamaśnannanu pibati yatheṣṭaṃ vāri dugdhaṃ rasaṃ vā।
smṛtimatibalamedhāsatvasārairupetaḥ kanakanikaṣagauraḥ sośnute dīrghamāyuḥ॥
au49.110
droṇe'mbhaso vraṇakṛtāṃ triśatādvipakvāt kvāthāḍhake palasamaistilatailapātram।
tiktāviṣādvayavarā girijanmatārkṣyaiḥ siddhaṃ paraṃ nikhilakuṣṭhaniṣūdanāya॥
au49.111
sahāmalakaśuktibhirdadhisareṇa tailena vā।
guḍena payasā ghṛtena yavasaktubhirvā saha।
tilena saha mākṣikeṇa palalena sūpena vā।
vapuṣkaramaruṣkaraṃ paramamedhyamāyuṣkaram॥
au49.112
bhallātakāni tīkṣṣṇāni pākīnyagnisamāni ca।
bhavanytamṛtakalpāni prayuktāni yathāvidhi॥
au49.113
kaphajo na sa rogāsti na vibandhostikaścana।
yaṃ na bhallātakaṃ hanyācchīghramagnibalapradam॥
au49.114
vātātapavidhānepi viśeṣeṇa vivarjayet।
kulatthadadhiśuktāni tailābhyaṅgāgnisevanam॥
au49.115
pañcāṣṭau sapta daśa vā pippalīrmadhusarpiṣā।
rasāyanaguṇānveṣī samāmekāṃ prayojayet॥
au49.116
tisrastisrastu pūrvāhne bhuktvāgre bhojanasya ca।
pippalyaḥ kiṃśukakṣārabhāvitā ghṛtabharjitāḥ।
prayojyā madhusammiśrā rasāyanaguṇauṣiṇā॥
au49.117
kramavṛdhyā daśāhāni daśapaippalikaṃ dinam।
vardhayet payasā sārddhaṃ tathaivāpanayet punaḥ॥
au49.118
jīrṇauṣadhaśca bhuñjīta ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpiṣā।
pippalīnāṃ sahasrasya prayogoyaṃ rasāyanam॥
au49.119
piṣṭāstā balibhiḥ peyāḥ śṛtā madhyabalairnaraiḥ।
śītīkṛtā drasvabalairyojyā doṣāmayān prati॥
au49.120
tadvaca chāgadugdhena dve sahasre prayojayet॥
au49.121
ebhiḥ prayogaiḥ pippalyaḥ kāsaśvāsagalagrahān।
yakṣmamehagrahaṇyarśaḥ pāṇḍutvaviṣamajvarān।
ghnanti śophaṃ vamiṃ hidhmāṃ plīhānaṃ vātaśoṇitam॥
au49.122
viḍaṅgacūrṇaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukacūrṇayuktaṃ śītatoyena samāśamupayuñjīta।
jīrṇe mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇena saghṛtamodanamaśnīyāt।
tena viśeṣādvigatakṛmidurnāmakuṣṭhapramehamedodoṣo varṣaśatamajara ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa।
