viḍaṅgacūrṇaṃ kṣaudrabhallātakakvāthābhyāṃ madhvāmalakarasābhyāṃ guḍūcīkvāthena ca etāṃścaturo yogān māsamupayuñjīteti samānaṃ pūrveṇa।
sarveṣu ca māsimāsi varṣaśatamāyuṣo'bhivṛddhiḥ॥
au49.123
alambuṣāṃ svena rasena bhāvitāṃ pṛthagghṛtakṣīramadhūṣṇavāribhiḥ।
pibettathā kāñjikatakramastubhirbhagandarorugrahagulmakāsavān॥
au49.124
uṣṇā vipāke kaṭukā kaṣāyamadhurā rase।
atyantadīpanī medhyā vātaśleṣmaharā ca sā॥
au49.125
varṣopayogāt kurute naraṃ varṣaśatāyuṣam।
dṛḍhendriyānalabalaṃ nirvalīpalitāmayam॥
au49.126
śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapaśuṣkāṇī cūrṇayitvā tattulyaguḍena saṅkṣudya ghṛtakumbhe dhānyarāśau saptparātraṃ nidadhyāt।
tato'nudite bhāsvati yathābalaṃ mātrāṃ sukhodakānupānāmupayojayet।
jīrṇe sukhāmbupariṣitaḥ śāliṣaṣṭikaudanaṃ saśarkareṇa payasāśnīyāt।
tasya māsaprayogādviśeṣeṇa vigatakuṣṭho grahaṇadhāraṇavān varṣaśatamajara ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa।
prayogataścordhvaṃ dviguṇaṃ parihāraḥ॥
au49.127
vākucikākarṣacūrṇaṃ sukhāmbunā pibet।
pītvā cātape nirvātoṣṇe vā garbhagṛhe tiṣṭhedaparāhṇe tadvadeva srānamaśanaṃ ca।
yūṣarasābhyāṃ vā।
tasya trisaptarātraprayogādvigatakuṣṭha ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.128
tvagromakeśadaśanān nakhāṃścamuktvā punarnavān labhate।
svaravarṇabalotsāhaṃ navaṃ vayo naṣṭapalitaṃ ca॥
au49.129
palāni daśa bākucyā daśaiva ca phalatrayāt।
sapta krimighnādayasastrīṇi dve girisambhavāt॥
au49.130
purapuṣkaramūlābhyāmāhareta palaṃ palam।
sūkṣmailārdhapalaṃ vyoṣaghanakesarakuṅkumam॥
au49.131
lodhratvakpatrayaṣṭyāhvacitrakaṃ kārṣikaṃ pṛthak।
śataṃbhallātakānāṃ ca sarvaṃ khaṇḍasamāṃsakam॥
au49.132
cūrṇayedatha tanmātrāṃ bhakṣayet pālikīṃ parām।
yatheṣṭaceṣṭo labhate varṣādrāsāyanān guṇān॥
au49.133
sarvarogān vijayate tvagvikārān viśeṣataḥ।
arśobhagandaraśvāsakāsapāṇḍvāmayakrimīn॥
au49.134
gulmaplīhāśmarīvardhamapramehārucipīnasān।
mandānalatvaṃ kṛśatāṃ śophagranthyarbudānapi॥
au49.135
vākucikāphalāni gomūtre saptarātraṃ vāsayet।
tato nistuṣīkṛtya chāyāyāṃ viśoṣayitvā susūkṣmaṃ ca sañcūrṇya tryahaṃ tryahaṃ kramaśo bhāvayettriphalākvathena kāravallīvāsābrāhmīguḍūcībhṛṅgarājasvarasaiḥ pṛthakpṛthak khadirāsanarājavṛkṣapicumandakvāthaiḥ॥
au49.136
tasya pītaḥ pratidinaṃ dhātrīphalarasāplutaḥ।
karṣaḥ sarvāmayān hanti tvagvikārānviśeṣataḥ॥
au49.137
asanakhadirayūṣairbhāvitāṃ somarājīṃ।
madhughṛtaśikhipathyālohacūrṇairupetām।
śaradamavalihānaḥ pāriṇāmān vikārāṃ।
styajati mitahitāśī tadvadāhārajātān॥
au49.138
tīvreṇa kuṣṭhena parītamūrttiryaḥsomarājīṃ niyamena khādet।
saṃvatsaraṃ kṛṣṇatiladvitīyāṃ sasomarājīṃ vapuṣātiśete॥
au49.139
ye somarājyā vituṣīkṛtāyāścūrṇairupetāt payasaḥ sujātāt।
uddhṛtya sāraṃ madhunā lihanti takraṃ tadevānu pibanti cānte॥
au49.140
te kuṣṭhinaḥ pakṣmadaridranetrā।
viśīrṇakarṇāṅgulināsikā vā।
vihāyavairūpyamapāsya rūpaṃ।
punaḥ prarūḍhā iva bhānti vṛkṣāḥ॥
au49.141
khadirāmbhasā pibedvā ravisevī tāṃ tayā yavāgūṃ vā।
gāyatrījalasiddhāṃ kuṣṭhī tattoyakāryakaraḥ॥
au49.142
gajaliṇḍakṣārayutā tatkṣārapāyino vilepibhujaḥ।
śvitrāṇi somarājī prasahya hanyāt pralepācca॥
au49.143
gomūtre saptarātraṃ śaśiśakalaphalaṃ vāsitaṃ lolayitvā।
kuryācchāyāviśuṣkaṃ pṛthagiti ca phalaṃ prāpunāṭaṃ ca śuṣkam॥
au49.144
aṃśastābhyāṃ tathāṃśaḥ kṛmiripudahana sphoṭakṛdbhyaḥ sa cūrṇo gomūtreṇopayuktaḥ pramitahitabhujaḥ ścitramāśveva hanti॥
au49.145
ikṣuragokṣurasiṃhī vyāghrī pañcāṃgulāmbunā pītā।
upalamaghanaṃ ghanaṃ vā rasāśināṃ hanti bākucikā॥
au49.146
uṣṇodakena piṣṭā pītā ca ghṛtānvitā jayet gulmam laghupañcamūlasiddhāṃ peyāmupayojayejjīrṇe॥
au49.147
kaṭvaṅgakuṭajayūṣairarśīṃsi bhagandaraṃ ca nāśayati।
mehān madyairnigadairniṣovitā bākucī prabalān॥
au49.148
viṣkirarasena pītā daśamūlarasena vā guḍūcyā vā।
apatantrakaṃ nihanyādāyāmaṃ vā rasānnabhujaḥ॥
au49.149
jaṭhareṣu pibenmūtrairjalodare traivṛtena yūṣeṇa।
śophe pāṇḍuvyādhāvavalgujaṃ śīghvariṣṭābhyām॥
au49.150
ikṣurakādikvāthairvardhmani mūtreṇa vā gavāṃ śastaḥ।
dhāroṣṇena tu payasā yuktaḥ śophajvarau hanti॥
au49.151
uṣṇāmbunā prayojyo lūtākīṭākhusarpadaṣṭeṣu।
kṛmiharacaturaṅgulayoḥ kvāthaḥ koṣṇaḥ kṛmiṇakoṣheṣu॥
au49.152
lekhāmindoḥ saghṛtāṃ sukhāmbunā putriṇī bhavati pītvā puṣṣodayeśvagandhāśṛtena payasā ca bhuñjānā॥
au49.153
vandhyāpi saptāhamimaṃprayogaṃ karoti yā harṣayatī sugandhiḥ।
priyaṃvadā sadvrataśaucayuktā sūte sutān sā niyamāt guṇāḍhyān॥
au49.154
snigdhairuṣṇairmadhurairharati gadānvātajān yutā paittān।
tiktakamadhurakaṣāyaiḥ kaphajāṃstriphalārasamadhubhyāṃ ca॥
au49.155
iti śamanī dhanyeyaṃ viṣagarabhūtopasargapāpmaghnī।
gehe sthitāpi rekhā cāndramasī kimuta koṣṭhasthā॥
au49.156
manuṣyamapyāgatamṛtyuśāsanaṃ praṇaṣṭabuddhīndriyamalpacetasam।
avalgujo mokṣayate mahābhayācchriyaṃ ca medhāṃ ca dadāti pupkalām॥
au49.157
haimavatyā vacāyāḥ piṇḍamāmalakamātraṃ payasāloḍya pibejjīrṇe payassarpirodana ityāhāraḥ।
evaṃ saptarātreṇa medhāvī bhavati।
saptabhiḥ saptarātraiḥ śrutadharo varṣaśatamajara ityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.158
itarasyā api vacāyā dvipalakvāthaṃ pibet jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa।
taccūrṇaṃ vā kṣaudrasarpibhyāṃ yathābalamavalihyāt।
jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirityādi samānaṃ pūrveṇa॥
au49.159
vacākalkaśatapākaṃ ghṛtadroṇamupayujya viśeṣāt grahonmādāpasmāragalagaṇḍagaṇḍamālāślīpadasvarabhedavimuktaḥ sarvārtheṣu siddhimān varṣaśatāyurbhavati॥
au49.160
śītavātahimadagdhatanūnāṃ stabdhabhagrakuṭilavyadhitāsthnām।
bheṣajasya pavanopahatānāṃ vakṣyate vidhirato laśunasya॥
au49.161
rāhoramṛtacauryeṇa lūnādye patitā galāt।
amṛtasya kaṇā bhūmau te rasonatvamāgatāḥ॥
au49.162
dvijānāśnanti tamato daityadehasumudbhavam।
sākṣādamṛtasambhūtergrāmaṇīḥ sa rasāyanam॥
au49.163
śīlayellaśunaṃ śīte vasante ca kapholbaṇaḥ।
ghanodayepi vātārttaḥ sadā vā grīṣmalīlayā।
raktapittabhavārogā jāyante raktapittinaḥ॥
au49.164
māsaḥ parosya rasakalkaniṣevaṇāya svacchandamapyupadiśanti vimardakaistu।
ṣaṇmāsamanyavidhinā na tu śastamāhuḥ pakṣaprayogamapi hīnataraṃ rasone॥
au49.165
srigdhaśuddhatanu śītamadhuropaskṛtāśayaḥ।
taduttaṃsāvataṃsābhyāṃ carcitānucarājiraḥ॥
au49.166
tasya kandān vasantānte himavacchakadeśajān।
apanītatvaco rātrau nimayenmadirādibhiḥ॥
au49.167
tatkalkasvarasaṃ prātaḥ śucitāntavapīḍitam।
madirāyāḥ surūḍhāyāstribhāgena samanvitam॥
au49.168
madyasyānyasya takrasya mastunaḥ kañjikasya vā।
tatkāla eva vā yuktaṃ yuktamālocya mātrayā॥
au49.169
tailasarpirvasāmajjakṣīramāsarasaiḥ pṛthak।
kvāthena vā yathāvyādhi rasaṃ kevalameva vā॥
au49.170
pibet gaṇḍūṣamātra prākkaṇṭhanāḍīviśuddhaye।
pratataṃ svedanaṃcānu vedanāyāṃ praśasyate॥
au49.171
śītāmbusekaḥ sahasā vamimūrcchāyayormukhe।
śeṣaṃ pibet klamāpāye sthiratāṃ gata ojasi॥
au49.172
vidāhaparihārāya paraṃ śītānulepanaḥ।
dhārayetsāmbukaṇikā muktākarpūramālikāḥ॥
au49.173
sahimasalilagarbhāścandraśubhrāmṛṇālīḥ kuvalayadalamālā hārayaṣṭīśca lolāḥ।
stanataṭaviniviṣṭāścārugātryo dadhānāstanusarasavilitā gāḍhamenaṃ svajeran॥
au49.174
nalinīdalatālavṛntavātaiḥ pragaladvārilavairjalārdrayā ca।
dayitākarapallavaiśca śītair śunasvedakṛtaṃ klamaṃ hareyuḥ॥
au49.175
kuḍavosyaparā mātrā tadarddhaṃ kevalasya tu।
palaṃ piṣṭasya tanmajjñaḥ sabhaktaṃ prākca śīlayet॥
au49.176
rasognikalpo mṛdunaujasā hi।
saṃyujyamānaḥ sahasaiva tasya।
dāhātisārāraticittanāśān।
kuryādatastaṃ tvarito na yuñjyāt॥
au49.177
jīrṇaśālyoddanaṃ jīrṇe śaṅkhakṛndendupāṇḍuram।
bhuñjīta yūṣaiḥ payasā rasairvā dhanvacāriṇām॥
au49.178
dīptāgnirmaṇḍakān khādet sarpiprmaṇḍopasecanān।
akhaṇḍamaṇḍalendvābhāniṇḍarīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitān॥
au49.179
rājikāśuktasamparkavinivartitagauravaiḥ।
piṣṭakācūrṇadhavalairvadhraiḥ saukarakairyutān॥
au49.180
madyamekaṃ pibettattu tṛṭprabandhe jalānvitam।
gandhamattakvaṇadali priyāvaktrendubodhitam॥
au49.181
amadyapo yastu phalāmbutukramavantisomaṃ ca sugandhi śītam।
sauvīrakaṃ jāṅgalajaṃ rasaṃ vā tuṣodakvaṃ vā parisikthikāṃ vā॥
au49.182
tatkalkaṃ vā samaghṛtaṃ ghṛtapātre khajāhatam।
sthitaṃ daśāhādaśnīyāttadvadvā vasayā samam॥
au49.183
sadyaḥ piṣṭaṃ sarpiṣā saṃyutaṃ vā niryāsena svena yuktaṃ ca kāmam।
yuñjītainaṃ pūrvakaireva pānaiḥ koṣṇāmbhobhirvaiṣa kalpotivīryaḥ॥
au49.184
rasonakalkaḥ sadṛśājasarpiḥ ṣaṇmāsamurvyāmuṣito nihanti।
abhyaṅgapānāñjananasyayukto manovikārān viṣamajvaraṃ ca॥
au49.185
samatailaṃ saśuktaṃ vā yavarāśau samāsthitam।
vātarogān jayet khādan ghṛtamāṃsottarāśanaḥ॥
au49.186
tailasarpirguḍasitāḥ pṛthakkuryāttulānmitāḥ।
dve tule laśunācchruddhāt tryūṣaṇāt kuḍayatrayam॥
au49.187
palaṃ tvacaśca tacślakṣṇaṃ nihitaṃ ghṛtabhājane।
dve same yavamadhyasthaṃ pūrvasmādadhikaṃ guṇaiḥ॥
au49.188
kṣuṇṇāṃ kṣipet kandatulāṃ takrasya palaviṃśatau।
gate ca saptarātre tu tulārddhamasitāttilāt॥
au49.189
dhautakṣuṇṇāt pṛthakkṣaudraghṛtaśuṇṭhīcatuṣpalam।
ajājīcavyadhānyāgnidvikṛṣṇāgranthidīpyakān॥
au49.190
palonmitāṃścaturjātāt palamekaṃ sucūrṇitam।
pṛthakpalāṣṭakaṃ tailātghṛtātkṣuṇṇāccasarṣapāt॥
au49.191
paṭūni pañca kṣārau dvau dadyāttatrākṣamānataḥ।
ekādaśāhaṃ taddhānye sthitamaśnan prage prage।
guṇānrāsāyanānsarvān sa prāpnoti nirāmayaḥ॥
au49.192
dvipaścamūlaniṣkvāthe nalvaṇe laśunāḍhakam।
piṣṭaṃ paryuṣitaṃ varṣaṃ hanti vātakaphāmayān॥
au49.193
tatkandakalkasvarase ghṛtatailaṃ pṛthakpacet।
śīlayecca yathāsātmyaṃ dāruṇānalapīḍitaḥ॥
au49.194
navanītasamāṃśaṃ vā khodattatkalkamarditī॥
au49.195
vikañcukaprājyarasonagarbhān saśūlyamāṃsān vividhopadaṃśān।
nimardakān vā ghṛtaśuktayuktān prakāmamadyāllaghutucchamaśnan॥
au49.196
kustumbarī jīrakabhṛṣṭamudgasauvarcalaślakṣṇarajovakīrṇaiḥ।
rasonakandāṅkurapatracitraiḥ savyañjanairnaikarasānuyātaiḥ॥
au49.197
tatkandasiddhān kramaśo yūṣakṣīrarasān pibet।
kaphapittānilāśaṅkī yathāsvauṣadhasaṃskṛtān॥
au49.198
kṛśośvagandhodbhavacūrṇakīrṇaṃ sannasvaro yaṣṭimadhūpadhānam।
tailena gulmī khadireṇa kuṣṭhī khādet kṛmighnaiḥ kṛmimān rasonam॥
au49.199
māṃsādamāṃsairyakṣmāṇamarśāṃsi kuṭajatvacā।
hanti sa śreṣṭhayā mehakāsaśvāsavilambikāḥ॥
au49.200
annasvarūpavijñānāt svarūpamupalabhya ca।
yathāyathaṃ prayogosya kāryastaṃ taṃ gadaṃ prati॥
au49.201
laśunasvarasāt prasthāndvātriṃśattilatailataḥ।
dvāvapetamalāt kiṇvādaṣṭaupiṣṭāccaṣaḍyavāt॥
au49.202
meṣaśṛṅgībhavāt kvāthādroṇaṃ pūtācca śītalāt।
snehapātre tadaikadhyaṃ nidadhyācca śucau dṛḍhe॥
au49.203
kramāttatra punardadyāt piṣṭaṃ prasthacatuṣṭayam।
pakṣātparamiyaṃ peyā surā vātavikāribhiḥ॥
au49.204
trirātramuṣitāṃ dhenuṃ laśunaṃ khādayettataḥ।
kṣīradadhyājyamathitaṃ brāhmaṇasyāpi śasyate॥
au49.205
pittaraktavinirmuktasamastāvaraṇāvṛte।
śuddhe vā vidyate vāyau na dravyaṃ laśunātparam॥
au49.206
sukhātmanāṃ viśeṣeṇa prayojyo laśunāsavaḥ।
nāradenoddhavasyaiṣa vātabhagnasya kalpitaḥ॥
au49.207
āmāmbupānekṣuvikāramatsyayānādhvavātātapabhāṣyacintāḥ।
svapnaṃ divā jāgaraṇaṃ niśāsu piṣṭaṃ vyavāyaṃ dadhi cātra necchet॥
au49.208
snehakalpavidhānena snehayuktaṃ prayojayet।
laśunaṃ snehasaṃyogāt garīyān jāyate hi saḥ॥
au49.209
pittakopabhayādante yuñjyānmṛduviecanam।
rasāyanaguṇānevaṃ paripūrṇān samaśnute॥
au49.210
priyāmbuguḍadugdhasya māṃsamadyāmlavidviṣaḥ।
atitikṣorajīrṇaṃ ca rasono vyāpade dhruvam॥
au49.211
pāṇḍūdarorakṣataśophatṛṣṇāpānātyayacchardiviṣavraṇeṣu।
paitte vikārekṣigadetisāre kṣāme śarīre ca sa varjanīyaḥ॥
au49.212
śīlita eṣa karoti durāpaṃ vahniśarīrabalaṃ samameva।
vaṅmatirūpaguṇāḍhyasutepsoḥ strīpuruṣasya ca bījaviśuddhim॥
au49.213
amṛtakaṇasamutthaṃ yo rasonaṃ rasonaṃ vidhiyutamitikhādecchītakāle sadaiva।
sa nayati śatajīvī strīsahāyo jarāntaṃ kanakaruciravarṇo nīrujastuṣṭijuṣṭaḥ॥
au49.214
rasonānantaraṃ vāyoḥ palāṇḍuḥ paramauṣadham।
sākṣādivasthitaṃ yatra śakādhipatijīvitam॥
au49.215
yasyopayogena śakāṅganānāṃ lāvaṇyasārādivinirmitānām।
kapolakāntyā vijitaḥ śaśāṅko rasātalaṃ gacchati nirvideva॥
au49.216
snigdhāṅgatvaṃ gauratā kāntimattā vanerdīptirvarṣmapuṣṭirvṛṣatvam।
samprāpyante yantraṇodvegamuktaiḥ ryasyābhyāsāddhāri dīrghaṃ sukhaṃ ca॥
au49.217
apyāhāre śīlito dīrghārātraṃ balyaścakṣuṣyastarpaṇaḥ sthairyakārī।
taistairyogairyojitoyaṃ palāṇḍustāṃstānātaṅkān mehināmucchinatti॥
au49.218
rasaṃ rasonavattasya pītvāśnīyāttathaiva ca।
sabījapūrasvarasamadirāmadhuśīdhupaḥ॥
au49.219
marakatamaṇinīlaṃ nālamasyātibālaṃ pariṇataśaśigauraṃ yacca bījaṃ supiṣṭam।
sasurasasumukhābhyāṃ prājyamāṃsaṃ saśuktaṃ mṛdudhavalasuvṛttairmaṇḍakairāttamūrtim॥
au49.220
vahuśaḥśobhitaṃ śubhraiḥ śaśāṅkaśakalopamaiḥ।
ghārikeṇḍarikāvallaiḥ kṣīrodāvayavairiva॥
au49.221
yavamudgamāṣagodhūma bahuvidha vikārakalpitān bhakṣyān।
kāmbalikarāgaṣāḍavasaṭṭakakhalakān saphalasārān॥
au49.222
paṭusurabhimadhuragandhān dhavalākṣakadhavalabahularasān।
kharjūradāḍimasitādrākṣāpānānupobhyasyet॥
au49.223
labhate balavarṇaujovīryasvarasaumanasyatejāṃsi।
kṣīṇaśakṛdrudhiropi ca rasonavattadrasaṃ pītvā॥
au49.224
surāsuraiḥkṣīrasamudramanthe gatāstaṭān ye'mṛtavipruṣaḥ purā।
babūva tebhyaḥ kila kukkuṭī yayā vrajanti devatvamivādya mānuṣāḥ॥
au49.225
kukkuṭāṇḍanibhaiḥ kandaiḥ kiñcit kaṭukapicchilaiḥ।
snigdhairmarakatacchāyaiḥ kharjūrasadṛśaicchadaiḥ॥
au49.226
nisvilarogaharāpi viśeṣato jayati dāruṇamapyanilāmayam।
gudajagulmatamoviṣanāśinī janayati sthiratāṃ vapuṣaḥ parām॥
au49.227
kuṭīṃ praviśyatatkandān bhakṣayetghṛtabharjitān।
payonupānaṃ dhāroṣṇaṃ tatreṣṭamasanāmbu vā॥
au49.228
tanmātravṛttistubhaveddaśāhaṃ viṃśatyahaṃ svādubhugapramādī।
jatrūrdhvakoṣṭhatrikasandhivātapāṇḍavāmayārśastimirāṇi jitvā॥
au49.229
valīpalitanirmuktaḥ sthirakeśadvijaśrutiḥ।
medhāmatismṛtiyuto jīvedvarṣaśatadvayam॥
au49.230
āpūryamāṇacandrapratipadamārabhyavardhayetkandam।
ekaikaṃ ghṛtabhṛṣṭaṃ prāgbhaktaṃ pathyabhukkhādet॥
au49.231
bhuñjītālpataraṃ dinārditamṛṣiḥ pakṣakṣaye bhakṣayan kṣīraṃ bījakavāri takramathavā pītvā sthitiṃ kalpayet।
māṃsaṃ prāśya tathā nakhadvijakacaḥ śīrṇotthitaiḥ kāntimān jīvatyabdaśatatrayaṃ dhṛtimatismṛtyādibhirbhūṣitaḥ॥
au49.232
kṣīreṇa kandacūrṇaṃ pibanyavāgūṃ ca pariṇate māsam।
lavaṇasnehavināṃ dṛḍhadṛgjīveccharaddviśatam॥
au49.233
timiraṃ kṣaudraghṛtābhyāṃ pathyabhujastadrajo jayenmāsāt।
kandatrayaṃ ca bhṛṣṭaṃ ghṛteśnato bhakṣitaṃ vātān॥
au49.234
tatkandasūkṣmarajasā tribhāgagodhūmacūrṇamiśreṇa।
payasā paktvā khādet ghṛtapūrānāntravṛddhiharān॥
au49.235
trīn kandakāṃśca niśi bhakṣayatājyabhṛṣṭān dhātrīphalāmbu sasitaṃ cahgalīpayo vā।
peyaṃ dṛgāmayajayāya niṣevitavyā kāmaṃ ca rogaśamamātraphalārthibhiḥ sā॥
au49.236
kṣīrānvitā mūlakatulyakandā saptāṣṭapatrāsitaraktakāṇḍā।
vibhartti yā pallavamabdaśabdāt sā kañcukī śvetavapurvareṇyā॥
au49.237
āṣāḍhe kārtike vāttaṃ tatkandaṃ śītalaṃ sthitam।
aṅguṣṭhaparvadvayasaṃ piṣṭaṃ kṣīrapalāṣṭake॥
au49.238
kuṭīpraveśastaṃ pītvā kṣīrameva pibedanu।
kṣīrameva ca jīrṇepi peyāṃ vā snehabharjitām॥
au49.239
kiñciduṣṇāmalavaṇāṃ spṛśeduṣṇāmbu no himam।
ekena saptarātreṇa kuṣṭhānyevaṃ niyacchati॥
au49.240
sarvavyādhīn dvitīyena tṛtīyena tu sarpavat।
tyaktvā tvacaṃ tato jīrṇāṃ keśadantanakhānapi।
dhīmedhārūpavān jīvet pañcavarṣaśatāni ca॥
au49.241
kañcukīkandacūrṇaṃ vā svena kṣīreṇa bhāvitam।
gokṣīrakuḍave nyataṃ karṣaṃ khaṇḍapalānvitam।
pītaṃ sarvābhayān hanti nakhakeśasthitānapi॥
au49.242
pītatatsvarasaṃ cūrṇaṃ tasyā madhughṛtānvitam।
khādanhitāśī saptāhaṃ tvagdoṣāṃstimiraṃ jayet॥
au49.243
viḍaṅgatāpyatriphalālohakañcukijaṃ rajaḥ।
saptarātratrayaṃ lihyānmadhunā saṃyatendriyaḥ॥
au49.244
kṣīreṇa bhojanaṃ jīrṇe śālerlābarasena vā।
tathāsya kācatyimire sukṛcchrāḥ śiraso gadāḥ॥
au49.245
medhāvinaḥ praṇaśyanti gātraṃ suptaṃ ca budhyate।
eṣa saptāmṛtaścūrṇaḥ sarvavyādhiṣu pūjitaḥ॥
au49.246
palaṃ cūrṇasya kañcukyāḥ kṣīraprasthe samāvapet।
snehaṃ dadhnastato lihyājjitātmā sasitāmadhu॥
au49.247
śālerannaṃ payaḥ pānaṃ māsamevaṃ prayojayet।
caturguṇaḥ parīhāraḥ śoṣaśābdasamadyutiḥ।
śatāni pañca varṣāṇāṃ jīveddeva ivorjitaḥ॥
au49.248
pacet palāni droṇepāṃ kañcukyāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ।
aṣṭāṃśaśiṣṭe tu ghṛtāt prasthaṃ kṣīrasamaṃ pacet॥
au49.249
śaṅkhapuṣpīvacākuṣṭhatrivṛtāmaradārubhiḥ।
varāyaṣṭīsitādrākṣāmahiṣākṣaiḥ palāṃśikaiḥ॥
au49.250
yuktaiḥ kamalakiñjalkatripalena hime'tra ca।
kṣaudrāccatuṣpalaṃ dadyādetanmartyāmṛtāhvayam।
cakṣuṣyaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ medhyaṃ varṇyaṃ varṣaśatapradam॥
au49.251
pacetpalāni kañcukyāstrīṇi lohātsucūrṇitāt।
palāśabījāccatvāri daśa dve ca phalatrayāt॥
au49.252
aṣṭādaśa śatāvaryā bījakasyaikāviṃśatiḥ।
jīvantyāḥ ṣoḍaśaikadhyaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vipācayet॥
au49.253
vahe'pāṃ pādaśeṣe ca pṛthagarddhāḍhakena ca।
pacet kāñjikamastubhyāṃ ghṛtaprasthaṃ picūnmitaiḥ॥
au49.254
śatāhvāruṣkaravacākuṣṭhailābiḍahiṅgubhiḥ।
sauvarcalānvitaiḥ padmakesarācca tribhiḥ palaiḥ॥
au49.255
pañcabhiḥ padmabījānāṃ padmadvādaśakena ca।
etat somāmṛtaṃ pītvā yassomo'dyāpi rājate॥
au49.256
idamupayujya sarpirativīryamudāraguṇaṃ bhavati suvāksudhīḥ sudṛḍhasubalaḥ subhagaḥ।
grahamarakopasargaviṣabhītibhiradhṛṣyavapurvijitajarājvaro nayati varṣaśatadvitayam॥
au49.257
dānavendra vijitān purā surān bhraṣṭakāntidhṛtidharyatejasaḥ।
vīkṣya viṣṇuramṛtaṃ kilāsṛjat gugguluṃ balavapurjayapradam॥
au49.258
adyāpyataḥ suragaṇāḥ kila dhūpamukhyān hitvā varāgaruturuṣkahimendudarpān।
nirdahyamānavapuṣṣo'pi śikhāṃ pibanto gandhena yasya muditā dadhati prasādam॥
au49.259
sa yogavāhī sa śivaḥ sa sārvaḥ sarvartusevyaḥ sukhaśīlanīyaḥ।
hantā jarāpāpmamalāmayānāṃ kartāgnimedhāsmṛtipāṭavānām॥
au49.260
gandhotkaṭaḥ sa dāhe snigdhadravapicchilo vigataśalyaḥ।
mahiṣākṣaḥ puṣparāga sphaṭikāsitanīradacchāyaḥ॥
au49.261
yaḥ padmarāgarāgo yaḥ kanakacchedapāṭalo yo vā।
jayatīndranīlamamalaṃ bhagnopyantikāntimatvena॥
au49.262
ātreyamunigītaśca mantroyaṃ karmasiddhikṛt।
bhagavān puṇḍarīkākṣo devāśca sapurandarāḥ॥
au49.263
jarāmaraṇaduḥkhebhyo yathā tegyutthitāḥ surāḥ।
upayoktustathaivāsya bhava tvaṃ hi mahābala॥
au49.264
pañcamūlasya mahataḥ kvāthena hitabhojinā।
gugguluḥ śīlito hanti sarvān vātakaphāmayān॥
au49.265
laghīyasopi tadvacca sukhoṣṇena jalena vā।
mastudhānyāmlamadyairvā vacādeḥ salilena vā॥
au49.266
varaṇādestu bādhiryadantakarṇaśirorujaḥ।
svarabhedodaraśvāsavardhmāntargulmavidradhīn॥
au49.267
vātapittāsrarogeṣu bṛṃhaṇārthini ceṣyate।
kvāthena vājigandhāyā jīvanīyagaṇasya vā॥
au49.268
kvāthenotpalamṛdvīkāraktacandanajanmanā।
vātapittaṃ nihantyeṣa padmakādigaṇasya vā॥
au49.269
cavyakuṣṭhaviḍaṅgānāṃ yānyā nāgarasya vā।
prasāriṇyāśca toyena gugguluḥ kaphavātajit॥
au49.270
tryūṣaṇāgnighanavellavarābhirbhakṣayan samaghṛtaṃ mahiṣākṣam।
āśu hanti kaphamārutamedodoṣajān balavatopi vikārān॥
au49.271
paṭolanimbatriphalāguḍūcī gāyatrirātridvayabījakānām।
kvāthaiḥ pṛthakpathyaparasya hanti māsena ghorān kaphapittarogān॥
au49.272
viśeṣācchophavīsarpaduṣṭavraṇabhagandarān।
śukrārtavamanodoṣapramehaśvitrapāṇḍutāḥ॥
au49.273
paṭolāriṣṭīrnayūhapiṣṭastulyarasāñjanaḥ।
galagogāpacīvyaṅgagranthisthaulyakṛmipraṇut॥
au49.274
śilājatusamaḥpītaḥ payasā vātaśoṇitam।
nivartayatyatibalaṃ kṣīramāṃsaghṛtāśinaḥ॥
au49.275
rasena payasā mūtrairvātapittakaphāpahaḥ।
brāhmīmaṇḍūkaśaṅkhānāṃ pṛthaṅmedhādikṛdrasaiḥ॥
au49.276
māgadhikāgnikaliṅgabiḍagairbilvadhṛtaiḥ savarāpalaṣaṭkaiḥ।
guggulunā sadṛśena sametaiḥ kṣaudrayutaiḥ sakalāmayanāśaḥ॥
au49.277
pibet palaśataṃ yosya vidhinā niyato yatiḥ।
nākālamṛtyorna vyādherna tasya jaraso bhayam॥
au49.278
kalpayedauṣadhaiḥ svai svairvyādhiṣu vyādhināśanaiḥ॥
au49.279
śilājatuvidhānaṃ ca gugguloḥ sarvamiṣyate॥
au49.280
guṇanidhirapikuryāt sotimātropayuktastimiravadanaśoṣaklabitākārśyamohān।
śamalaśithilabhāvaṃ deharaukṣyaṃ ca tasmādrajanicaraniṣevīsyyānna rogeṣvamīṣu॥
au49.281
grīṣmerkataptā girayo jatutulyaṃ vamanti yat।
hemādiṣaṭdhāturasaṃ procyate tacchilājatu॥
au49.282
sarvadoṣapraśamanaṃ sarvarogavināśanam।
śilābhyo yasya yajjātaṃ dhātostattadguṇaṃ vadet॥
au49.283
sarvaṃ ca tiktakaṭukaṃ nātyuṣṇaṃ kaṭu pākataḥ।
chedanaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa lauhaṃ tatra praśasyate॥
au49.284
gomūtragandhi kṛṣṇaṃ guggulvābhaṃ viśarkaraṃ mṛtsnam।
snigdhamanamlakaṣāyaṃ mdṛu guru ca śilājatu śreṣṭham॥
au49.285
rāsnādaśamūlabalā punarnavairaṇḍaśuṇṭhimadhukānām।
kvāthena bhāvitaṃ tadviśeṣato vātarogaghnam॥
au49.286
drākṣābhīrupaṭolatrāyantiguḍūcijīvanīyānām।
niryūheṇa subhinnaṃ śastaṃ pittāmaye sutarām॥
au49.287
krimijidvacāphalatraya karañjaghanamukhyapañcamūlānām।
sahapañcakolakānāṃ kvāthena kaphāmaye bhāvyam॥
au49.288
laghupañcamūlaśuṇṭhī drākṣākāśmaryavājigandhānām।
saguḍūciśarabalānāṃ rasena pittānilagadeṣu॥
au49.289
ghanakuṣṭhavacātriphalā suradāruviḍaṅgapañcakolānām।
rajanīmaricātiviṣā yuktānāṃ vātakaphajeṣu॥
au49.290
pāṭhāpaṭolanimbatriphalāghanakuṭajasaptaparṇānām।
trāyantyamṛtātiviṣāsahitānāṃ pittakaphajeṣu॥
au49.291
nicaye'pidoṣabalato yogānetān vikalpya yujjīta।
vividhagaṇasaṅgrahoktaistaistaiśca gaṇairgiressāram॥
au49.292
vyādhivyādhitasātmyaṃ samanusaran bhāvayedayaḥ pātre।
prākkevalajaladhautaṃ śuṣkaṃ kvāthaistato bhāvyam॥
au49.293
samagirijamaṣṭaguṇite niṣkkāthyaṃ bhāvanauṣadhaṃ toye।
tanniryūhe'ṣṭāṃśe pūtoṣṇe prakṣipet girijam॥
au49.294
tat samarasatāṃ yātaṃ saṃśuṣkaṃ prakṣipedrase bhūyaḥ।
svaisvairevaṃ kvāthairbhāvyaṃ vārān bhavet sapta॥
au49.295
atha snigdhasya śuddhasya ghṛtaṃ tiktakasādhitam।
tryahaṃ yuñjīta girijamekaikena tathā tryaham॥
au49.296
phalatrayasya yūṣeṇa paṭolyā madhukasya ca।
yogayogyaṃ tatastasya kālāpekṣaṃ prayojayet॥
au49.297
śilājamevaṃ dehasya bhavatyatyupakārakam।
guṇān samagrān kurute sahasā vyāpadaśca na॥
au49.298
ekatrisaptasaptāhaṃ karṣamarddhapalaṃ palam।
hīnamadhyottamo yogaḥ śilājasya kramānmataḥ॥
au49.299
saṃskṛtaṃ saṃskṛte dehe prayuktaṃ girijāhvayam।
yuktaṃ vyastaiḥ samastairvā tāmrāyorūpyahemabhiḥ॥
au49.300
kṣīreṇāloḍitaṃ kuryācchīghraṃ rāsāyanaṃ phalam।
hanyādrogānaśeṣāṃśca jīrṇe hitamitāśinaḥ॥
au49.301
vyāyāmātapamārutacetaḥsantāpaguruvidāhyādi।
upayogādapi parato dviguṇaṃ parivarjayet kālam॥
au49.302
kulatthān kākamācīṃ ca kapotāṃśca sadā tyajet।
pibenmāhendramudakaṃ kaupaṃ prāsravaṇāmbu vā॥
au49.303
jvarī jvaraghnāmbudaparpaṭādeḥ kvāthena raktī madhuyaṣṭikāyāḥ।
śoṣī saraiḥ kravyabhugāmiṣotthairmāyuramāṃsaiḥ payasā ca kārśye॥
au49.304
madhvambunā medasi sampravṛddhe kṣīreṇa payākulabuddhisatvaḥ।
pāṇḍvāmayārttāvudare saśophe pibecchilājaṃ mahiṣījalena॥
au49.305
aśma vīratarādyena kuṣṭhaṃ khadiravāriṇā।
viṣaṃ viṣaghnairagadairhantyevaṃ tadyathāmayam॥
au49.306
śailajatrikaṭukṣaudrakṣaudradhātūn niṣevate।
kṣīraudanāśī yo jīrṇe yakṣmaṇā na sa bādhyate॥
asa49.307। subhāvitātsāragaṇaistulāṃ pītvā śilodbhavāt।
sārāṃbunaiva bhuñjānaḥ śāliṃ jāṅgalajai rasaiḥ॥
au49.308
vyapohya madhumehākhyamantakaṃ rogasaṅkaram।
vapurvarṇabalopetaḥ śataṃ jīvatyanāmayaḥ॥
au49.309
śilāhvāt ṣoḍaśapalaṃ tristrirekatra bhāvayet।
varāyā daśamūlasya guḍūcyāḥ karkaśasya ca॥
au49.310
balāyā madhuyaṣṭyāśca rase gavye ca vāriṇi।
kṣīre sakṛtkrameṇaivaṃ saptakṛtvastathā punaḥ॥
au49.311
kākoliyugmaghanapuṣkaravahnirāsnā medāyugarddhicavikāgajapippalīnām।
pāṭhādvijīvakanikumbhavidāriyugma vīrāvarīmadhuphalāṃśumatīdvayānām॥
au49.312
palikānāmabdroṇe siddhānāṃ pādaśeṣite kvāthe।
bhāvitamitthaṃ girijaṃ dvipalaiścūrṇīkṛtairyuñjyāt॥
au49.313
karkaṭaśṛṅgīdhātrīvyoṣaistālīsapatrakuḍabena।
cūrṇapalena vidāryāstvakṣīryāḥ karṣayugmena॥
au49.314
dvipalena caturjātāttaila ghṛtakṣaudraśarkarābhiśca।
dvipalāddviguṇābhiḥ kāryā guṭikāstatokṣasamāḥ॥
au49.315
tāḥ śuṣkā navakumbhe jātīpuṣpādhivāsite sthāpyāḥ।
tāsāmekāṃ khādet pratidinamanupānamatreṣṭam॥
au49.316
kṣīrarasadāḍimāmbho mārdvīkasurāsavānyatamam।
jīrṇennaṃ laghu bhojyaṃ yūṣapayaḥpiśitaniryūhaiḥ॥
au49.317
saptāhamātramevaṃ sarvānnīnaḥ kramāt bhavet parataḥ।
bhaktasyānte prāgvā guṭikā na virudhyate saiṣā॥
au49.318
nirapāyā bhūriphalā parihārasukhopayojitā jayati।
prabalamapi vātaśoṇitamūrustambhaṃ jvaraṃ dīrgham॥
au49.319
bhagamūtraśukradoṣaplīhayakṛdraktapāṇḍuhṛdrogān।
vardhmavamigulmapīnasahidhmākāsāruciśvāsān॥
au49.320
vidradhimudaraṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śvitraṃ jāḍyaṃ kṣayaṃ madaṃ mūrcchām।
unmādamapasmāraṃ mukhanetraśirogadāṃstāṃtān॥
au49.321
ānāhamatīsāraṃ halīmakaṃ kāmalāgrahaṇirogān।
granthyarbudān sapiṭakān bhagandaraṃ gaṇḍamālāṃ ca॥
au49.322
atikārśyamatisthaulyaṃ svedamathaślīpadaṃ gude kīlān।
daṃṣṭrāviṣaṃ samūlaṃ garaprayogān sughorāṃśca॥
au49.323
abhicāramarātikṛtaṃ duḥsvapnaṃ bhautikīṃ tathā bādhām।
pāpmālakṣmīṃ ceyaṃ guṭikā śamayecchivā nāmnā॥
au49.324
vṛṣyāyuṣyā dhanyā kāntiyaśaḥśrīvibodhinī medhyā।
kurute nṛpavallabhatāṃ jayaṃ vivāde ca vaktrasthā॥
au49.325
jitakhalativalīpalitā jīvayati sukhaṃ śatadvayaṃ śaradām।
varṣadvayaprayogādvarṣaśatacatuṣṭayaṃ jīvet॥
au49.326
na sostirogo bhuvi sādhyarūpo jatvaśmajaṃ yaṃ na jayet prasahya।
tatkālayogairvidhivatprayuktaiḥ svasthasya corjāṃ vipulāṃ dadhāti॥
au49.327
amaramandiramandarasambhavācchatapalaṃ girijādupayojaya।
yadi jarāmayaduḥkhavivarjitāṃ suciramicchasi jīvitasantatim॥
au49.328
daśaguṇamupayuṅkte yaḥ śataṃ śailajātāllaghuhitamitabhojī varjayan varjanīyān।
satatasamanuṣaktān varjitān vaidyavṛndairvidhamati sagadaughān nekṣate cāyuṣontam॥
au49.329
samudvabhūvāmṛtamanthanotthaḥ svedaḥ śilābhyo'mṛtavān gireḥ prāk।
yo mandarasyātmabhuvā hitāya nyastaḥ sa śaileṣu śilājarūpī॥
au49.330
suvarṇaśailaprabhavo viṣṇunā kāñcano rasaḥ।
tāpī kirātacīneṣu yavaneṣu ca nirmitaḥ॥
au49.331
tāpyāṃ sūryāṃśusantapto mādhave māsi dṛśyate।
madhuraḥ kāñcanābhāsaḥ sāmlo rajatasannibhaḥ॥
au49.332
kiṃcit kaṣāya ubhayaḥ śītaḥ pāke kaṭurlaghuḥ।
śilāniryāsavaccātra kulatthādīn parityajet॥
au49.333
na tanniṣevī jarasābhibhṛyate na pannagairnāpi garairna vṛścikaiḥ।
na pāṇḍumehajvaraśophayakṣmabhirna kaṇṭhanetraśravaṇatvagāmayaiḥ॥
au49.334
sodaśvitko mākṣikadhātuḥ saghṛto vā sakṣaudro vā kṣaudraghṛtābhyāṃ sahito vā।
sāmbhasko vā tailayuto vā vinihantā tvagdoṣāṇāṃ sarvaviṣāṇāṃ sagarāṇām॥
au49.335
akṣadrākṣāyomalamustāmalakānāṃ savyoṣāṇāṃ parvataniryāsayutānām।
datvā tulyaṃ mākṣikadhātuṃ madhumiśraṃ lihyātpāṇḍuvyādhyabhibhūtaḥ śivamicchan॥
au49.336
aṃśaḥ śuṇṭhyā lohamalāṃśo badarāṃśaḥ pippalyaṃśo mākṣikadhāturdviguṇāṃśaḥ।
kṣaudraṃ kāmaṃ kṛṣṇatilānāmapi cāṃśaḥ śreṣṭhā piṇḍī pāṇḍuvikāraśvayathughnī॥
au49.337
sāyaścūrṇaṃ mākṣikadhātuṃ madhumiśraṃ vyoṣopetaṃ parvataniryāsasametam।
kṣīrāhāro yo'valihānaḥ prayatātmā kṛtyudvāraṃ śoṣamapohatyacireṇa॥
au49.338
lohaṃ sarpirmākṣikadhāturmadhumātrā dhātrīcūrṇaṃ ke saramambuprabhavānām।
yogaḥ kuryādeṣa sitābhāgavimiśraścakṣurghrāṇaśrotrarasajñānavibodham॥
au49.339
kṛtyaikasthaṃ mākṣikadhātuṃ triphalāṃ ca bhrāṣṭre paktvā ye sahaviṣkaṃ vilihanti।
pathyādāstān vārdhakadoṣā na bhajante māturdoṣāḥ stanyanivṛttāniva vālān॥
au49.340
samaśnato mākṣikadhātucūrṇaṃ sarpirmadhubhyāṃ triphalārajaśca।
śanaiḥ śanairyāti jarā vināśaṃ pratyantavāsādiva lokayātrā॥
au49.341
trikoṇakāṇḍā subahupratānā phaleṣu pītā kusumeṣu raktā।
patraiḥsadugdhairmṛduromavadbhistāmbūlatulyairghanakandamūlā॥
au49.342
pavanavivasvadaṃśuvanitādiṣukāmacarā vividhamanaḥśarīragadavṛndanivṛttikarī।
bhuvi paramauṣadhirmahiṣavallarīti prathitā kvacidapi vṛddhadāraka iyatvapi vellarikā॥
au49.343
vasante saṅgṛhītānāṃ śoṣitānāmanātape।
vṛddhadārakamūlānāṃ tulāṃ saṃcūrṇyaṃ sarpiṣā॥
au49.344
āplāvya ghṛtapātrasthāṃ dhānye pakṣamupekṣitām।
lihyādanu pivetkṣīraṃ jīrṇe kṣīraghṛtāśanaḥ॥
au49.345
tatprayogājjarājīṇā vṛddhā dārakatāmiyāt।
bhagnāsthirgadgadaḥ paṅguḥ kṛśo hrasvonyarūpatām॥
au49.346
nirastāśeṣadoṣotthanakhabhedādyupadravaḥ।
apasmāragrahonmādapāpmālakṣmīvivarjitaḥ।
dīptāgnirbalavān vāgmī jīvedvarṣaśatāni ṣaṭ॥
au49.347
cūrṇitairaśvagandhāyāḥ saṃyutaṃ triṃśatā palaiḥ।
tattulyaṃ dārakaṃ prāśya payasā sarpiṣāthavā॥
au49.348
jīrṇo pūrvavadaśnīyādyo jīvet sa samāḥ śatam।
vājivego gajaprāṇaḥ surūpo bhāskaradyutiḥ॥
au49.349
aśvagandhena saṃyojyau varīgokṣurakau pṛthak॥
au49.350
yo lihyāt sarpiṣā cūrṇaṃ vṛddhadārakamūlajam।
saptāhaṃ yūṣabhaktāśī syāt sa kinnaratulyavāk॥
au49.351
svarasena śatāvaryā saptāhaṃ bhāvitaṃ ca tat।
lihānaḥ pūrvavanmāsaṃ śataṃ jīvenmahāmatiḥ॥
au49.352
lihyādvā madhusarpirbhyāṃ dhātrīsvarasabhāvitam।
kṣīreṇa vā pibanmāsaṃ śataṃ jīvedaruksudhīḥ॥
au49.353
vṛddhadārakamūlānāṃ rasaṃ kṣīreṇa yaḥ pibet।
tatkalkasiddhaṃ sarpirvā sajīvennīrujaḥ śatam॥
au49.354
pītaṃ vellarikāmūlaṃ gomūtreṇa sahoṣitam।
kuṣṭhagulmodaragaraślīpadārśopacīrjayet॥
au49.355
pippalī triphalā dārvī mahauṣadhapunarnavāḥ।
pṛthagdaśapalāḥ sarvaistulyāṃśo vṛddhadārakaḥ॥
au49.356
dhānyāmlapītastaccūrṇo jīrṇe svacchandabhojanaḥ।
ślīpadāmamarudvardhmagulmodaragarān haret॥
au49.357
śauṇḍī viśvavarādvīpivellamustāḥ samāṃśakāḥ।
tulyavellarikāmūlāḥ sājyakṣaudrāstathāguṇāḥ॥
au49.358
tatphalāt svarasaṃ karṣaṃ lihaṃstulyājyamākṣikam।
gavyaṃ pibedanu payo māhiṣaṃ vā yatheṣṭabhuk॥
au49.359
pañcāhena jayet kāsān saptāhena tvagāmayān।
mahākuṣṭhāni māsena bhavenmāsadvayena tu।
pañcavarṣaśatāyuṣko dhīmedhābalarūpavān॥
au49.360
vellarīphalamūlānāṃ pippalyāśca samaṃ rajaḥ।
vellarīphalamūlotthasvarasenaiva bhāvayet॥
au49.361
amṛtāyā rasenānu tataḥ śuṣkaṃ ghṛtāplutam।
nikhanet ghṛtakumbhasthaṃ karīṣe bahusañcaye॥
au49.362
māsāduddhṛtya taṃ lehaṃ yo varṣamupayojayet।
sahasrāyuḥ sa jarasā sahasā nābhibhūyate॥
au49.363
kuṣṭhacūrṇatulāṃ kṣaudraghṛtasya dvitulānvitām।
dhānyarāśau dinaśataṃ nihitāmupayojayet॥
au49.364
sugandhikāyo dṛkśrotrasvaravarṇeṣvatīndriyaḥ।
gatavyādhijaro jīvet saptavarṣaśatāni nā॥
au49.365
kuṭīpraveśaḥ kṣaṇināṃ paricchadavatāṃ hitaḥ।
atonyathā tu ye teṣāṃ sauryamārutiko vidhiḥ॥
au49.366
vātātapasahā yogā vakṣyante'to viśeṣataḥ।
sukhopacārā bhraṃśe'pi ye na dehasya bādhakāḥ॥
au49.367
śītodakaṃ payaḥ kṣaudraṃ ghṛtamekaikaśo dviśaḥ।
triśaḥ samastamathavā prākpītaṃ sthāpayedvayaḥ॥
au49.368
harītakīmāgadhikākṣadhātrīścūrṇīkṛtā loharajovimiśrāḥ।
sarpirmadhubhyāmadataḥ śarīraṃ kālāgradūtī na jarā dunoti॥
au49.369
harītakīmāgadhikāviḍaṅgaśaśāṅkalekhāmalakacchavīnām।
sitopalautapaghṛtānvitānāṃ rogā na leḍhāramabhidravanti॥
au49.370
triphalāmasanodakena piṣṭāṃ rajanīṃ paryuṣitāmayaḥ kapāle।
madhunā madhurāṃ lihan hinasti sthavimānaṃ jarasaṃ gadāṃśca sarvān॥
au49.371
khadirāsanayūṣabhāvitāyāstriphalāyā ghṛtamākṣikaplutāyāḥ।
niyamena narā niṣevitāro yadi jīvantyajarāḥ kimatra citram॥
au49.372
asanasvarasena bhāvitānāmabhayānāṃ saviḍaṅgataṇḍulānām।
madhuloharajoghṛtāplutānāṃ na hi leḍhāramabhidravanti rogāḥ॥
au49.373
bījakamya rasamaṅgulihāryaṃ śarkarāmadhughṛtaṃ triphalāṃ ca।
śīlayatsu puruṣeṣu jarattāsvāgatāpi vinivarttata eva॥
au49.374
darvīpralepāsriphalākaṣāyaḥ sitopalā tailamadhupragāḍhaḥ।
sapippalīnāgaralohareṇustanoḥ sapatnīṃ jarasaṃ nihanti॥
au49.375
phalatrayatryūṣaṇacūrṇayuktāṃ drākṣāṃ sasarpirmadhuśarkarāṃ ca।
kṣīrānupānaṃ puruṣā lihanto jīvanti nirdhūtajarāvikārāḥ॥
au49.376
harītakīṃ sarpiṣi sampratāpya samaśnatastat pibato ghṛtaṃ ca।
bhaveccirasthāyi balaṃ śarīre sakdtkṛtaṃ sādhu yathā kṛtajñe॥
au49.377
ārāccitānāṃ kalaśaṃ purāṇaṃ dhātrīphalānāṃ madhunaśca pūrṇam।
saṃvatsarārddhaṃ nihitaṃ yaveṣu niṣevamāṇo jarasaṃ nihanti॥
au49.378
dhātrīkṛmighnāsanasāracūrṇaṃ satailasarpirmadhulohareṇu।
niṣevamāṇasya bhavennarasya tāruṇyalāvaṇyamapi praṇaṣṭam॥
au49.379
navāmalakaśuktayo madhu ghṛtaṃ rajaścāyasaṃ catuṣṭayamayoghaṭasthamiti cūrṇitaṃ vatsaram॥
au49.380
krameṇa lihataḥ payonupibataśca pathyāśinaściraṃ bhavati jīvitaṃ kṣayamupaiti pṛthavījarā॥
au49.381
cūrṇaṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāmalakāmṛtānāṃ lihan sasarpirmadhubhāgayuktam।
vṛṣasthiraḥśāntavikāraduḥkhaḥ samāḥ śataṃ jīvati kṛṣṇakeśaḥ॥
au49.382
viḍaṅgasāraṃ madhukaṃ ca piṣṭaṃ bhallātakakvāthamadhupragāḍham।
arśāṃsi jantūṃśca jayatyudīrṇān vahniṃ ca sandhukṣayati kṣaṇena॥
au49.383
viḍaṅgabhallātakacitrakāṇāṃ guḍottarāṇāmabhayānvitānām।
tailena cūrṇāni niṣevamāṇān śarīriṇo nopatapanti rogāḥ॥
au49.384
viḍaṅgabhallātakanāgarāṇi ye'śnanti sarpirmadhusaṃyutāni।
jarānadīṃ rogataraṅgiṇīṃ te lāvaṇyayuktāḥ puruṣāstaranti॥
au49.385
viḍaṅgakalkaṃ svarasena dhātryāḥ kṣaudreṇa yuktaṃ ca pibennaro yaḥ।
drākṣārasakṣaudrapariplutaṃ vā vijitya rogān sa bhavecchatāyuḥ॥
au49.386
cūrṇaṃ samaṃ māgadhikākaṇānāṃ viḍaṅgacūrṇena sacitrakeṇa।
niṣevamāṇo madhutailamiśraṃ vayaḥparīṇāmajale na majjet॥
au49.387
punarnavasyārddhapalaṃ palaṃ vā piṣṭaṃ pibedyaḥ payasārddhāmāsam।
māsadvayaṃ tattriguṇaṃ samāṃ vā jīrṇopi bhūyaḥ sapunarnavaḥ syāt॥
au49.388
mūrvābṛhatyaṃśumatībalānāmuśīrapāṭhāsanasārivāṇām।
kālānusāryāgarucandanānāṃ vadanti paunarnavameva kalpam॥
au49.389
śatavarīkalkakaṣāyasiddhaṃ ye sarpiraśnanti sitādvitīyam।
tān jīvitādhvānamabhiprapannān na vipralumpanti vikāracorāḥ॥
au49.390
pītāśvagandhā payasārddhamāsaṃ ghṛtena tailena sukhāmbunā vā।
kṛśasya puṣṭiṃ vapuṣo vidhatte bālasya sasyasya yathā suvṛṣṭiḥ॥
au49.391
dine dine kṛṣṇatilaprakuñcaṃ samaśnataḥ śītajalānupānam।
poṣaḥ śarīrasya bhavatyanalpo dṛḍhībhavantyāmaraṇācca dantāḥ॥
au49.392
śilājatukṣaudraviḍaṅgasarpirlohābhayāpāradatāpyabhakṣaḥ।
āpūryate durbaladehadhātustripañcarātreṇa yathā śaśāṅkaḥ॥
au49.393
madhu madhurasā lājā bhārṅgī madhūkaśatāvarī।
kamalakusumatvakṣīrībhiḥ samaṃ jatu pārvatam।
pracurahaviṣā lehaṃ līḍhvā samṛddhasitopalaṃ।
śithilajaraso mandātakā bhavanti cirāyuṣaḥ॥
au49.394
gāyatrīśikhiśiṃśapāsanaśivā vellākṣakāruṣkarān piṣṭvāṣṭau daśaṣaṭguṇembhasi dṛtān khaṇḍaiḥ sahāyomayaiḥ।
pātre lohakṛte tryahaṃ ravikarairāloḍayan pācayedagnau cānu mṛdau salohaśakalaṃ pādasthitaṃ tat pacet॥
au49.395
pūtasyāṃśaḥ kṣīratoṃśastathāṃśau bhārṅgānniryāsāt pibaryāstrayoṃśāḥ।
aṃśāścatvārastatra hayyaṅgavīnādekīkṛtyaitat sādhayet kṛṣṇalauhe॥
au49.396
vimalayā sitayā madhunāthavā yutamayuktamidaṃ yadi vā ghṛtam।
svarucibhojanapānaviceṣṭito bhavati nā palaśaḥ pariśīlayan॥
au49.397
śrīmān nirdhūtapāpmā vanamahiṣabalo vājivegaḥ sthirāṅgo keśairbhṛṅgāṅganīlairmadhusurabhimukho naikayoṣinniṣevī।
vāṅmedhādhīsamṛddhaḥ supaṭuhutavaho māsamātropayogāddhattesau nārasiṃhaṃ vapuranalaśikhātaptacāmīkarābham॥
au49.398
haviridamatiprabhāvaṃ svamiva vapurnirmitaṃ nṛsiṃhena।
naśyanti yato bhītā vyādhyādhijarāsurā dūrāt॥
au49.399
bhṛṅgapravālānamunaivabhṛṣṭān ghṛtena yaḥ khādati yantritātmā।
viśuddhakoṣṭho'sanasārāsiddhadugdhānupastatkṛtabhojanārthaḥ॥
au49.400
māsopayogāt sa sukhī jīvatyabdaśata trayam।
gṛhṇāti sakṛdapyuktamaviluptasmṛtīndiryaḥ॥
au49.401
anenaiva ca kalpena yastailamupayojayet।
tānevāpnoti sa guṇān kṛṣṇakeśaśca jāyate॥
au49.402
kāśmaryāṇāṃ tulāṃ māsaṃ sthitāṃ madhughṛtokṣitām।
upayujya payonnāśī ciraṃ jīvati kāntimān॥
au49.403
uktāni śakyāni phalānvitāni yugānurūpāṇi rasāyanāni।
mahānuśaṃsānyapi cāparāṇi prāptyādikaṣṭāni na kīrttitāni॥
au49.404
amānuṣāṇāmativismayānāṃ satkarmaṇāṃ yadyapi tāni hetuḥ।
samūlakāṣaṃ tu kaṣanti dehaṃ bhraṃśādvidhestena vivarjitāni॥
au49.405
yugasvabhāvādyadi cauṣadhīnāṃ kriyāsu śaktiḥ parikalpyate'lpā।
āyurbalādiṣvapi sā tatheti yatnānniṣevyāṇi rasāyanāni॥
au49.406
na cauṣadhīnāmapi sarvathaiva prabhāvahāniḥ parikalpanīyā।
phalaṃ prayātyūrdhvamadhastrivṛttu pratyakṣataḥ kasya na siddhametat॥
au49.407
adeśakālopahitānyasātmyānyatyuṣṇatīkṣṇāni yathauṣadhāni।
nāśaṃ nayante sahasaiva dehaṃ samyakprayuktāni tathaiva vṛddhim॥
au49.408
jitvā tasmādindriyādīn suduṣṭān kālopetaḥ śvaddadhāno yathāvat।
āyuḥprajñātejasāṃ yadvivṛdhyai vīryopetaṃ śīlayedauṣadhaṃ tat॥
au49.409
utsāhavīrairapi sarvakālaṃ narairagamyāni tapodaridraiḥ।
mahārṇavānāmiva dustarāṇāṃ pārāṇyapārāṇi rasāyanānām॥
au49.410
rasāyanānāmupayogasampadā kṛtaprasādairmaladoṣadhātubhiḥ।
sthiraṃ śarīraṃ kriyate śarīriṇāṃ kulaṃ yathā satpuruṣairadhiṣṭhitam॥
au49.411
dāntendriyeṇa śāstrārthaṃ yathāvadanutiṣṭhātā।
kiyadvā dīrghadarśitvaṃ nendratvamapi durlabham॥
au49.412
rasāyanavidhibhraṃśājjāyeran vyādhayo yadi।
yathāsvamauṣadhaṃ teṣāṃ kāryaṃ muktvā rasāyanam॥
au49.413
adhyākrāntā ye'mlapaṭukṣārakaṭūṣṇairdravyaistīkṣṇaiḥ sannihitā teṣu jarattā।
sandhukṣyognistairupajāte ca vivarjyā yogāstegnau dhātusamṛddheḥ sa hi mūlam॥
au49.414
āyuryogāḥ sādhvapi yuktā mṛduvahnau nairarthakyaṃ yānti kṛtaghne'pyupakārāḥ।
dīpte vahnau te tu guṇaughairapi tucchā vistīryante pātranisṛṣṭā iva bhogāḥ॥
au49.415
satyavādinamakrodhamadhyātmapravaṇendriyam।
śāntaṃ sadvṛttanirataṃ vidyānnityarasāyanam॥
au49.416
guṇairobhiḥ samuditaḥ sevate yo rasāyanam।
sanirvṛtātmā dīrghāyuḥ paratreha ca modate॥
au49.417
śāstrānusāriṇī caryā cittajñāḥ pārśvavarttinaḥ।
buddhiraskhalitārtheṣu paripūrṇaṃ rasāyanam॥
au49.418
gavāmṛjutvena kṛtānukārairananyavāgāśayadehaceṣṭaiḥ।
sthirendriyāyurjvalanaiḥ suśīlaiḥ suvṛddha gopaiḥ samadhiṣṭhiteṣu॥
au49.419
prājyājyadugdhauṣadhipādapeṣu humbhāravairvalgitavatsakeṣu।
maṭhapraveśena vināpi siddhiṃ vrajanti goṣṭheṣu rasāyanāni॥
॥iti ekonapaccāśodhyāyaḥ॥
॥iti saptamaṃ rasāyanākhyamaṅgaṃ sampūrṇam॥
॥atha pañcaśo'dhyāyaḥ॥
au50.1
athāto vājīkaraṇavidhiṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ।
iti ha smāhu rātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ॥
au50.2
vājīkaraṇamanvicchet satataṃ viṣayī pumān।
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirapatyaṃ ca guṇavattatra saṃśritam।
apatyasantānakaraṃ yatsadyaḥ sampraharṣaṇam॥
au50.3
vājīvātibalo yena yātyapratihato'ṅganāḥ।
bhavatyatipriyaḥ strīṇāṃ yena yenopacīyate।
tadvājīkaraṇaṃ taddhi dehasyaujaskaraṃ param॥
au50.4
sāro hi jīvalokasya strī strīguṇasamanvitā।
striyaḥ sāddhvyaḥ prasuvate narān guṇamayāniva॥
au50.5
gotravṛddhikarāhyetā gṛhiṇyo gṛhadevatāḥ।
gṛhaṃ hi jīnametābhirna śrīmadapi śobhate॥
au50.6
na tu tā api śobhante jarasānugatā iva।
puṃyogena vinā strīṇāṃ sa hi saṃvananaṃ param॥
au50.7
vājīkaraṇanityasya kāmaṃ kāmaṃ siṣeviṣoḥ।
na śarīramavāpnoti na vā ratiratiḥ kṣayam॥
au50.8
acchāyaḥ pūtikusumaḥ phalena rahito drumaḥ।
yathaikaścaikaśākhaśca nirapatyastathā naraḥ॥
au50.9
adṛṣṭaputrapautrasya kulatantvantavarttinaḥ।
saṃsārasukhabāhyasya kīdṛśaṃ nāma jīvitam॥
au50.10
asambandhohyaputrasya nityameva paraḥ paraḥ।
sīdatyasyāvasāne ca gṛhaṃ susthepyanāyakam।
ato vājīkarā yogā niṣevyāḥ śukravarddhanāḥ॥
au50.11
kalyasyodagravayaso vājīkaraṇasevinaḥ।
sarveṣvṛtuṣvaharaharvyavāyo na nivāryate॥
au50.12
cintājarābhyāṃ śukraṃ tu vyādhibhiḥ karmakarśanāt।
kṣayaṃ gacchatyanaśanāt strīṇāṃ cātiniṣevaṇāt॥
au50.13
śukrakṣayāt bhayācchokādavisrambhādasevanāt।
atiharṣādatisthaulyānmalopacayataḥ śramāt॥
au50.14
strīṇāmakauśalāddoṣadarśanādabhicārataḥ।
meḍhrāmayāt sumahataḥ krodhato'dharmakīrttanāt।
tṛptasyāpi striyo gantuṃ na śaktirupajāyate॥
au50.15
nahi jātabalāḥ sarve narāścāpatyabhāginaḥ।
bṛhaccharīrā balinaḥ kecinnārīṣu durbalāḥ॥
au50.16
santi cālpāśrayāḥ strīṣu balavanto bahuprajāḥ।
narāścaṭakavatkecidvrajanti bahuśaḥ striyaḥ॥
au50.17
gajavaccaprasiñcanti kecinna bahugāminaḥ।
kecitprayatnairvāhyante vṛṣāḥ kecitsvabhāvataḥ॥
au50.18
tasmātprayogān vakṣyāmi durbalānāṃ balapradān।
sukhopabhogān balināṃ bhūyaśca balavarddhanān॥
au50.19
atha snigdhaviśuddhānāṃ nirūhān sānuvāsanān।
ghṛtatailarasakṣīraśarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutān॥
au50.20
yogavidyojayet pūrvaṃ kṣīramāṃsarasāśinām।
tato vājīkarānyogān śukrāpatyabalapradān॥
au50.21
śarekṣukuśakāśānāṃ vidāryā vīraṇasya ca।
mūlāni kaṇṭakāryāśca jīvakarṣabhakau balām॥
au50.22
mede dve dve ca kākolyau sūpyaparṇyau śatāvarīm।
aśvagandhāmatibalāmātmaguptāṃ punarnavām॥
au50.23
vīrāṃ payasyāṃ jīvantīmṛddhiṃ rāsnāṃ trikaṇṭakam।
madhukaṃ śāliparṇīṃ ca bhāgāṃstripalikān pṛthak॥
au50.24
māṣāṇāmāḍhakaṃ caitat dvidroṇe sādhayedapām।
rasenāḍhakaśeṣeṇa pacettena ghṛtāḍhakam॥
au50.25
datvā vidārīdhātrīkṣurasānāmāḍhakāḍhakam।
ghṛtāccaturguṇaṃ kṣīraṃ peṣyāṇīmāni cāvapet॥
au50.26
vīrāṃ svaguptāṃ kākolyau yaṣṭīṃ phalgu dvipippalīm।
drākṣāṃ vidārīṃ kharjūraṃ madhukāni śatāvarīm॥
au50.27
tatsiddhapūtaṃ cūrṇasya pṛthakprasthena yojayet।
śarkarāyāstugāyāśca pippalyāḥ kuḍavena ca॥
au50.28
maricasya prakuñcena pṛthagarddhapalonmitaiḥ।
tvagelākesaraiḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ kṣaudradvikuḍavena ca॥
au50.29
palamātraṃ tataḥ khādet pratyahaṃ rasadugdhamuk।
tenārohati vājīva kuliṅgaiva hṛṣyati॥
au50.30
māṣātmaguptābījānāmāḍhakaṃ prasṛtonmitam।
medāśvagandharddhivarī vīrā yaṣṭī dvijīvakam॥
au50.31
śūrpe'pāṃ vipacettena pādaśeṣeṇa pācayet।
vidārīkṣurasaprasthadvayena sadṛśena ca॥
au50.32
sarvaiḥ kṣīreṇa haviṣo navāt prasthaṃ śṛte'tra ca।
sitākṣaudrasitākhyānāṃ pṛthagdadyāccatuṣpalam॥
au50.33
palaṃ kaṇāt purobhaktaṃ lihaṃstatpalapūrvakam।
taruṇīṣvavatṛptāsu prasabhaṃ rāsabhāyate॥
au50.34
medādibhiśca karṣāṃśaiḥ śṛtaṃ bāṣkayaṇaṃ payaḥ।
saśarkarākṣaudraghṛtaṃ śukravṛddhikaraṃ param॥
au50.35
payasā pāyasastena māṣakaṇḍūkarīphalaiḥ।
vṛṣyo vegakaraḥ siddhaḥ saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaraḥ॥
au50.36
śvadaṃṣṭrāyā vidāryāśca rase kṣīracaturguṇe।
ghṛtāḍhyaḥ sādhito vṛṣyo māṣaṣaṣṭikapāyasaḥ॥
au50.37
madhūlikā māṣaparṇī sitā śṛṅgāṭakaṃ yavāḥ।
svaguptāmūlayaṣṭyāhvavidārīkṣurakāḥ samāḥ॥
au50.38
sapriyālāḥ kṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ pṛthaṅmadhvājyaṣaḍguṇam।
pādābhyāmaspṛśanbhūmiṃ lihankālyamataḥ picum।
labhate valamutsāhaṃ strīśca yāti kuliṅgavat॥
au50.39
svaguptā kṣīrakākolī vidārī jīvakadvayam।
tilāḥ saluñcitā bhṛṣṭāḥ śarkarājyamadhuplutam।
taccūrṇaṃ prasṛtaṃ līḍhvā gacchati pramadāśatam॥
au50.40
prasṛtaṃ māṣacūrṇasya dhātrīsvarasabhāvitam।
vidārīrajaso vāpi lihan madhughṛtadrutam।
kṣīrānupaścaṭakavaddaśakṛtvo vrajet striyaḥ॥
au50.41
cūrṇa vidāryā bahuśaḥ svarasenaiva bhāvitam।
kṣaudrasarpiryutaṃ līḍhvā pramadā daśa gacchati॥
au50.42
kṛṣṇā dhātrīphalarajaḥ svarasenaivabhāvitam।
śarkarāmadhusarpirbhirlīḍhvā yo'nu payaḥ pibet।
sa naro'śītivarṣopi yuveva parihṛṣyati॥
au50.43
karṣaṃ madhukacūrṇasya ghṛtakṣaudrasamanvitam।
payonupānaṃ yo lihyānnityavegaḥ sa nā bhavet॥
au50.44
kulīraśṛṅgyā yaḥ kalkamāloḍya payasā pibet।
sitāghṛtapayonnāśī sa nārīṣu vṛṣāyate॥
au50.45
dhānyamāṣarasaḥ kṣīraṃ kṣaudramikṣuraso ghṛtam।
dvimedājīvakayugakvāthaścaikatra yojitaḥ।
pītaḥ karoti puruṣaṃ pramadāśatagāminam॥
au50.46
bhallātakaiścaturbhistu dugdhasyārddhāḍhakaṃ pacet।
pītaṃ karoti vṛṣatāṃ sujīrṇasyāpi dehinaḥ॥
au50.47
svayaṅguptekṣurakayorbījacūrṇaṃ saśarkaram।
dhāroṣṇena naraḥ pītvā payasā rāsabhāyate।
uccaṭācūrṇamapyevaṃ śatāvaryāśca yojayet॥
au50.48
sūpyaparṇī dvikākolī jīvakarṣabhakaiḥ śṛtam।
laghunā pañcamūlena dvikākolīyutena vā।
payo'tivṛṣyamabhyasya vṛddho'pi taruṇāyate॥
au50.49
kṣīriṇī ca śvadaṃṣṭrā ca phāṇitaṃ śarkarā madhu।
gṛṣṭikṣīraṃ navaṃ sarpiretat puṃsavanaṃ param॥
au50.50
aśvatthaphalamūlatvakśṛṅgasiddhaṃ payo naraḥ।
pītvā saśarkaraṃ śītaṃ kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati॥
au50.51
payaḥ payasyayā siddhaṃ śukrakṛtsājyamākṣikam॥
au50.52
śatāvarīkatkarase payo daśaguṇaṃ ghṛtam।
śṛtaṃ sapippalīkṣaudraśarkaraṃ vṛṣyamuttamam॥
au50.53
śatāvarīrasaprasthaṃ kṣīraprasthacatuṣṭayam।
prasthaṃ ghṛtasya śuktyaṃśaṃ drākṣāmāṃsīparūṣakam॥
au50.54
jīvakarṣabhayaṣṭyāhvabalāmedākaśerukam।
priyālabījaṃ kākolīyugmaṃ caikatra pācayet॥
au50.55
pakvapūte kṣipeccāsmin kuḍavāṃśāṃ sitopalām।
gṛṣṭikṣīrānupaḥ prāśya tannārīṣu vṛṣāyate।
vijayeta ca vātāsraṃ pittāsroraḥkṣatakṣayān॥
au50.56
jīvakakṣīrakākolīsthirāhaṃsapadīghanaḥ।
śaṭhīkṣugaṇḍikāyaṣṭīmṛṇālaiḥ karṣikaiḥ pacet॥
au50.57
ghṛtaprasthaṃ daśaguṇe kṣīre tat balapuṣṭikṛt।
vandhyānāṃ putrajananaṃ śukravarddhanaśodhanam॥
au50.58
jalāḍhake svayaṃguptāmūlāt pañcapalaṃ pacet।
pādaśeṣe ca saṃcūrṇya kuḍavāṃśāḥ pṛthak kṣipet॥
au50.59
svaguptāmūlagodhūmamāṣekṣurakapippalīḥ।
sapriyālaphalakṣaudrāḥ prasthārddhaṃ navasarpiṣaḥ॥
au50.60
sitopalātulāpādaṃ kuryāttān modakāṃstataḥ।
modakaṃ bhakṣayitvaikaṃ ṣaṣṭiṃ vrajati yoṣitām॥
au50.61
palāṃśān bṛhatīvyāghrīpṛśniparṇītrikaṇṭakān।
dvyāḍhakenāmbhasā paktvā pādaśeṣe rase sthite॥
au50.62
palāni kṣīrakākolyāḥ pañca māgadhikāpalam।
svaguptāphalamūlānāṃ māṣāṇāmikṣurasya ca॥
au50.63
vidāryā madhunaścātra kuḍavaṃ kuḍavaṃ kṣipet।
pṛthak dvau mudgatilayorghṛte śaṣkulikāstataḥ।
pacedekāṃ tataḥ prāśya śataṃ vrajati yoṣitām॥
au50.64
svaguptāmūlacūrṇena drutena payasā kṛtāḥ।
ghṛte saśarkarākṣaudrā bhakṣyā vegaśatapradāḥ॥
au50.65
māṣātmaguptāgodhūmaśāliṣaṣṭikapaiṣṭikān।
śarkarāyā vidāryāśca cūrṇānīkṣurakasya ca॥
au50.66
saṃyojya kṣīrasarpirbhyāṃ ghṛte pūpalikāḥ pacet।
payonupānāstāḥ śīghraṃ kurvanti vṛṣatāṃ param॥
au50.67
cūrṇaṃ māṣāttilācchālervidāryāśca sasaindhavam।
rasena puṇḍrakasyekṣoḥ plutaṃ vārāhamedasi।
paktvā śaṣkulikrāḥ khādannārohet ṣaṣṭimaṅganāḥ॥
au50.68
mukhapriyāṇāṃ snigdhānāṃ phalānāṃ madhurātmanām।
phalānāmātmaguptāyāḥ śālermāṣāttilāt ghṛtāt॥
au50.69
mudgāt godhūmataścāpi kuḍavaṃ kuḍavaṃ pṛthak।
cūrṇitairnistuṣaistaistu kṣīreṇāloḍya marditaiḥ।
pakvāṃ pūpalikāṃ khādan strīṣu hṛṣyati vājivat॥
au50.70
śarkarāmāṣagodhūmatugākṣīrīpayoghṛtaiḥ।
pakvāmutkārikāṃ khādet kṛkavākurasānupaḥ॥
au50.71
māyuraṃ taittiraṃ hāṃsamevameva rasaṃ pibet।
anenāśva ivodīrṇo balī liṅgaṃ samarpayet॥
au50.72
piṣṭvā varāhamāṃsāni datvā maricasaindhave।
kolavadguṭikāḥ kṛtvā tapte sarpiṣi varttayet॥
au50.73
varttanastambhitāstāśca prakṣepyāḥ kaukkuṭe rase।
ghṛtāḍhye gandhapiśune dadhidāḍimasārike॥
au50.74
yathā na bhindyādguṭikāstathā taṃ sādhayedrasam।
taṃ pibanbhakṣayaṃstāśca balī bāleyavadvrajet।
māṃsāni balayuktāni tathānyānyapi kalpayet॥
au50.75
māṣānaṃkuritānśuddhān nistuṣānsājahāphalān।
ghṛtāḍhye māhiṣarase dadhidāḍimasārike॥
au50.76
prakṣipya sādhayedyuktyā dhānyajīrakanāgaraiḥ।
pīto bhuktaśca sa rasaḥ kurute śukramakṣayam॥
au50.77
haṃsabarhiṇadakṣāṇḍān bhṛṣṭāṃstaptena sarpiṣā।
surānupānān yaḥ khādet sa tṛptastarppayetstriyaḥ॥
au50.78
ārdrāṇi matsyamāṃsāniśapharīrvā subharjitāḥ।
tapte sarpiṣi yaḥ khādet sa gacchet strīṣu na kṣayam॥
au50.79
ghṛtabhṛṣṭān rase chāge rohitān phalasārike।
anupītarasān siddhānapatyārthī prayojayet॥
au50.80
ghṛtaṃ māṣān sabastāṇḍān phalāmle māhiṣe rase।
svādau vā sādhayet pūtaṃ tadrasaṃ bharjayet ghṛte॥
au50.81
īṣallavaṇitaṃ yuktaṃ dhānyajīrakanāgaraiḥ।
pītaḥ sa vṛṣyo balyaśca bṛṃhaṇaśca paraṃ rasaḥ॥
au50.82
caṭakāṃstaittire tadvattittirīn kaukkuṭe rase।
kalpayecchikhino hāṃse haṃsān vā śikhije rase॥
au50.83
tṛptiṃ caṭakamāṃsānāṃ gatvā yonu payaḥ pibet।
prabhūtakālasaṃruddhāḥ santarpayati yoṣitaḥ॥
au50.84
ghṛtāḍhyaṃ kukvuṭaṃ śūlyaṃ śītaṃ khādet samākṣikam।
pibeccānantaraṃ kṣīraṃ ya icchecchukramakṣayam॥
au50.85
pippalīlavaṇairyuktau bastāṇḍau kṣīrasarpiṣā।
sādhitau bhakṣayedyastu sa gacchet pramadāśatam॥
au50.86
bastāṇḍasiddhe godugdhe bhāvitānasakṛttilān।
yaḥ khādetsasitān gacchet sa strāśatamapūvavat॥
au50.87
bhuktvā yo māṣasūpena ghṛtāḍyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam।
payaḥ pibati jāgarti kṛtsnāṃ rātriṃ sa vegavān॥
au50.88
ātmaguptāphalaṃ māṣān kharjūrāṇi śatāvarīm।
śṛṅgāṭakāni mṛdvīkā pacettat prasṛtonmitam॥
au50.89
kṣīraprasthaṃ jalaprasthametat kṣīrāvaśeṣitam।
śucinā vāsasā pūtaṃ yojayet prasṛtaistribhiḥ॥
au50.90
śarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ sarpiṣo'bhinavasya ca।
tatpibet kṣaudrasaṃyuktaṃ bhuñjānaḥ ṣaṣṭikaudanam।
tathā jarāparītopi putraiḥ sa parivāryate॥
au50.91
drākṣākharjarakharjūrīmastakānyajahāphalam।
payasyābhīrumāṣāṃśca madhukāni ca sādhayet॥
au50.92
toyāḍhake palāṃśāni pādaśeṣeṇa tena ca।
kṣīraprasthaṃ pacet kṣīraśeṣeṇādyāt ghṛtānvitam।
ṣaṣṭikānnaṃ sitājyena yogo'yaṃ śukrakṛt param॥
au50.93
jīvakarṣabhakau medā jīvantī śrāvaṇīdvayam।
kharjūraṃ madhukaṃ drākṣāṃ vidārīṃ viśvabheṣajam॥
au50.94
śṛṅgāṭakāni capalā navaṃ sarpiḥpayo jalam।
ghṛtāvaśeṣitaṃ siddhaṃ śarkarāmākṣikānvitam॥
au50.95
ṣaṣṭikaudanasaṃyuktamupayojyaṃ yathābalam।
tadvṛṣyaṃ balakṛdvarṇyaṃ kaṇṭhyaṃ dehasya bṛṃhaṇam॥
au50.96
gṛṣṭirbaṣkayaṇī nīrugūrdhvaśṛṅgī catuḥstanī।
sāndrasvādubahukṣīrā rūpaśīlasamanvitā॥
au50.97
ikṣubhirmāṣaparṇena yā supuṣṭārjunena vā।
tatkṣīraṃ sasitākṣaudraghṛtaṃ putryaṃ ratipradam॥
au50.98
śukralairjīvanīyākhyairbṛṃhaṇairbalavarddhanaiḥ।
vayasaḥ sthāpanaiścetat payaḥ siddhaṃ pṛthakpṛthak॥
au50.99
yuktaṃ godhūmacūrṇena saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaram।
paryāyeṇopayoktavyamicchatā śukramakṣayam॥
au50.100
medāṃ payasyāṃ jīvantīṃ vidārīṃ kaṇṭakārikām।
māṣān śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ kṣīrīkāṃ godhūmān śāliṣaṣṭikān॥
au50.101
tatkṣīrerddhodake siddhān kārṣikānāḍhakonmite।
visarjayetpayaśśeṣaṃ tatpūtaṃ kṣaudrasarpiṣā।
sitayā ca yutaṃ pītvā vṛddhopi taruṇāyate॥
au50.102
maṇḍalairjātarūpasya sutaptaistatpayaḥ śṛtam।
siddhaṃ puṃsavanaṃ vṛṣyaṃ sasitāghṛtamākṣikam।
rūpyāyastāmnasīsānāmayameva pṛthagvidhiḥ॥
au50.103
cūrṇitāḥ pippalīstriṃśat prakuñce tailasarpiṣoḥ।
bhṛṣṭāḥ saśarkarākṣaudrāḥ kṣīreṇāloḍitāḥ pibet।
aśnaṃśca ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpirbhyāṃ vājivadbhavet॥
au50.104
candrāṃśuśubhraṃ payasā ghṛtāḍhyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam।
śarkarāmadhusaṃyuktaṃ bhuñjāno nā vṛṣāyate॥
au50.105
dadhnaḥ sareṇa saghṛto bhakṣitaḥ ṣaṣṭikaudanaḥ।
sailātugoṣaṇakṣaudraḥ śarkarāḍhyena śukrakṛt॥
au50.106
adhyaṇḍāmārṣabhīṃcaiva svayaḍguptāphalāni ca।
pādalepaṃ naraḥ kṛtvā niśi vegairna hīyate॥
au50.107
varṣābhūmūlamṛdvīkāsvayaṅguptāphalāni ca।
siddhaścaraṇalepoyaṃ bhuvaṃ padbhyāṃ tu na spṛśet॥
au50.108
ghṛtakṣīrāśano nityaṃ nirvyādhirnityago yuvā।
saṅkalpapravaṇo ityaṃ naraḥ strīṣu vṛṣāyate॥
au50.109
ātmaguptāphalaṃ māṣā godhūmaḥ śāliṣaṣṭikam।
ikṣurikṣurakaḥ kṣīraṃ kṣaudraṃ drākṣā sitopalā॥
au50.110
uccaṭā śaramūlāni vidārī saśatāvarī।
jīvanīyāni svarjūraṃ mocacocaphalāni ca॥
au50.111
ebhirbhakṣyāṇi peyāni lehyāni ca ghṛtāni ca।
nityamāsevamānasya strīṣu harṣo vivarddhate॥
au50.112
jīvanīyaghṛtakṣīramadhutailasitārasaiḥ।
rasakṣīrāśinaḥ kṣipraṃ vṛṣaṃ kurvanti bastayaḥ॥
au50.113
siddhabastivikalpoktān balaśukrasutapradān।
yuñjīta bastīn putrārthī putrakāmoditaṃ ca yat॥
au50.114
yatkiñcinmadhuraṃ snigdhaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ balavarddhanam।
manaso harṣaṇaṃ yacca tatsava vṛṣyamucyate॥
au50.115
dravyairevaṃvidhaistasmāt bhāvitaḥ pramadāṃ vrajet।
ātmavegena codīrṇaḥ srīguṇaiśca praharṣitaḥ॥
au50.116
iṣṭāhyekaikaśopyarthā harṣaprītikarāḥ param।
kiṃ punaḥ strīśarīre ye saṅghaghātena pratiṣṭhitāḥ॥
au50.117
rucibhedena lokasya daivayogāñca yoṣitām।
taṃ taṃ prāpya vivarddhante naraṃ rūpādayo guṇāḥ॥
au50.118
tasmādyā yasya hṛdayaṃ viśatīva varāṅganā।
tulyasvabhāvā yā hārimṛjārūpaguṇānvitā॥
au50.119
pāśabhūtairvahantyaṅgairlāvaṇyamiva mūrtimat।
ālapantyamṛteneva yā gātrāṇi niṣiñcati॥
au50.120
pibantīva ca paśyantī spṛśantī limpatīva yā।
nityamutsavabhūtā yā yā samānamanaḥśayā॥
au50.121
nayatyutsukatāṃ ceto nityaṃ sannihitāpi yā।
yayā viyukto niḥstrīkamaratirmanyate jagat॥
au50.122
pragalbhā rītasaṅgrāme svasthā lajjāmayī ca yā।
bahuśopi ca yāṃ gatvā tatpūrvamiva gacchati॥
au50.123
caritairnirvikārā yā vikārairiva nirmitā।
kāntānuvṛttiparamā sā strī vṛṣṭyatamā matā॥
au50.124
abhyañjanodvartanasekagandhasrakcitravastrābharaṇaprakārāḥ।
sugandhipuṣpotkarareṇukīrṇā mṛdurmanojñā vipulā ca śayyā॥
au50.125
prājñāḥ kalājñā vaśagā vinītāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ prītikarā vayasyāḥ।
visrambhasatvaprakṛtikriyaikyāccharīramātreṇa pṛthaktvabhūtāḥ॥
au50.126
kāntā vanāntāḥ parapuṣṭaghuṣṭā ramyāḥ sravantyaḥ satataṃ sravantyaḥ।
madyaṃ madāmodakaraṃ viśeṣādhdṛdyā prasannā surabhiḥ prasannā॥
au50.127
śakāṅganāgaṇḍatalābhipāṇḍutāmbulapatraṃ parivāraśobhi।
prasādhanaṃ strīmukhapaṅkajānāṃ yadāyudhaṃ mūrtamivātmajasya॥
au50.128
himācaloddhūnitadugdhasindhusamudbhavatphenacayāvadātam।
saudhaṃ sudhāśubhratarāḥ karāśca candrasya kurvanti paraṃ vṛṣatvam॥
au50.129
bandhena pūrvopahitena puṃsaḥ khinnasya vṛttiḥ karaṇāntareṇa।
saṃvāhanaṃ sparśasukhaiḥ karaiśca karotyapūrvāmiva manmathecchām॥
au50.130
prāyogikādhikaraṇoditācitraceṣṭāsaṃśīlanodbhavadanalparasārdracittaḥ।
vṛṣyopayogaparibṛṃhitadehadhāturnārīmanāṃsi vaśamānayati prasahya॥
au50.131
tasmānnityaṃ strīṣu vāñchan priyatvaṃ vṛṣyairyogairjātakāmo'pi kāmī।
satvaṃa sātmyaṃ deśakālau ca budhvā cātuṣṣaṣṭe ceṣṭite vyāpriyeta॥
au50.132
valayasvanasaṅkulamuṣṭiravadviguṇīkṛtamekhalikāninadaḥ।
calanūpuraśabdayuto'pi muhuḥ śamamāvahate na ratātiśayaḥ॥
au50.133
sarvārthasiddhiḥ prathamonurāgaḥ śṛṅgāragāndharvakathāviśeṣāḥ।
sītkāragarbhaṃ hasitaṃ sahāvaṃ chinnākṣaraṃ vibhramavacca gītam॥
au50.134
savyājasandīrśatacārugātraṃ vṛttaṃ priyāṇāmavalokitaṃ ca।
cūtāṅkuraṃ puṣpaphalaṃ yathartu vidyutvadudyotitagarjitāni॥
au50.135
vihaṅgabhṛṅgastanitānuyātaṃ strīkūjitaṃ bhūṣaṇaśiñjitāni।
kāle yathāsvaṃ vapuṣaśca śuddhiḥ saṅkalpayonerdhuramudvahanti॥
au50.136
srotassu śudveṣvamale śarīre vṛṣyaṃ yadādyaṃ mitamatti kāle।
vṛṣāyate tena paraṃ manuṣyastadbṛṃhaṇaṃ dehabalapradaṃ ca॥
au50.137
tasmāt purā śodhanameva kāryaṃ balānurūpaṃ na ca vṛṣyayogāḥ।
sidhyanti dehe kaluṣe prayuktāḥ kliṣṭe yathā vāsasi rāgayogāḥ॥
au50.138
upadiṣṭe vicitre'smin vaktavyārthānurodhataḥ।
kartavyamevakartavyaṃ prāṇābādhe'pi netarat॥
au50.139
etat svarūpaṃ śāstrasya yadvyāpitvena varṇyate।
spṛśati nyūnatādoṣo mahānavyāpini dhruvam॥
au50.140
vīryahīnairasampūrṇaiḥ prayogairapi bhūṣitam।
arthānatantrayattantraṃ tantratāmāpnuyāt katham॥
au50.141
haṃsabarhiṇadakṣāṇḍā yadyapyatyarthaśukralāḥ।
munayaḥ sadayā brūyustānyogeṣvanyathā katham॥
au50.142
kathaṃ vā sarvaevaite yogā rāgāgnidīpanāḥ।
kliṣṭasaṅkalpajananāḥ proktāḥ saṃsāravarddhanāḥ॥
au50.143
trikāladarśibhirdivyaiḥ satvadoṣaṣivarjitaiḥ।
pūrvācāryaiḥ kṛtaṃ vartma ko laṅghayitmumarhati॥
au50.144
prakrānte sarvathā sarvamuktaṃ bhavati sūditam।
nāhi leśābhidhānena labhyaḥ sarvārthasaṅgrahaḥ॥
au50.145
tathā ca gardabhīkṣīraṃ māṃsamaśvasya hastinām।
maddāsāgaratoyaṃ ca proktaṃ nirupayogyapi॥
au50.146
adyatve'pi viśeṣeṇa bhūritantrārthasaṅgrahāt।
saṅgrahādyannabudhyeta tajjñānamatidurlabham॥
au50.147
yathā pratijñātamiti krameṇa vedoyamaṣṭāṅganidhernibaddhaḥ।
abhyasyato mārgamivāryasatyaṃ sañjāyate svārthaparārthasiddhiḥ॥
au50.148
pitāmahamukhodgīrṇamityāyurvedavāṅmayam।
jīvitārogyadharmārthasukhagauravakīrttikṛt॥
au50.149
alaṅkṛtaṃ yuktipadaiḥ sadratnairiva kāñcanam।
ṣaṭtriṃśatārthadurgeṣu bhiṣajāṃ saṅkramairiva॥
au50.150
tatrādhikaraṇaṃ yogo hetvarthorthaḥ padasya ca।
pradeśoddeśanirdeśavākyaśeṣāḥ prayojanam॥
au50.151
upadeśāpadeśātideśārthāpattinirṇayāḥ।
prasaṅgaikāntanaikāntāḥ sāpavargo viparyayaḥ॥
au50.152
pūrvapakṣavidhānānumatavyākhyānasaṃśayāḥ।
atītānāgatāpekṣā svasaṃjñohya samuccayāḥ॥
au50.153
nidarśanaṃ nirvacanaṃ niyogo'tha vikalpanam।
pratyutsārastathoddhāraḥ sambhavastantrayuktayaḥ॥
au50.154
sarasaḥ suptapadmasya ravidīdhitayo yathā।
yathā gṛhasya dīpābhāstathā tantrasya yuktayaḥ॥
au50.155
adhīyāno'pi tantrāṇi tantrayuktyavicakṣaṇaḥ।
nādhigacchati tantrārthamarthaṃ bhāgyakṣaye yathā॥
au50.156
vākyārthayojanodatā yuktayastviṣṭasiddhidāḥ।
asadvādiprayuktānāṃ vākyānāṃ pratiṣedhakāḥ॥
au50.157
līnavyatyāsaleśoktigaditānāṃ prakāśakāḥ।
vākyanyāyodadheḥ sāraṃ gṛhītvaivaṃ vyavasthitāḥ॥
au50.158
etadāgamasiddhatvāt pratyakṣaphaladarśanāt।
prayojyaṃ mantravattantraṃ tantrajñānaviśāradaiḥ॥
au50.159
pittāmahena lokasya smṛtvā tadidamavyayam।
akālamṛtyurakṣārthamalauhaṃ varma nirmitam॥
au50.160
sujñātametadamṛtaṃ svasthāsvasthasukhāspadam।
yathepsitaphalāśeṣapuruṣārthaprasādhanam॥
au50.161
idaṃ śāstramadṛṣṭīnāmevamālokakāryapi।
maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasyeva na prakāśāya jāyate॥
au50.162
dhruvaṃ vaidyeṣu kalyāṇamāyurvedānusāriṣu।
itareṣvitaracchatraviṣajvalanakarmasu॥
au50.163
kuryāt prayuktaṃ śastrādi saśeṣamapi rogiṇam।
na tvevaṃ bheṣajaṃ mohādanālocitayojitam॥
au50.164
sadā doṣauṣadhādīni vīkṣya dvādaśa tatvataḥ।
kuryāccikitsitaṃ prājño na yogaireva kevalaiḥ॥
au50.165
mātrādi samyagajñātvā yadṛcchāpratipāditaḥ।
hinasti vyādhitaṃ yogo ghṛtamākṣikayoriva॥
au50.166
dṛṣṭvā viṣeṣyamṛtatāṃ ghṛtādau māraṇātmatām।
śāstratatvaṃ na vijñāya sa durātmā cikitsati॥
au50.167
sugītaścaiṣa kasyāpi mahāśloko mahātmanaḥ।
vaidyāścāśrutaśāstrārthā mūrkhāśca prabhāviṣṇavaḥ।
akālamṛtyavo hyete vicaranti mahītale॥
au50.168
lobhayantyāturaṃ mūḍhā ye citraiḥ karmakauśalaiḥ।
tebhyo rakṣetsadātmānamātmā yasmāt sudurlabhaḥ॥
au50.169
te dhruṇākṣaravatkañciduttārya niyatāyuṣam।
ghnanti vaidyābhimānena śatānyaniyatāyuṣām॥
au50.170
rogārtasya viṣaṇṇasya yatnalabhyasukhāyuṣaḥ।
avaidyo nirghṛṇaḥkrūro yaḥ karoti bhiṣagjitam॥
au50.171
pāpasya mṛtyudūtasya durmatestyaktadharmaṇaḥ।
naro narakapātī syāttasya sambhāṣaṇādapi॥
au50.172
atantrīkṛtatantrārthaḥ śāstramātropajīvinaḥ।
rājñāṃ pramādādrāṣṭrāṇi caranti vyādhavṛttayaḥ॥
au50.173
tān kālapāśasadṛśān varjayecchāstradūṣakān।
seveta śamavijñānajñānapūrṇān bhiṣaktamān॥
au50.174
annapānāni pathyāni vyādhinirghātamauṣadham।
rasāyanāni vṛṣyāṇi prāpyante vaidyasaṃśrayāt॥
au50.175
arājakā yathā deśā bhartṛhīnā yathā gṛhāḥ।
āturādyāstathā pādāḥ śocyā vaidyānadhiṣṭhitāḥ॥
au50.176
prāṇācāryaṃ budhastasmāddayāluṃ vijitendriyam।
aśvināviva devendraḥ pūjayedādṛtaḥ sadā॥
au50.177
yajñasya hi śiraśchinnamaśvibhyāṃ sandhitaṃ punaḥ।
pātitā daśanāḥ pūṣṇo bhagasya ca vilocane॥
au50.178
rājayakṣmārditaścandrastābhyāmeva cikitsitaḥ।
somānnipatito vajrī bhujastambhe ca dāruṇe॥
au50.179
bhārgavaścavanaḥ kāmī vṛddhaḥ san vikṛtiṃ gataḥ।
vīryavarṇabalopetaḥ kṛtastābhyāṃ punaryuvā॥
au50.180
ebhiścānyaiśca bahubhiḥ karmābhīrbhiṣaguttamau।
babhūvaturbhṛśaṃ pūjyāvindrādīnāṃ mahātmanām॥
au50.181
aśvibhyāṃ sahitaḥ somaṃ prātaḥ pibati vāsavaḥ।
sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca bhagavānaśvibhyāṃ saha modate॥
au50.182
aśvinoḥ kalpyate bhāgo yajñeṣu brāhmaṇairapi।
aśvināvagnirindraśca vedeṣu sutarāṃ stutāḥ॥
au50.183
vaidyavityaśvinau tasmāt pūjyete vibudhairapi।
ajarairamarairnityaṃ sukhitairevamādṛtaiḥ॥
au50.184
vyādhimṛtyujarāgrastairduḥkhaprāyaiḥ sukhārthibhiḥ।
kiṃ punarbhiṣajo martyaiḥ pūjyāḥ syurnātiśaktitaḥ॥
au50.185
śīlavān matimān yukto dvijātirvedapāragaḥ।
prāṇibhiḥ pitṛvatpūjyaḥ prāṇācāryaḥ sa hi smṛtaḥ॥
au50.186
vidyāsamāptau bhiṣajāṃ dvitīyā jātirucyate।
na vaidyo vaidyaśabdaṃ hi labhate pūrvajanmanā॥
au50.187
vidyāsamāptāvāṣa vā brahmaṃ vā bhiṣajaṃ dhruvam।
tasvamāviśati jñānāttena vaidyo dvijaḥ smṛtaḥ॥
au50.188
nāvadhyāyenna cākrośedahitaṃ na samācaret।
prāṇācāryaṃ budhaḥ kacchidicchannāyuranaśvaram॥
au50.189
bhiṣagapyāturān sarvān svasutāniva yatnavān।
ābādhebhyo'bhisaṃrakṣet jñānaṃ dharmanusmaran॥
au50.190
kurvate ye tu vṛtyarthaṃ cikitsāpaṇyavikrayam।
te hitvā kāñcanaṃ rāśiṃ pāṃsurāśimupāsate॥
au50.191
rogākhyāndāruṇānpāśānantakāntikakarṣiṇaḥ।
yaśchitvā yacchati prāṇāndātā nāstyeva tatsamaḥ॥
au50.192
na jīvitapradānāddhi dānamanyadviśiṣyate।
tasmādupācaret svena svena niḥsvatapasvinaḥ॥
au50.193
satvārthamīhamānasya vaidyasyaivaṃ mahāmateḥ।
vartante sannidhānena niyataṃ siddhidevatāḥ॥
au50.194
kvaciddharmaḥ kvacinmitraṃ kvacidarthaḥ kvacidyaśaḥ।
karmābhyāsaḥ kvacicceti cikitsā nāsti niṣphalā॥
au50.195
nityamādaravān vaidyastasmādārtānupācaret।
prāṇānsahātmanaḥ kīrtyā nihantyeṣāmanādarāta॥
au50.196
sarvatra maitrī karuṇātureṣu nirāmadeheṣu nṛṣu pramodaḥ।
manasyupekṣāpakṛtiṃ vrajatsu vaidyasya sadvṛttamalaṃ tanoti॥
au50.197
sāmiṣeṇāpi cittena jīvitocchedakāriṇaḥ।
yo nihantyāmayān vaidyaḥ sopi kenopamīyatām॥
au50.198
kimuta nirāmiṣeṇa manasā karuṇāmṛdunā kṛpaṇaviśiṣṭayoḥ sadṛśamādaramudvahatā।
atiguru bodhisatvacaritaṃ satataṃ vidadhacchamayati rogajālamapi yotivirodhi mithaḥ॥
au50.199
dāhaḥ śūlaṃ tṛḍādhmānaṃ kṣutkṣāmatvamarocakam।
kaḥ prākṛto jayedrogān nityamanyonyarodhinaḥ॥
au50.200
mārutāmagrahonbhādamadān susadṛśākṛtīn।
ko jānīyāccikitsedvādūrabhitnakriyākramān॥
au50.201
prāṇācārthaṃ vedapāraṃ prayātaṃ budhyā yuktaṃ pūjayennityamasmāt।
yasminyasya prāṇayātrā nibaddhā tasmai yacchan ko dhanānāṃ dhanāyet॥
au50.202
āyurvedaṃ ślokalakṣeṇa pūva brahmāmnāsīdagniveśādayastu।
kṛtsnajñeyaprāptasārāḥ svatantrāstasyaikaikaṃ naikadhāṅgaṃ vitenuḥ॥
au50.203
bhiṣagvaro vāgbhaṭa ityabhūnme pitāmaho nāmadharo'smi yasya।
sutobhavattasya ca siṃhaguptastasyāpyahaṃ sindhuṣu labdhajanmā॥
au50.204
samadhigamya guroravalokitāt gurutarācca pituḥ pratibhā mayā।
subahubheṣajaśāstravilocanāt suvihito'ṅgavibhāgavinirṇayaḥ॥
au50.205
pūrvoktameva vadatā kimivoditaṃ syācchraddhālutuṣṭijananaṃ na bhavatyapūrvam।
saṅkṣiptasaṃśayitavistṛtaviprakīrṇaḥ kṛtsnortharāśiriti sādhu sa eva dṛṣṭaḥ॥
au50.206
āyurvedodadheḥ pāramapārasya prayāti kaḥ।
viśvavyādhyauṣadhijñānasārastveṣa samuccitaḥ॥
au50.207
smṛtvedamuditaṃ pūrvaṃ śrutvedānīṃ dvayoḥ punaḥ।
smarttuḥ śrotuśca sutarāṃ śraddhātuṃ kasya yujyate॥
au50.208
athavā śrutamapyetat smartureva kramāgatam।
abhidhātṛviśeṣeṇa kiṃ tathāpi prayojanam॥
au50.209
ūrdhvameti madanaṃ trivṛtādho vastumātraka iti pratipādye।
madvidho yadi vadedathavātriḥ kathyatāṃ ka iva karmaṇi bhedaḥ॥
au50.210
sādhvasādhviti vivekaviyukto lokapaṅktikṛtabhaktiviśeṣaḥ।
bāliśo bhavati no khalu vidvān sūkta eva ramate matirasya॥
au50.211
iti munivacanānāṃ jīvitopāśrayāṇāmabhilaṣitasamṛddhau kalpavṛkṣopamānām।
yaduditamiha puṇyaṃ kurvato menuvādaṃ bhavatu vigatarogo nirvṛtastena lokaḥ॥
॥iti pañcaśo'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ॥
॥iti śrīsiṃhaguptasūnuśrīmadvāgbhaṭācāryaviracitāṣṭāṅgasaṅgrahe ṣaṣṭhamuttarasthānaṃ sampūrṇam॥
